# User Provided Header
# Khora Repository Documentation

This file is auto-generated by Repomix and provides a comprehensive view of the Khora codebase for AI-assisted development.

## Purpose

Khora is a Memory Lake system that combines knowledge graph (Neo4j), vector database (pgvector), and relational database (PostgreSQL) into a unified knowledge storage and retrieval platform.

## Key Features

- **Hybrid Search**: Vector + graph + keyword search with Reciprocal Rank Fusion
- **Multi-Tenancy**: Organization -> Workspace -> Namespace hierarchy with ACLs
- **Event Sourcing**: Immutable event log for temporal queries and audit trails
- **LiteLLM Integration**: Unified access to OpenAI, Anthropic, Google, and other LLM providers
- **Prefect Pipelines**: Orchestrated ingestion with checksum-based change detection
- **Semantic Extraction**: LLM-powered entity and relationship extraction

## Integration

This file can be used with AI tools like Claude, ChatGPT, or Cursor for:
- Code analysis and understanding
- API and integration development
- Documentation generation
- Refactoring suggestions

## File: alembic/env.py
````python
 1: """Alembic migration environment configuration."""
 2: 
 3: import asyncio
 4: import os
 5: from logging.config import fileConfig
 6: 
 7: from sqlalchemy import pool
 8: from sqlalchemy.engine import Connection
 9: from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import async_engine_from_config
10: 
11: from alembic import context
12: 
13: # Import models for autogenerate support
14: from khora.db.models import Base
15: 
16: # this is the Alembic Config object, which provides
17: # access to the values within the .ini file in use.
18: config = context.config
19: 
20: # Interpret the config file for Python logging.
21: if config.config_file_name is not None:
22:     fileConfig(config.config_file_name)
23: 
24: # Set target metadata for autogenerate
25: target_metadata = Base.metadata
26: 
27: 
28: def get_url() -> str:
29:     """Get database URL from environment."""
30:     url = os.getenv("KHORA_DATABASE_URL", "")
31:     if not url:
32:         raise ValueError("KHORA_DATABASE_URL environment variable not set")
33: 
34:     # Convert to async URL
35:     if url.startswith("postgresql://"):
36:         url = url.replace("postgresql://", "postgresql+asyncpg://", 1)
37:     elif url.startswith("postgres://"):
38:         url = url.replace("postgres://", "postgresql+asyncpg://", 1)
39: 
40:     return url
41: 
42: 
43: def run_migrations_offline() -> None:
44:     """Run migrations in 'offline' mode.
45: 
46:     This configures the context with just a URL
47:     and not an Engine, though an Engine is acceptable
48:     here as well. By skipping the Engine creation
49:     we don't even need a DBAPI to be available.
50:     """
51:     url = get_url()
52:     context.configure(
53:         url=url,
54:         target_metadata=target_metadata,
55:         literal_binds=True,
56:         dialect_opts={"paramstyle": "named"},
57:     )
58: 
59:     with context.begin_transaction():
60:         context.run_migrations()
61: 
62: 
63: def do_run_migrations(connection: Connection) -> None:
64:     """Run migrations with a connection."""
65:     context.configure(connection=connection, target_metadata=target_metadata)
66: 
67:     with context.begin_transaction():
68:         context.run_migrations()
69: 
70: 
71: async def run_async_migrations() -> None:
72:     """Run migrations in 'online' mode with async engine."""
73:     configuration = config.get_section(config.config_ini_section, {})
74:     configuration["sqlalchemy.url"] = get_url()
75: 
76:     connectable = async_engine_from_config(
77:         configuration,
78:         prefix="sqlalchemy.",
79:         poolclass=pool.NullPool,
80:     )
81: 
82:     async with connectable.connect() as connection:
83:         await connection.run_sync(do_run_migrations)
84: 
85:     await connectable.dispose()
86: 
87: 
88: def run_migrations_online() -> None:
89:     """Run migrations in 'online' mode."""
90:     asyncio.run(run_async_migrations())
91: 
92: 
93: if context.is_offline_mode():
94:     run_migrations_offline()
95: else:
96:     run_migrations_online()
````

## File: src/khora/acl/checker.py
````python
  1: """ACL checker with permission inheritance for Khora Memory Lake."""
  2: 
  3: from __future__ import annotations
  4: 
  5: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
  6: from enum import Enum
  7: from typing import Any
  8: from uuid import UUID
  9: 
 10: from loguru import logger
 11: 
 12: 
 13: class Permission(str, Enum):
 14:     """Permission levels in the ACL system."""
 15: 
 16:     READ = "read"  # Can read/query data
 17:     WRITE = "write"  # Can create/update data
 18:     ADMIN = "admin"  # Can manage permissions
 19:     OWNER = "owner"  # Full control including deletion
 20: 
 21:     def __ge__(self, other: Permission) -> bool:
 22:         """Check if this permission is >= another."""
 23:         order = [Permission.READ, Permission.WRITE, Permission.ADMIN, Permission.OWNER]
 24:         return order.index(self) >= order.index(other)
 25: 
 26:     def __gt__(self, other: Permission) -> bool:
 27:         """Check if this permission is > another."""
 28:         return self != other and self >= other
 29: 
 30:     def __le__(self, other: Permission) -> bool:
 31:         """Check if this permission is <= another."""
 32:         return other >= self
 33: 
 34:     def __lt__(self, other: Permission) -> bool:
 35:         """Check if this permission is < another."""
 36:         return other > self
 37: 
 38: 
 39: @dataclass
 40: class Principal:
 41:     """A principal (user, role, or API key) that can have permissions."""
 42: 
 43:     principal_type: str  # user, role, api_key
 44:     principal_id: str
 45:     metadata: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
 46: 
 47:     @classmethod
 48:     def user(cls, user_id: str) -> Principal:
 49:         """Create a user principal."""
 50:         return cls(principal_type="user", principal_id=user_id)
 51: 
 52:     @classmethod
 53:     def role(cls, role_name: str) -> Principal:
 54:         """Create a role principal."""
 55:         return cls(principal_type="role", principal_id=role_name)
 56: 
 57:     @classmethod
 58:     def api_key(cls, key_id: str) -> Principal:
 59:         """Create an API key principal."""
 60:         return cls(principal_type="api_key", principal_id=key_id)
 61: 
 62:     @classmethod
 63:     def system(cls) -> Principal:
 64:         """Create a system principal with full access."""
 65:         return cls(principal_type="system", principal_id="system")
 66: 
 67: 
 68: @dataclass
 69: class PermissionGrant:
 70:     """A permission grant for a principal on a resource."""
 71: 
 72:     principal: Principal
 73:     resource_type: str  # organization, workspace, namespace
 74:     resource_id: UUID
 75:     permission: Permission
 76:     inherited_from: tuple[str, UUID] | None = None  # (resource_type, resource_id) if inherited
 77: 
 78: 
 79: class ACLChecker:
 80:     """ACL checker with permission inheritance.
 81: 
 82:     Supports hierarchical permissions:
 83:     - Organization -> Workspace -> Namespace
 84:     - Permissions at higher levels cascade down
 85:     """
 86: 
 87:     # Resource type hierarchy (parent -> child)
 88:     HIERARCHY = {
 89:         "organization": "workspace",
 90:         "workspace": "namespace",
 91:         "namespace": None,
 92:     }
 93: 
 94:     def __init__(self) -> None:
 95:         """Initialize the ACL checker."""
 96:         # In-memory permission store for quick lookups
 97:         # In production, this would be backed by the database
 98:         self._grants: list[PermissionGrant] = []
 99: 
100:     def grant(
101:         self,
102:         principal: Principal,
103:         resource_type: str,
104:         resource_id: UUID,
105:         permission: Permission,
106:     ) -> PermissionGrant:
107:         """Grant a permission to a principal.
108: 
109:         Args:
110:             principal: Principal to grant permission to
111:             resource_type: Type of resource
112:             resource_id: ID of resource
113:             permission: Permission to grant
114: 
115:         Returns:
116:             PermissionGrant object
117:         """
118:         grant = PermissionGrant(
119:             principal=principal,
120:             resource_type=resource_type,
121:             resource_id=resource_id,
122:             permission=permission,
123:         )
124:         self._grants.append(grant)
125:         logger.debug(
126:             f"Granted {permission.value} on {resource_type}/{resource_id} to {principal.principal_type}:{principal.principal_id}"
127:         )
128:         return grant
129: 
130:     def revoke(
131:         self,
132:         principal: Principal,
133:         resource_type: str,
134:         resource_id: UUID,
135:         permission: Permission | None = None,
136:     ) -> int:
137:         """Revoke permissions from a principal.
138: 
139:         Args:
140:             principal: Principal to revoke from
141:             resource_type: Type of resource
142:             resource_id: ID of resource
143:             permission: Specific permission to revoke (None = all)
144: 
145:         Returns:
146:             Number of grants revoked
147:         """
148:         before = len(self._grants)
149:         self._grants = [
150:             g
151:             for g in self._grants
152:             if not (
153:                 g.principal.principal_type == principal.principal_type
154:                 and g.principal.principal_id == principal.principal_id
155:                 and g.resource_type == resource_type
156:                 and g.resource_id == resource_id
157:                 and (permission is None or g.permission == permission)
158:             )
159:         ]
160:         revoked = before - len(self._grants)
161:         if revoked:
162:             logger.debug(f"Revoked {revoked} grants from {principal.principal_type}:{principal.principal_id}")
163:         return revoked
164: 
165:     def check(
166:         self,
167:         principal: Principal,
168:         resource_type: str,
169:         resource_id: UUID,
170:         required_permission: Permission,
171:         *,
172:         parent_ids: dict[str, UUID] | None = None,
173:     ) -> bool:
174:         """Check if a principal has a permission on a resource.
175: 
176:         Checks both direct grants and inherited permissions from parent resources.
177: 
178:         Args:
179:             principal: Principal to check
180:             resource_type: Type of resource
181:             resource_id: ID of resource
182:             required_permission: Permission required
183:             parent_ids: Optional dict of parent resource IDs for inheritance
184: 
185:         Returns:
186:             True if permission is granted
187:         """
188:         # System principal always has access
189:         if principal.principal_type == "system":
190:             return True
191: 
192:         # Check direct grant
193:         if self._has_direct_grant(principal, resource_type, resource_id, required_permission):
194:             return True
195: 
196:         # Check inherited permissions from parent resources
197:         if parent_ids:
198:             for parent_type, parent_id in self._get_parent_chain(resource_type, parent_ids):
199:                 if self._has_direct_grant(principal, parent_type, parent_id, required_permission):
200:                     return True
201: 
202:         return False
203: 
204:     def _has_direct_grant(
205:         self,
206:         principal: Principal,
207:         resource_type: str,
208:         resource_id: UUID,
209:         required_permission: Permission,
210:     ) -> bool:
211:         """Check for a direct grant (no inheritance)."""
212:         for grant in self._grants:
213:             if (
214:                 grant.principal.principal_type == principal.principal_type
215:                 and grant.principal.principal_id == principal.principal_id
216:                 and grant.resource_type == resource_type
217:                 and grant.resource_id == resource_id
218:                 and grant.permission >= required_permission
219:             ):
220:                 return True
221:         return False
222: 
223:     def _get_parent_chain(
224:         self,
225:         resource_type: str,
226:         parent_ids: dict[str, UUID],
227:     ) -> list[tuple[str, UUID]]:
228:         """Get the chain of parent resources for inheritance."""
229:         chain = []
230:         current_type = resource_type
231: 
232:         # Walk up the hierarchy
233:         for parent_type, child_type in self.HIERARCHY.items():
234:             if child_type == current_type and parent_type in parent_ids:
235:                 chain.append((parent_type, parent_ids[parent_type]))
236:                 current_type = parent_type
237: 
238:         return chain
239: 
240:     def get_effective_permissions(
241:         self,
242:         principal: Principal,
243:         resource_type: str,
244:         resource_id: UUID,
245:         *,
246:         parent_ids: dict[str, UUID] | None = None,
247:     ) -> list[PermissionGrant]:
248:         """Get all effective permissions for a principal on a resource.
249: 
250:         Includes both direct and inherited permissions.
251: 
252:         Args:
253:             principal: Principal to check
254:             resource_type: Type of resource
255:             resource_id: ID of resource
256:             parent_ids: Optional dict of parent resource IDs
257: 
258:         Returns:
259:             List of effective PermissionGrant objects
260:         """
261:         effective = []
262: 
263:         # Direct grants
264:         for grant in self._grants:
265:             if (
266:                 grant.principal.principal_type == principal.principal_type
267:                 and grant.principal.principal_id == principal.principal_id
268:                 and grant.resource_type == resource_type
269:                 and grant.resource_id == resource_id
270:             ):
271:                 effective.append(grant)
272: 
273:         # Inherited grants
274:         if parent_ids:
275:             for parent_type, parent_id in self._get_parent_chain(resource_type, parent_ids):
276:                 for grant in self._grants:
277:                     if (
278:                         grant.principal.principal_type == principal.principal_type
279:                         and grant.principal.principal_id == principal.principal_id
280:                         and grant.resource_type == parent_type
281:                         and grant.resource_id == parent_id
282:                     ):
283:                         # Mark as inherited
284:                         inherited_grant = PermissionGrant(
285:                             principal=grant.principal,
286:                             resource_type=resource_type,
287:                             resource_id=resource_id,
288:                             permission=grant.permission,
289:                             inherited_from=(parent_type, parent_id),
290:                         )
291:                         effective.append(inherited_grant)
292: 
293:         return effective
294: 
295:     def list_grants(
296:         self,
297:         *,
298:         principal: Principal | None = None,
299:         resource_type: str | None = None,
300:         resource_id: UUID | None = None,
301:     ) -> list[PermissionGrant]:
302:         """List grants with optional filtering.
303: 
304:         Args:
305:             principal: Filter by principal
306:             resource_type: Filter by resource type
307:             resource_id: Filter by resource ID
308: 
309:         Returns:
310:             List of matching grants
311:         """
312:         grants = self._grants
313: 
314:         if principal:
315:             grants = [
316:                 g
317:                 for g in grants
318:                 if g.principal.principal_type == principal.principal_type
319:                 and g.principal.principal_id == principal.principal_id
320:             ]
321: 
322:         if resource_type:
323:             grants = [g for g in grants if g.resource_type == resource_type]
324: 
325:         if resource_id:
326:             grants = [g for g in grants if g.resource_id == resource_id]
327: 
328:         return grants
````

## File: src/khora/acl/enforcer.py
````python
  1: """Cross-layer ACL enforcement for Khora Memory Lake."""
  2: 
  3: from __future__ import annotations
  4: 
  5: from collections.abc import Callable
  6: from dataclasses import dataclass
  7: from functools import wraps
  8: from typing import TYPE_CHECKING, Any, TypeVar
  9: from uuid import UUID
 10: 
 11: from loguru import logger
 12: 
 13: from .checker import ACLChecker, Permission, Principal
 14: 
 15: if TYPE_CHECKING:
 16:     pass
 17: 
 18: F = TypeVar("F", bound=Callable[..., Any])
 19: 
 20: 
 21: class ACLError(Exception):
 22:     """Raised when an ACL check fails."""
 23: 
 24:     def __init__(
 25:         self,
 26:         message: str,
 27:         *,
 28:         principal: Principal | None = None,
 29:         resource_type: str | None = None,
 30:         resource_id: UUID | None = None,
 31:         required_permission: Permission | None = None,
 32:     ) -> None:
 33:         super().__init__(message)
 34:         self.principal = principal
 35:         self.resource_type = resource_type
 36:         self.resource_id = resource_id
 37:         self.required_permission = required_permission
 38: 
 39: 
 40: @dataclass
 41: class ACLContext:
 42:     """Context for ACL enforcement containing the current principal."""
 43: 
 44:     principal: Principal
 45:     namespace_id: UUID | None = None
 46:     workspace_id: UUID | None = None
 47:     organization_id: UUID | None = None
 48: 
 49:     @property
 50:     def parent_ids(self) -> dict[str, UUID]:
 51:         """Get parent IDs for permission inheritance."""
 52:         ids = {}
 53:         if self.workspace_id:
 54:             ids["workspace"] = self.workspace_id
 55:         if self.organization_id:
 56:             ids["organization"] = self.organization_id
 57:         return ids
 58: 
 59: 
 60: class ACLEnforcer:
 61:     """Enforces ACL checks across all storage layers.
 62: 
 63:     Provides a unified way to check and enforce permissions
 64:     before operations on any storage backend.
 65:     """
 66: 
 67:     def __init__(self, checker: ACLChecker | None = None) -> None:
 68:         """Initialize the ACL enforcer.
 69: 
 70:         Args:
 71:             checker: ACLChecker instance (creates new one if None)
 72:         """
 73:         self._checker = checker or ACLChecker()
 74:         self._enabled = True
 75: 
 76:     @property
 77:     def checker(self) -> ACLChecker:
 78:         """Get the underlying ACL checker."""
 79:         return self._checker
 80: 
 81:     @property
 82:     def enabled(self) -> bool:
 83:         """Check if ACL enforcement is enabled."""
 84:         return self._enabled
 85: 
 86:     def enable(self) -> None:
 87:         """Enable ACL enforcement."""
 88:         self._enabled = True
 89:         logger.info("ACL enforcement enabled")
 90: 
 91:     def disable(self) -> None:
 92:         """Disable ACL enforcement (for testing/development)."""
 93:         self._enabled = False
 94:         logger.warning("ACL enforcement disabled")
 95: 
 96:     def check_permission(
 97:         self,
 98:         context: ACLContext,
 99:         resource_type: str,
100:         resource_id: UUID,
101:         required_permission: Permission,
102:     ) -> bool:
103:         """Check if the current principal has permission.
104: 
105:         Args:
106:             context: ACL context with principal
107:             resource_type: Type of resource
108:             resource_id: ID of resource
109:             required_permission: Permission required
110: 
111:         Returns:
112:             True if permitted
113: 
114:         Raises:
115:             ACLError: If permission denied
116:         """
117:         if not self._enabled:
118:             return True
119: 
120:         has_permission = self._checker.check(
121:             context.principal,
122:             resource_type,
123:             resource_id,
124:             required_permission,
125:             parent_ids=context.parent_ids,
126:         )
127: 
128:         if not has_permission:
129:             raise ACLError(
130:                 f"Permission denied: {context.principal.principal_type}:{context.principal.principal_id} "
131:                 f"requires {required_permission.value} on {resource_type}/{resource_id}",
132:                 principal=context.principal,
133:                 resource_type=resource_type,
134:                 resource_id=resource_id,
135:                 required_permission=required_permission,
136:             )
137: 
138:         return True
139: 
140:     def check_namespace_read(self, context: ACLContext, namespace_id: UUID) -> bool:
141:         """Check read permission on a namespace."""
142:         return self.check_permission(context, "namespace", namespace_id, Permission.READ)
143: 
144:     def check_namespace_write(self, context: ACLContext, namespace_id: UUID) -> bool:
145:         """Check write permission on a namespace."""
146:         return self.check_permission(context, "namespace", namespace_id, Permission.WRITE)
147: 
148:     def check_namespace_admin(self, context: ACLContext, namespace_id: UUID) -> bool:
149:         """Check admin permission on a namespace."""
150:         return self.check_permission(context, "namespace", namespace_id, Permission.ADMIN)
151: 
152:     def check_workspace_read(self, context: ACLContext, workspace_id: UUID) -> bool:
153:         """Check read permission on a workspace."""
154:         return self.check_permission(context, "workspace", workspace_id, Permission.READ)
155: 
156:     def check_workspace_admin(self, context: ACLContext, workspace_id: UUID) -> bool:
157:         """Check admin permission on a workspace."""
158:         return self.check_permission(context, "workspace", workspace_id, Permission.ADMIN)
159: 
160:     def check_organization_read(self, context: ACLContext, organization_id: UUID) -> bool:
161:         """Check read permission on an organization."""
162:         return self.check_permission(context, "organization", organization_id, Permission.READ)
163: 
164:     def check_organization_admin(self, context: ACLContext, organization_id: UUID) -> bool:
165:         """Check admin permission on an organization."""
166:         return self.check_permission(context, "organization", organization_id, Permission.ADMIN)
167: 
168:     def require(
169:         self,
170:         resource_type: str,
171:         permission: Permission,
172:         *,
173:         resource_id_param: str = "namespace_id",
174:         context_param: str = "context",
175:     ) -> Callable[[F], F]:
176:         """Decorator to require a permission for a function.
177: 
178:         Usage:
179:             @enforcer.require("namespace", Permission.WRITE)
180:             async def create_document(context: ACLContext, namespace_id: UUID, ...):
181:                 ...
182: 
183:         Args:
184:             resource_type: Type of resource to check
185:             permission: Required permission
186:             resource_id_param: Name of parameter containing resource ID
187:             context_param: Name of parameter containing ACLContext
188: 
189:         Returns:
190:             Decorator function
191:         """
192: 
193:         def decorator(func: F) -> F:
194:             @wraps(func)
195:             async def wrapper(*args: Any, **kwargs: Any) -> Any:
196:                 # Get context and resource_id from kwargs
197:                 context = kwargs.get(context_param)
198:                 resource_id = kwargs.get(resource_id_param)
199: 
200:                 if context is None or resource_id is None:
201:                     raise ValueError(f"Missing required parameter: {context_param} or {resource_id_param}")
202: 
203:                 # Check permission
204:                 self.check_permission(context, resource_type, resource_id, permission)
205: 
206:                 return await func(*args, **kwargs)
207: 
208:             return wrapper  # type: ignore
209: 
210:         return decorator
211: 
212: 
213: # Default enforcer instance
214: _default_enforcer: ACLEnforcer | None = None
215: 
216: 
217: def get_enforcer() -> ACLEnforcer:
218:     """Get the default ACL enforcer.
219: 
220:     Returns:
221:         Default ACLEnforcer instance
222:     """
223:     global _default_enforcer
224:     if _default_enforcer is None:
225:         _default_enforcer = ACLEnforcer()
226:     return _default_enforcer
````

## File: src/khora/api/routes/memory.py
````python
  1: """Memory CRUD API routes for Khora Memory Lake."""
  2: 
  3: from __future__ import annotations
  4: 
  5: from typing import Any
  6: from uuid import UUID
  7: 
  8: from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException, Query, status
  9: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field
 10: 
 11: from khora.api.deps import ACLEnforcerDep, MemoryLakeDep, PrincipalDep
 12: from khora.query import SearchMode
 13: 
 14: router = APIRouter(prefix="/memory", tags=["memory"])
 15: 
 16: 
 17: # =============================================================================
 18: # Request/Response Models
 19: # =============================================================================
 20: 
 21: 
 22: class RememberRequest(BaseModel):
 23:     """Request to store a memory."""
 24: 
 25:     content: str = Field(..., description="Content to remember")
 26:     namespace_id: UUID | None = Field(None, description="Target namespace (uses default if not specified)")
 27:     title: str = Field("", description="Optional title")
 28:     source: str = Field("", description="Optional source identifier")
 29:     metadata: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict, description="Optional metadata")
 30:     skill_name: str = Field("general_entities", description="Extraction skill to use")
 31: 
 32: 
 33: class RememberResponse(BaseModel):
 34:     """Response from remember operation."""
 35: 
 36:     document_id: str
 37:     namespace_id: str
 38:     chunks_created: int
 39:     entities_extracted: int
 40:     relationships_created: int
 41: 
 42: 
 43: class RecallRequest(BaseModel):
 44:     """Request to recall memories."""
 45: 
 46:     query: str = Field(..., description="Search query")
 47:     namespace_id: UUID | None = Field(None, description="Namespace to search (uses default if not specified)")
 48:     limit: int = Field(10, ge=1, le=100, description="Maximum results")
 49:     mode: str = Field("hybrid", description="Search mode: vector, graph, hybrid, all")
 50:     min_similarity: float = Field(0.5, ge=0.0, le=1.0, description="Minimum similarity threshold")
 51: 
 52: 
 53: class ChunkResult(BaseModel):
 54:     """A chunk in recall results."""
 55: 
 56:     id: str
 57:     content: str
 58:     document_id: str
 59:     score: float
 60: 
 61: 
 62: class EntityResult(BaseModel):
 63:     """An entity in recall results."""
 64: 
 65:     id: str
 66:     name: str
 67:     entity_type: str
 68:     description: str
 69:     score: float
 70: 
 71: 
 72: class RecallResponse(BaseModel):
 73:     """Response from recall operation."""
 74: 
 75:     query: str
 76:     namespace_id: str
 77:     chunks: list[ChunkResult]
 78:     entities: list[EntityResult]
 79:     context_text: str
 80: 
 81: 
 82: class ForgetRequest(BaseModel):
 83:     """Request to forget a memory."""
 84: 
 85:     document_id: UUID = Field(..., description="Document ID to forget")
 86:     namespace_id: UUID | None = Field(None, description="Namespace for verification")
 87: 
 88: 
 89: class ForgetResponse(BaseModel):
 90:     """Response from forget operation."""
 91: 
 92:     deleted: bool
 93:     document_id: str
 94: 
 95: 
 96: # =============================================================================
 97: # Routes
 98: # =============================================================================
 99: 
100: 
101: @router.post("/remember", response_model=RememberResponse)
102: async def remember(
103:     request: RememberRequest,
104:     lake: MemoryLakeDep,
105:     principal: PrincipalDep,
106:     enforcer: ACLEnforcerDep,
107: ) -> RememberResponse:
108:     """Store content in the memory lake.
109: 
110:     Processes the content through the ingestion pipeline:
111:     1. Creates a document
112:     2. Chunks the content
113:     3. Generates embeddings
114:     4. Extracts entities and relationships
115:     """
116:     try:
117:         result = await lake.remember(
118:             request.content,
119:             namespace=request.namespace_id,
120:             title=request.title,
121:             source=request.source,
122:             metadata=request.metadata,
123:             skill_name=request.skill_name,
124:         )
125: 
126:         return RememberResponse(
127:             document_id=str(result.document_id),
128:             namespace_id=str(result.namespace_id),
129:             chunks_created=result.chunks_created,
130:             entities_extracted=result.entities_extracted,
131:             relationships_created=result.relationships_created,
132:         )
133:     except Exception as e:
134:         raise HTTPException(
135:             status_code=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,
136:             detail=f"Failed to remember: {str(e)}",
137:         )
138: 
139: 
140: @router.post("/recall", response_model=RecallResponse)
141: async def recall(
142:     request: RecallRequest,
143:     lake: MemoryLakeDep,
144:     principal: PrincipalDep,
145: ) -> RecallResponse:
146:     """Recall memories relevant to a query.
147: 
148:     Searches across vector, graph, and keyword indexes
149:     and returns ranked results.
150:     """
151:     # Map mode string to enum
152:     mode_map = {
153:         "vector": SearchMode.VECTOR,
154:         "graph": SearchMode.GRAPH,
155:         "hybrid": SearchMode.HYBRID,
156:         "all": SearchMode.ALL,
157:     }
158:     mode = mode_map.get(request.mode.lower(), SearchMode.HYBRID)
159: 
160:     try:
161:         result = await lake.recall(
162:             request.query,
163:             namespace=request.namespace_id,
164:             limit=request.limit,
165:             mode=mode,
166:             min_similarity=request.min_similarity,
167:         )
168: 
169:         # Convert to response format
170:         chunks = [
171:             ChunkResult(
172:                 id=str(chunk.id),
173:                 content=chunk.content,
174:                 document_id=str(chunk.document_id),
175:                 score=score,
176:             )
177:             for chunk, score in result.chunks
178:         ]
179: 
180:         entities = [
181:             EntityResult(
182:                 id=str(entity.id),
183:                 name=entity.name,
184:                 entity_type=entity.entity_type.value,
185:                 description=entity.description,
186:                 score=score,
187:             )
188:             for entity, score in result.entities
189:         ]
190: 
191:         return RecallResponse(
192:             query=result.query,
193:             namespace_id=str(result.namespace_id),
194:             chunks=chunks,
195:             entities=entities,
196:             context_text=result.context_text,
197:         )
198:     except Exception as e:
199:         raise HTTPException(
200:             status_code=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,
201:             detail=f"Failed to recall: {str(e)}",
202:         )
203: 
204: 
205: @router.delete("/forget", response_model=ForgetResponse)
206: async def forget(
207:     request: ForgetRequest,
208:     lake: MemoryLakeDep,
209:     principal: PrincipalDep,
210:     enforcer: ACLEnforcerDep,
211: ) -> ForgetResponse:
212:     """Remove a memory from the lake."""
213:     try:
214:         deleted = await lake.forget(
215:             request.document_id,
216:             namespace=request.namespace_id,
217:         )
218: 
219:         return ForgetResponse(
220:             deleted=deleted,
221:             document_id=str(request.document_id),
222:         )
223:     except Exception as e:
224:         raise HTTPException(
225:             status_code=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,
226:             detail=f"Failed to forget: {str(e)}",
227:         )
228: 
229: 
230: @router.get("/documents/{document_id}")
231: async def get_document(
232:     document_id: UUID,
233:     lake: MemoryLakeDep,
234:     principal: PrincipalDep,
235: ) -> dict[str, Any]:
236:     """Get a document by ID."""
237:     document = await lake.storage.get_document(document_id)
238:     if not document:
239:         raise HTTPException(
240:             status_code=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND,
241:             detail=f"Document not found: {document_id}",
242:         )
243: 
244:     return {
245:         "id": str(document.id),
246:         "namespace_id": str(document.namespace_id),
247:         "status": document.status.value,
248:         "title": document.metadata.title,
249:         "source": document.metadata.source,
250:         "chunk_count": document.chunk_count,
251:         "entity_count": document.entity_count,
252:         "created_at": document.created_at.isoformat(),
253:         "processed_at": document.processed_at.isoformat() if document.processed_at else None,
254:     }
255: 
256: 
257: @router.get("/entities")
258: async def list_entities(
259:     lake: MemoryLakeDep,
260:     principal: PrincipalDep,
261:     namespace_id: UUID | None = Query(None),
262:     entity_type: str | None = Query(None),
263:     limit: int = Query(100, ge=1, le=1000),
264: ) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
265:     """List entities in a namespace."""
266:     entities = await lake.list_entities(
267:         namespace=namespace_id,
268:         entity_type=entity_type,
269:         limit=limit,
270:     )
271: 
272:     return [
273:         {
274:             "id": str(e.id),
275:             "name": e.name,
276:             "entity_type": e.entity_type.value,
277:             "description": e.description,
278:             "mention_count": e.mention_count,
279:             "confidence": e.confidence,
280:         }
281:         for e in entities
282:     ]
283: 
284: 
285: @router.get("/entities/{entity_id}")
286: async def get_entity(
287:     entity_id: UUID,
288:     lake: MemoryLakeDep,
289:     principal: PrincipalDep,
290: ) -> dict[str, Any]:
291:     """Get an entity by ID."""
292:     entity = await lake.get_entity(entity_id)
293:     if not entity:
294:         raise HTTPException(
295:             status_code=status.HTTP_404_NOT_FOUND,
296:             detail=f"Entity not found: {entity_id}",
297:         )
298: 
299:     return {
300:         "id": str(entity.id),
301:         "namespace_id": str(entity.namespace_id),
302:         "name": entity.name,
303:         "entity_type": entity.entity_type.value,
304:         "description": entity.description,
305:         "attributes": entity.attributes,
306:         "mention_count": entity.mention_count,
307:         "confidence": entity.confidence,
308:         "source_document_ids": [str(d) for d in entity.source_document_ids],
309:         "created_at": entity.created_at.isoformat(),
310:     }
311: 
312: 
313: @router.get("/entities/{entity_id}/related")
314: async def get_related_entities(
315:     entity_id: UUID,
316:     lake: MemoryLakeDep,
317:     principal: PrincipalDep,
318:     max_depth: int = Query(2, ge=1, le=5),
319:     limit: int = Query(20, ge=1, le=100),
320: ) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
321:     """Get entities related to a given entity."""
322:     related = await lake.find_related_entities(
323:         entity_id,
324:         max_depth=max_depth,
325:         limit=limit,
326:     )
327: 
328:     return [
329:         {
330:             "id": str(e.id),
331:             "name": e.name,
332:             "entity_type": e.entity_type.value,
333:             "relevance_score": score,
334:         }
335:         for e, score in related
336:     ]
````

````python
 23:     """Request to create an organization."""
 24:

 91:     request: CreateOrganizationRequest,
 92:     lake: MemoryLakeDep,
 93:     principal: PrincipalDep,
 94:     enforcer: ACLEnforcerDep,
 95: ) -> OrganizationResponse:
 96:     """Create a new organization."""
 97:     org = Organization(
 98:         name=request.name,
 99:         slug=request.slug or request.name.lower().replace(" ", "-"),
100:         metadata=request.metadata,
101:     )
102: 
103:     try:
104:         created = await lake.storage.create_organization(org)
105:         return OrganizationResponse(
106:             id=str(created.id),

108:             slug=created.slug,
109:             tenancy_mode=created.tenancy_mode.value,

292: async def list_namespaces(
293:     workspace_id: UUID,
294:     lake: MemoryLakeDep,
295:     principal: PrincipalDep,
296: ) -> list[NamespaceResponse]:
297:     """List namespaces in a workspace."""
298:     namespaces = await lake.storage.list_namespaces(workspace_id)
299: 
300:     return [
301:         NamespaceResponse(
302:             id=str(n.id),
303:             workspace_id=str(n.workspace_id),
304:             name=n.name,
305:             slug=n.slug,
306:             description=n.description,
307:             config_overrides=n.config_overrides,
308:             created_at=n.created_at.isoformat(),
309:         )
310:         for n in namespaces
311:     ]
````

````python
33:         Health status with timestamp
34:     """

36:         "status": "healthy",
37:         "timestamp": datetime.now(UTC).isoformat(),

43: async def readiness_check(request: Request) -> dict[str, Any]:
44:     """Readiness check for Kubernetes/orchestration.
45: 
46:     Checks that all required services are available.
47: 
48:     Returns:
49:         Readiness status with component checks
50:     """

52:     checks: dict[str, bool] = {}
53:

55:     # - Database connections
56:     # - External services
57:

59:     checks["config_loaded"] = config is not None
60:

65:         "timestamp": datetime.now(UTC).isoformat(),
66:         "checks": checks,
67:     }

76:     Returns:
````

## File: src/khora/api/routes/sync.py
````python
  1: """Sync management API routes for Khora Memory Lake."""
  2: 
  3: from __future__ import annotations
  4: 
  5: from typing import Any
  6: from uuid import UUID
  7: 
  8: from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException, status
  9: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field
 10: 
 11: from khora.api.deps import ACLEnforcerDep, MemoryLakeDep, PrincipalDep
 12: from khora.pipelines import PipelineManager
 13: 
 14: router = APIRouter(prefix="/sync", tags=["sync"])
 15: 
 16: 
 17: # =============================================================================
 18: # Request/Response Models
 19: # =============================================================================
 20: 
 21: 
 22: class IngestRequest(BaseModel):
 23:     """Request to ingest documents."""
 24: 
 25:     namespace_id: UUID
 26:     documents: list[dict[str, Any]] = Field(..., description="List of documents with 'content' key")
 27:     skill_name: str = Field("general_entities", description="Extraction skill to use")
 28: 
 29: 
 30: class IngestResponse(BaseModel):
 31:     """Response from ingestion."""
 32: 
 33:     total_documents: int
 34:     processed_documents: int
 35:     skipped_documents: int
 36:     total_chunks: int
 37:     total_entities: int
 38:     total_relationships: int
 39: 
 40: 
 41: class SyncRequest(BaseModel):
 42:     """Request to sync from an external source."""
 43: 
 44:     namespace_id: UUID
 45:     source: str = Field(..., description="Source name (e.g., 'github', 'notion')")
 46:     connector_config: dict[str, Any] = Field(default_factory=dict, description="Connector configuration")
 47:     skill_name: str = Field("general_entities", description="Extraction skill to use")
 48: 
 49: 
 50: class SyncResponse(BaseModel):
 51:     """Response from sync operation."""
 52: 
 53:     source: str
 54:     documents_fetched: int
 55:     documents_processed: int
 56:     checkpoint: str | None
 57: 
 58: 
 59: class CheckpointResponse(BaseModel):
 60:     """Sync checkpoint response."""
 61: 
 62:     namespace_id: str
 63:     source: str
 64:     checkpoint: str | None
 65: 
 66: 
 67: # =============================================================================
 68: # Routes
 69: # =============================================================================
 70: 
 71: 
 72: @router.post("/ingest", response_model=IngestResponse)
 73: async def ingest_documents(
 74:     request: IngestRequest,
 75:     lake: MemoryLakeDep,
 76:     principal: PrincipalDep,
 77:     enforcer: ACLEnforcerDep,
 78: ) -> IngestResponse:
 79:     """Ingest documents into the memory lake.
 80: 
 81:     This endpoint runs the full ingestion pipeline:
 82:     1. Stage documents (checksum-based change detection)
 83:     2. Chunk documents
 84:     3. Generate embeddings
 85:     4. Extract entities and relationships
 86:     """
 87:     manager = PipelineManager(storage=lake.storage)
 88: 
 89:     try:
 90:         run = await manager.run_ingestion(
 91:             request.namespace_id,
 92:             request.documents,
 93:             skill_name=request.skill_name,
 94:         )
 95: 
 96:         result = run.metadata.get("result", {})
 97:         return IngestResponse(
 98:             total_documents=result.get("total_documents", len(request.documents)),
 99:             processed_documents=result.get("processed_documents", 0),
100:             skipped_documents=result.get("skipped_documents", 0),
101:             total_chunks=result.get("total_chunks", 0),
102:             total_entities=result.get("total_entities", 0),
103:             total_relationships=result.get("total_relationships", 0),
104:         )
105:     except Exception as e:
106:         raise HTTPException(
107:             status_code=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,
108:             detail=f"Ingestion failed: {str(e)}",
109:         )
110: 
111: 
112: @router.post("/source", response_model=SyncResponse)
113: async def sync_source(
114:     request: SyncRequest,
115:     lake: MemoryLakeDep,
116:     principal: PrincipalDep,
117:     enforcer: ACLEnforcerDep,
118: ) -> SyncResponse:
119:     """Sync documents from an external source.
120: 
121:     Performs incremental sync using checkpoints to track progress.
122:     """
123:     manager = PipelineManager(storage=lake.storage)
124: 
125:     try:
126:         run = await manager.run_sync(
127:             request.namespace_id,
128:             request.source,
129:             connector_config=request.connector_config,
130:         )
131: 
132:         result = run.metadata.get("result", {})
133:         return SyncResponse(
134:             source=request.source,
135:             documents_fetched=result.get("documents_fetched", 0),
136:             documents_processed=result.get("documents_processed", 0),
137:             checkpoint=result.get("checkpoint"),
138:         )
139:     except Exception as e:
140:         raise HTTPException(
141:             status_code=status.HTTP_500_INTERNAL_SERVER_ERROR,
142:             detail=f"Sync failed: {str(e)}",
143:         )
144: 
145: 
146: @router.get("/checkpoint/{namespace_id}/{source}", response_model=CheckpointResponse)
147: async def get_checkpoint(
148:     namespace_id: UUID,
149:     source: str,
150:     lake: MemoryLakeDep,
151:     principal: PrincipalDep,
152: ) -> CheckpointResponse:
153:     """Get the last sync checkpoint for a source."""
154:     checkpoint = await lake.storage.get_sync_checkpoint(namespace_id, source)
155: 
156:     return CheckpointResponse(
157:         namespace_id=str(namespace_id),
158:         source=source,
159:         checkpoint=checkpoint,
160:     )
161: 
162: 
163: @router.put("/checkpoint/{namespace_id}/{source}")
164: async def set_checkpoint(
165:     namespace_id: UUID,
166:     source: str,
167:     checkpoint: str,
168:     lake: MemoryLakeDep,
169:     principal: PrincipalDep,
170:     enforcer: ACLEnforcerDep,
171: ) -> CheckpointResponse:
172:     """Set the sync checkpoint for a source."""
173:     await lake.storage.set_sync_checkpoint(namespace_id, source, checkpoint)
174: 
175:     return CheckpointResponse(
176:         namespace_id=str(namespace_id),
177:         source=source,
178:         checkpoint=checkpoint,
179:     )
180: 
181: 
182: @router.get("/pipelines")
183: async def list_pipelines(
184:     lake: MemoryLakeDep,
185:     principal: PrincipalDep,
186: ) -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
187:     """List available pipelines."""
188:     from khora.pipelines.registry import get_registry
189: 
190:     registry = get_registry()
191:     pipelines = registry.all_pipelines()
192: 
193:     return [
194:         {
195:             "name": p.name,
196:             "description": p.description,
197:             "tags": p.tags,
198:             "version": p.version,
199:         }
200:         for p in pipelines
201:     ]
````

## File: src/khora/api/deps.py
````python
  1: """FastAPI dependencies for Khora Memory Lake."""
  2: 
  3: from __future__ import annotations
  4: 
  5: from typing import Annotated
  6: from uuid import UUID
  7: 
  8: from fastapi import Depends, Header, HTTPException, Request, status
  9: 
 10: from khora.acl import ACLContext, ACLEnforcer, Principal
 11: from khora.config import KhoraConfig
 12: from khora.memory_lake import MemoryLake
 13: 
 14: # Global instances (set during app startup)
 15: _memory_lake: MemoryLake | None = None
 16: _acl_enforcer: ACLEnforcer | None = None
 17: 
 18: 
 19: def set_memory_lake(lake: MemoryLake) -> None:
 20:     """Set the global MemoryLake instance."""
 21:     global _memory_lake
 22:     _memory_lake = lake
 23: 
 24: 
 25: def set_acl_enforcer(enforcer: ACLEnforcer) -> None:
 26:     """Set the global ACL enforcer."""
 27:     global _acl_enforcer
 28:     _acl_enforcer = enforcer
 29: 
 30: 
 31: async def get_memory_lake() -> MemoryLake:
 32:     """Get the MemoryLake instance."""
 33:     if _memory_lake is None:
 34:         raise HTTPException(
 35:             status_code=status.HTTP_503_SERVICE_UNAVAILABLE,
 36:             detail="Memory Lake not initialized",
 37:         )
 38:     return _memory_lake
 39: 
 40: 
 41: async def get_config(request: Request) -> KhoraConfig:
 42:     """Get the application configuration."""
 43:     return request.app.state.config
 44: 
 45: 
 46: async def get_acl_enforcer() -> ACLEnforcer:
 47:     """Get the ACL enforcer."""
 48:     if _acl_enforcer is None:
 49:         # Return a disabled enforcer if not configured
 50:         enforcer = ACLEnforcer()
 51:         enforcer.disable()
 52:         return enforcer
 53:     return _acl_enforcer
 54: 
 55: 
 56: async def get_current_principal(
 57:     x_user_id: Annotated[str | None, Header()] = None,
 58:     x_api_key: Annotated[str | None, Header()] = None,
 59:     authorization: Annotated[str | None, Header()] = None,
 60: ) -> Principal:
 61:     """Extract the current principal from request headers.
 62: 
 63:     Supports:
 64:     - X-User-ID header for user identification
 65:     - X-API-Key header for API key authentication
 66:     - Authorization header (Bearer token)
 67:     """
 68:     if x_user_id:
 69:         return Principal.user(x_user_id)
 70: 
 71:     if x_api_key:
 72:         return Principal.api_key(x_api_key)
 73: 
 74:     if authorization and authorization.startswith("Bearer "):
 75:         # Extract user from token (simplified - real impl would validate)
 76:         token = authorization[7:]
 77:         return Principal.user(f"token:{token[:8]}")
 78: 
 79:     # Anonymous/system principal for unauthenticated requests
 80:     return Principal.system()
 81: 
 82: 
 83: async def get_acl_context(
 84:     principal: Annotated[Principal, Depends(get_current_principal)],
 85:     namespace_id: UUID | None = None,
 86: ) -> ACLContext:
 87:     """Create an ACL context for the current request."""
 88:     return ACLContext(
 89:         principal=principal,
 90:         namespace_id=namespace_id,
 91:     )
 92: 
 93: 
 94: def require_namespace_read(
 95:     namespace_id: UUID,
 96:     context: ACLContext,
 97:     enforcer: ACLEnforcer,
 98: ) -> None:
 99:     """Require read permission on a namespace."""
100:     enforcer.check_namespace_read(context, namespace_id)
101: 
102: 
103: def require_namespace_write(
104:     namespace_id: UUID,
105:     context: ACLContext,
106:     enforcer: ACLEnforcer,
107: ) -> None:
108:     """Require write permission on a namespace."""
109:     enforcer.check_namespace_write(context, namespace_id)
110: 
111: 
112: # Type aliases for dependency injection
113: MemoryLakeDep = Annotated[MemoryLake, Depends(get_memory_lake)]
114: ConfigDep = Annotated[KhoraConfig, Depends(get_config)]
115: PrincipalDep = Annotated[Principal, Depends(get_current_principal)]
116: ACLEnforcerDep = Annotated[ACLEnforcer, Depends(get_acl_enforcer)]
````

## File: src/khora/cli/__init__.py
````python
 1: """Command-line interface for Khora."""
 2: 
 3: from __future__ import annotations
 4: 
 5: from pathlib import Path
 6: 
 7: import click
 8: 
 9: from ..logging_config import setup_logging
10: from .server import serve
11: 
12: 
13: @click.group()
14: @click.version_option(version="0.0.1")
15: @click.option(
16:     "--log-level",
17:     type=click.Choice(["DEBUG", "INFO", "WARNING", "ERROR"], case_sensitive=False),
18:     default="INFO",
19:     help="Set logging level",
20: )
21: @click.option(
22:     "--json-logs",
23:     is_flag=True,
24:     help="Output logs in JSON format for structured logging",
25: )
26: @click.option(
27:     "--log-file",
28:     type=click.Path(path_type=Path),
29:     help="Write logs to file (in addition to console)",
30: )
31: @click.pass_context
32: def cli(ctx: click.Context, log_level: str, json_logs: bool, log_file: Path | None) -> None:
33:     """Khora - Deyta's memory lake and materialization of knowledge.
34: 
35:     Commands:
36:     - serve: Start the FastAPI server for API access
37:     """
38:     setup_logging(level=log_level.upper(), json_logs=json_logs, log_file=log_file)
39:     ctx.ensure_object(dict)
40:     ctx.obj["log_level"] = log_level
41:     ctx.obj["json_logs"] = json_logs
42: 
43: 
44: # Register commands
45: cli.add_command(serve)
46: 
47: 
48: def main() -> None:
49:     """Main entry point."""
50:     cli()
51: 
52: 
53: __all__ = ["cli", "main"]
````

## File: src/khora/cli/server.py
````python
 1: """Server command for Khora CLI."""
 2: 
 3: from __future__ import annotations
 4: 
 5: import os
 6: from pathlib import Path
 7: 
 8: import click
 9: 
10: 
11: @click.command(name="serve")
12: @click.option(
13:     "--host",
14:     default="127.0.0.1",
15:     help="Host to bind the server to",
16: )
17: @click.option(
18:     "--port",
19:     default=8000,
20:     type=int,
21:     help="Port to bind the server to",
22: )
23: @click.option(
24:     "--reload",
25:     is_flag=True,
26:     help="Enable auto-reload for development",
27: )
28: @click.option(
29:     "--config",
30:     type=click.Path(exists=True, path_type=Path),
31:     help="Path to configuration file",
32: )
33: @click.option(
34:     "--no-auth",
35:     is_flag=True,
36:     help="Disable authentication (for local development)",
37: )
38: @click.pass_context
39: def serve(ctx: click.Context, host: str, port: int, reload: bool, config: Path | None, no_auth: bool) -> None:
40:     """Start the FastAPI server for API access.
41: 
42:     The server provides:
43:     - REST API for knowledge management
44:     - Health check endpoints
45:     """
46:     import uvicorn
47: 
48:     log_level = ctx.obj.get("log_level", "info").lower() if ctx.obj else "info"
49: 
50:     # Set auth enabled flag via environment for reload mode
51:     if no_auth:
52:         os.environ["KHORA_AUTH_ENABLED"] = "false"
53:         click.echo(click.style("Warning: ", fg="yellow") + "Authentication is disabled")
54: 
55:     if reload:
56:         # When reload is enabled, uvicorn needs an import string, not the app object
57:         uvicorn.run(
58:             "khora.api.app:create_app",
59:             host=host,
60:             port=port,
61:             reload=reload,
62:             factory=True,
63:             log_level=log_level,
64:         )
65:     else:
66:         # Without reload, we can pass the app object directly
67:         from ..api.app import create_app
68:         from ..config import load_config
69: 
70:         app_config = load_config(config) if config else load_config()
71: 
72:         # Override auth_enabled if --no-auth is set
73:         if no_auth:
74:             # Create a new config with auth disabled
75:             app_config = app_config.model_copy(update={"auth_enabled": False})
76: 
77:         app = create_app(app_config)
78: 
79:         uvicorn.run(
80:             app,
81:             host=host,
82:             port=port,
83:             log_level=log_level,
84:         )
````

## File: src/khora/config/llm.py
````python
  1: """LiteLLM configuration for unified LLM access.
  2: 
  3: Provides a unified interface to all LLM providers (OpenAI, Anthropic, Google, etc.)
  4: with fallbacks and routing. Based on the memoryman/potemkin pattern.
  5: """
  6: 
  7: from __future__ import annotations
  8: 
  9: import os
 10: from pathlib import Path
 11: from typing import Any
 12: 
 13: import yaml
 14: from loguru import logger
 15: from pydantic import BaseModel, Field
 16: 
 17: 
 18: class LiteLLMConfig(BaseModel):
 19:     """Configuration for LiteLLM unified model access.
 20: 
 21:     This configuration provides a unified interface to all LLM providers
 22:     including OpenAI, Anthropic, Google, and others through LiteLLM.
 23:     """
 24: 
 25:     # Primary model configuration
 26:     model: str = Field(
 27:         default="gpt-4o-mini",
 28:         description="Primary model to use (e.g., gpt-4o-mini, claude-sonnet-4-20250514, gemini-2.0-flash)",
 29:     )
 30:     api_key_env: str = Field(
 31:         default="OPENAI_API_KEY",
 32:         description="Environment variable name for API key",
 33:     )
 34: 
 35:     # Model parameters
 36:     temperature: float = Field(
 37:         default=0.7,
 38:         ge=0.0,
 39:         le=2.0,
 40:         description="Sampling temperature for generation",
 41:     )
 42:     max_tokens: int = Field(
 43:         default=2000,
 44:         gt=0,
 45:         description="Maximum tokens to generate",
 46:     )
 47: 
 48:     # Request configuration
 49:     timeout: int = Field(
 50:         default=30,
 51:         gt=0,
 52:         description="Request timeout in seconds",
 53:     )
 54:     max_retries: int = Field(
 55:         default=3,
 56:         ge=0,
 57:         description="Maximum number of retries on failure",
 58:     )
 59:     retry_wait: int = Field(
 60:         default=2,
 61:         ge=0,
 62:         description="Wait time between retries in seconds",
 63:     )
 64: 
 65:     # Concurrency
 66:     max_concurrent_llm_calls: int = Field(
 67:         default=10,
 68:         gt=0,
 69:         description="Maximum concurrent LLM API calls",
 70:     )
 71: 
 72:     # Router configuration for fallbacks
 73:     model_list: list[dict[str, Any]] | None = Field(
 74:         default=None,
 75:         description="List of model configurations for router fallbacks",
 76:     )
 77:     router_settings: dict[str, Any] | None = Field(
 78:         default=None,
 79:         description="Router settings (routing_strategy, num_retries, etc.)",
 80:     )
 81: 
 82:     # Embedding model configuration
 83:     embedding_model: str = Field(
 84:         default="text-embedding-3-small",
 85:         description="Model to use for embeddings",
 86:     )
 87:     embedding_api_key_env: str | None = Field(
 88:         default=None,
 89:         description="Environment variable for embedding API key (defaults to api_key_env)",
 90:     )
 91:     embedding_dimension: int = Field(
 92:         default=1536,
 93:         gt=0,
 94:         description="Embedding vector dimension",
 95:     )
 96: 
 97:     @classmethod
 98:     def from_yaml(cls, path: str | Path) -> LiteLLMConfig:
 99:         """Load configuration from a YAML file.
100: 
101:         Args:
102:             path: Path to the YAML configuration file
103: 
104:         Returns:
105:             LiteLLMConfig instance
106:         """
107:         path = Path(path)
108:         with path.open() as f:
109:             data = yaml.safe_load(f)
110:         return cls.model_validate(data or {})
111: 
112:     @classmethod
113:     def from_dict(cls, config: dict[str, Any]) -> LiteLLMConfig:
114:         """Create configuration from a dictionary.
115: 
116:         Args:
117:             config: Configuration dictionary (can be nested under 'llm' key)
118: 
119:         Returns:
120:             LiteLLMConfig instance
121:         """
122:         # Handle nested configuration
123:         if "llm" in config:
124:             config = config["llm"]
125: 
126:         # Handle config_file path
127:         if "config_file" in config:
128:             return cls.from_yaml(config["config_file"])
129: 
130:         return cls.model_validate(config)
131: 
132:     def get_api_key(self) -> str:
133:         """Get the API key from environment variable."""
134:         key = os.environ.get(self.api_key_env, "")
135:         if not key:
136:             logger.warning(f"API key environment variable {self.api_key_env} not set")
137:         return key
138: 
139:     def get_embedding_api_key(self) -> str:
140:         """Get the embedding API key from environment variable."""
141:         env_var = self.embedding_api_key_env or self.api_key_env
142:         key = os.environ.get(env_var, "")
143:         if not key:
144:             logger.warning(f"Embedding API key environment variable {env_var} not set")
145:         return key
146: 
147: 
148: def configure_litellm(config: LiteLLMConfig | None = None) -> None:
149:     """Configure LiteLLM with the given configuration.
150: 
151:     This function should be called once at application startup to configure
152:     LiteLLM's global settings.
153: 
154:     Args:
155:         config: LiteLLM configuration (uses defaults if None)
156:     """
157:     try:
158:         import litellm
159:     except ImportError:
160:         logger.warning("litellm package not installed, skipping configuration")
161:         return
162: 
163:     if config is None:
164:         config = LiteLLMConfig()
165: 
166:     # Critical for compatibility across providers
167:     litellm.drop_params = True
168: 
169:     # Disable verbose logging and telemetry
170:     litellm.set_verbose = False
171:     litellm.telemetry = False
172: 
173:     # Set up API keys from environment
174:     api_key = config.get_api_key()
175:     if api_key:
176:         # LiteLLM uses provider-specific env vars, so we ensure they're set
177:         if "openai" in config.model.lower() or config.model.startswith("gpt"):
178:             os.environ.setdefault("OPENAI_API_KEY", api_key)
179:         elif "claude" in config.model.lower() or "anthropic" in config.model.lower():
180:             os.environ.setdefault("ANTHROPIC_API_KEY", api_key)
181:         elif "gemini" in config.model.lower():
182:             os.environ.setdefault("GOOGLE_API_KEY", api_key)
183: 
184:     logger.info(f"LiteLLM configured with model: {config.model}")
185: 
186: 
187: def create_litellm_router(config: LiteLLMConfig) -> Any:
188:     """Create a LiteLLM router for fallback handling.
189: 
190:     Args:
191:         config: LiteLLM configuration with model_list
192: 
193:     Returns:
194:         LiteLLM Router instance
195:     """
196:     try:
197:         from litellm import Router
198:     except ImportError:
199:         logger.warning("litellm package not installed")
200:         return None
201: 
202:     if not config.model_list:
203:         logger.warning("No model_list configured, router not created")
204:         return None
205: 
206:     router_settings = config.router_settings or {
207:         "routing_strategy": "simple-shuffle",
208:         "num_retries": config.max_retries,
209:     }
210: 
211:     router = Router(
212:         model_list=config.model_list,
213:         **router_settings,
214:     )
215: 
216:     logger.info(f"LiteLLM router created with {len(config.model_list)} models")
217:     return router
218: 
219: 
220: async def acompletion(
221:     prompt: str,
222:     config: LiteLLMConfig | None = None,
223:     *,
224:     system_prompt: str | None = None,
225:     **kwargs: Any,
226: ) -> str:
227:     """Async completion with LiteLLM.
228: 
229:     Args:
230:         prompt: User prompt
231:         config: LiteLLM configuration (uses defaults if None)
232:         system_prompt: Optional system prompt
233:         **kwargs: Additional arguments passed to litellm.acompletion
234: 
235:     Returns:
236:         Generated text response
237:     """
238:     try:
239:         import litellm
240:     except ImportError:
241:         raise RuntimeError("litellm package not installed. Run: pip install litellm")
242: 
243:     if config is None:
244:         config = LiteLLMConfig()
245: 
246:     messages = []
247:     if system_prompt:
248:         messages.append({"role": "system", "content": system_prompt})
249:     messages.append({"role": "user", "content": prompt})
250: 
251:     response = await litellm.acompletion(
252:         model=config.model,
253:         messages=messages,
254:         temperature=kwargs.pop("temperature", config.temperature),
255:         max_tokens=kwargs.pop("max_tokens", config.max_tokens),
256:         timeout=kwargs.pop("timeout", config.timeout),
257:         num_retries=kwargs.pop("num_retries", config.max_retries),
258:         **kwargs,
259:     )
260: 
261:     return response.choices[0].message.content
262: 
263: 
264: async def aembedding(
265:     text: str | list[str],
266:     config: LiteLLMConfig | None = None,
267:     **kwargs: Any,
268: ) -> list[list[float]]:
269:     """Async embedding generation with LiteLLM.
270: 
271:     Args:
272:         text: Text or list of texts to embed
273:         config: LiteLLM configuration (uses defaults if None)
274:         **kwargs: Additional arguments passed to litellm.aembedding
275: 
276:     Returns:
277:         List of embedding vectors
278:     """
279:     try:
280:         import litellm
281:     except ImportError:
282:         raise RuntimeError("litellm package not installed. Run: pip install litellm")
283: 
284:     if config is None:
285:         config = LiteLLMConfig()
286: 
287:     # Ensure text is a list
288:     if isinstance(text, str):
289:         text = [text]
290: 
291:     response = await litellm.aembedding(
292:         model=config.embedding_model,
293:         input=text,
294:         timeout=kwargs.pop("timeout", config.timeout),
295:         **kwargs,
296:     )
297: 
298:     return [item["embedding"] for item in response.data]
````

## File: src/khora/config/resolver.py
````python
  1: """Hierarchical configuration resolver for Khora Memory Lake.
  2: 
  3: Resolves configuration values with inheritance from namespace -> workspace -> organization -> global.
  4: """
  5: 
  6: from __future__ import annotations
  7: 
  8: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
  9: from typing import TYPE_CHECKING, Any
 10: from uuid import UUID
 11: 
 12: from loguru import logger
 13: 
 14: if TYPE_CHECKING:
 15:     from khora.core.models import MemoryNamespace, Organization, Workspace
 16:     from khora.storage import StorageCoordinator
 17: 
 18: 
 19: @dataclass
 20: class ResolvedConfig:
 21:     """Resolved configuration with inheritance applied."""
 22: 
 23:     values: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
 24:     sources: dict[str, str] = field(default_factory=dict)  # key -> source level
 25: 
 26:     def get(self, key: str, default: Any = None) -> Any:
 27:         """Get a configuration value."""
 28:         return self.values.get(key, default)
 29: 
 30:     def get_source(self, key: str) -> str | None:
 31:         """Get the source level for a configuration key."""
 32:         return self.sources.get(key)
 33: 
 34: 
 35: class ConfigResolver:
 36:     """Resolves configuration with hierarchical inheritance.
 37: 
 38:     Configuration inheritance order (highest to lowest priority):
 39:     1. Namespace config_overrides
 40:     2. Workspace metadata config
 41:     3. Organization metadata config
 42:     4. Global application config
 43:     """
 44: 
 45:     def __init__(
 46:         self,
 47:         storage: StorageCoordinator | None = None,
 48:         global_config: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 49:     ) -> None:
 50:         """Initialize the config resolver.
 51: 
 52:         Args:
 53:             storage: StorageCoordinator for fetching hierarchy
 54:             global_config: Global application configuration
 55:         """
 56:         self._storage = storage
 57:         self._global_config = global_config or {}
 58: 
 59:     async def resolve_for_namespace(
 60:         self,
 61:         namespace_id: UUID,
 62:         *,
 63:         keys: list[str] | None = None,
 64:     ) -> ResolvedConfig:
 65:         """Resolve configuration for a namespace.
 66: 
 67:         Args:
 68:             namespace_id: Namespace to resolve config for
 69:             keys: Optional list of keys to resolve (None = all)
 70: 
 71:         Returns:
 72:             ResolvedConfig with inherited values
 73:         """
 74:         if self._storage is None:
 75:             return ResolvedConfig(values=dict(self._global_config), sources={k: "global" for k in self._global_config})
 76: 
 77:         # Fetch namespace
 78:         namespace = await self._storage.get_namespace(namespace_id)
 79:         if namespace is None:
 80:             logger.warning(f"Namespace {namespace_id} not found")
 81:             return ResolvedConfig(values=dict(self._global_config), sources={k: "global" for k in self._global_config})
 82: 
 83:         # Fetch workspace
 84:         workspace = await self._storage.get_workspace(namespace.workspace_id)
 85: 
 86:         # Fetch organization if workspace exists
 87:         organization = None
 88:         if workspace:
 89:             organization = await self._storage.get_organization(workspace.organization_id)
 90: 
 91:         return self._merge_configs(
 92:             namespace=namespace,
 93:             workspace=workspace,
 94:             organization=organization,
 95:             keys=keys,
 96:         )
 97: 
 98:     def _merge_configs(
 99:         self,
100:         namespace: MemoryNamespace | None,
101:         workspace: Workspace | None,
102:         organization: Organization | None,
103:         keys: list[str] | None,
104:     ) -> ResolvedConfig:
105:         """Merge configurations from all levels."""
106:         result = ResolvedConfig()
107: 
108:         # Start with global config
109:         for key, value in self._global_config.items():
110:             if keys is None or key in keys:
111:                 result.values[key] = value
112:                 result.sources[key] = "global"
113: 
114:         # Apply organization config
115:         if organization and organization.metadata:
116:             config = organization.metadata.get("config", {})
117:             for key, value in config.items():
118:                 if keys is None or key in keys:
119:                     result.values[key] = value
120:                     result.sources[key] = "organization"
121: 
122:         # Apply workspace config
123:         if workspace and workspace.metadata:
124:             config = workspace.metadata.get("config", {})
125:             for key, value in config.items():
126:                 if keys is None or key in keys:
127:                     result.values[key] = value
128:                     result.sources[key] = "workspace"
129: 
130:         # Apply namespace config (highest priority)
131:         if namespace and namespace.config_overrides:
132:             for key, value in namespace.config_overrides.items():
133:                 if keys is None or key in keys:
134:                     result.values[key] = value
135:                     result.sources[key] = "namespace"
136: 
137:         return result
138: 
139:     def resolve_immediate(
140:         self,
141:         global_config: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
142:         organization_config: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
143:         workspace_config: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
144:         namespace_config: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
145:     ) -> ResolvedConfig:
146:         """Resolve configuration from provided values (no storage lookup).
147: 
148:         Useful for testing or when hierarchy data is already loaded.
149: 
150:         Args:
151:             global_config: Global configuration
152:             organization_config: Organization-level config
153:             workspace_config: Workspace-level config
154:             namespace_config: Namespace-level config
155: 
156:         Returns:
157:             ResolvedConfig with merged values
158:         """
159:         result = ResolvedConfig()
160: 
161:         # Apply in order of priority (lowest to highest)
162:         for config, source in [
163:             (global_config or self._global_config, "global"),
164:             (organization_config or {}, "organization"),
165:             (workspace_config or {}, "workspace"),
166:             (namespace_config or {}, "namespace"),
167:         ]:
168:             for key, value in config.items():
169:                 result.values[key] = value
170:                 result.sources[key] = source
171: 
172:         return result
173: 
174:     def get_pipeline_config(self, resolved: ResolvedConfig) -> dict[str, Any]:
175:         """Extract pipeline-specific configuration.
176: 
177:         Args:
178:             resolved: ResolvedConfig instance
179: 
180:         Returns:
181:             Pipeline configuration dict
182:         """
183:         return {
184:             "chunking_strategy": resolved.get("chunking_strategy", "semantic"),
185:             "chunk_size": resolved.get("chunk_size", 512),
186:             "chunk_overlap": resolved.get("chunk_overlap", 50),
187:             "embedding_model": resolved.get("embedding_model", "text-embedding-3-small"),
188:             "extraction_model": resolved.get("extraction_model", "gpt-4o-mini"),
189:             "extraction_skill": resolved.get("extraction_skill", "general_entities"),
190:         }
191: 
192:     def get_llm_config(self, resolved: ResolvedConfig) -> dict[str, Any]:
193:         """Extract LLM-specific configuration.
194: 
195:         Args:
196:             resolved: ResolvedConfig instance
197: 
198:         Returns:
199:             LLM configuration dict
200:         """
201:         return {
202:             "model": resolved.get("llm_model", "gpt-4o-mini"),
203:             "temperature": resolved.get("llm_temperature", 0.7),
204:             "max_tokens": resolved.get("llm_max_tokens", 2000),
205:             "timeout": resolved.get("llm_timeout", 30),
206:         }
````
