## File: src/khora/core/models/document.py
````python
  1: """Document and chunk models for Khora Memory Lake.
  2: 
  3: Documents represent source content that is chunked, embedded, and stored
  4: for semantic search and retrieval.
  5: """
  6: 
  7: from __future__ import annotations
  8: 
  9: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
 10: from datetime import UTC, datetime
 11: from enum import Enum
 12: from typing import Any
 13: from uuid import UUID, uuid4
 14: 
 15: 
 16: class DocumentStatus(str, Enum):
 17:     """Document processing status."""
 18: 
 19:     PENDING = "pending"  # Waiting to be processed
 20:     PROCESSING = "processing"  # Currently being processed
 21:     COMPLETED = "completed"  # Successfully processed
 22:     FAILED = "failed"  # Processing failed
 23:     ARCHIVED = "archived"  # Archived, not actively used
 24: 
 25: 
 26: @dataclass
 27: class DocumentMetadata:
 28:     """Metadata associated with a document."""
 29: 
 30:     source: str = ""  # Source identifier (URL, file path, etc.)
 31:     source_type: str = ""  # Type of source (file, url, api, etc.)
 32:     content_type: str = ""  # MIME type or content classification
 33:     title: str = ""
 34:     author: str = ""
 35:     language: str = "en"
 36:     checksum: str = ""  # For change detection
 37:     size_bytes: int = 0
 38:     custom: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
 39: 
 40: 
 41: @dataclass
 42: class Document:
 43:     """A document to be processed and stored in the memory lake.
 44: 
 45:     Documents are the primary input unit. They are chunked, embedded,
 46:     and stored for retrieval. Entities and relationships are extracted
 47:     from documents during processing.
 48:     """
 49: 
 50:     id: UUID = field(default_factory=uuid4)
 51:     namespace_id: UUID = field(default_factory=uuid4)
 52:     content: str = ""
 53:     metadata: DocumentMetadata = field(default_factory=DocumentMetadata)
 54:     status: DocumentStatus = DocumentStatus.PENDING
 55: 
 56:     # Processing info
 57:     chunk_count: int = 0
 58:     entity_count: int = 0
 59:     error_message: str | None = None
 60: 
 61:     # Timestamps
 62:     created_at: datetime = field(default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(UTC))
 63:     updated_at: datetime = field(default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(UTC))
 64:     processed_at: datetime | None = None
 65: 
 66:     @property
 67:     def is_processed(self) -> bool:
 68:         """Check if the document has been successfully processed."""
 69:         return self.status == DocumentStatus.COMPLETED
 70: 
 71:     def mark_processing(self) -> None:
 72:         """Mark the document as currently processing."""
 73:         self.status = DocumentStatus.PROCESSING
 74:         self.updated_at = datetime.now(UTC)
 75: 
 76:     def mark_completed(self, chunk_count: int, entity_count: int) -> None:
 77:         """Mark the document as successfully processed."""
 78:         self.status = DocumentStatus.COMPLETED
 79:         self.chunk_count = chunk_count
 80:         self.entity_count = entity_count
 81:         self.processed_at = datetime.now(UTC)
 82:         self.updated_at = datetime.now(UTC)
 83:         self.error_message = None
 84: 
 85:     def mark_failed(self, error: str) -> None:
 86:         """Mark the document as failed."""
 87:         self.status = DocumentStatus.FAILED
 88:         self.error_message = error
 89:         self.updated_at = datetime.now(UTC)
 90: 
 91: 
 92: @dataclass
 93: class ChunkMetadata:
 94:     """Metadata associated with a chunk."""
 95: 
 96:     document_id: UUID = field(default_factory=uuid4)
 97:     chunk_index: int = 0  # Position in document
 98:     start_char: int = 0  # Start character offset
 99:     end_char: int = 0  # End character offset
100:     token_count: int = 0
101:     custom: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
102: 
103: 
104: @dataclass
105: class Chunk:
106:     """A chunk of text from a document with its embedding.
107: 
108:     Chunks are the unit of storage and retrieval for vector search.
109:     Each chunk has an embedding vector for semantic similarity search.
110:     """
111: 
112:     id: UUID = field(default_factory=uuid4)
113:     namespace_id: UUID = field(default_factory=uuid4)
114:     document_id: UUID = field(default_factory=uuid4)
115:     content: str = ""
116:     metadata: ChunkMetadata = field(default_factory=ChunkMetadata)
117: 
118:     # Embedding vector (stored in pgvector)
119:     embedding: list[float] | None = None
120:     embedding_model: str = ""
121: 
122:     # Timestamps
123:     created_at: datetime = field(default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(UTC))
124: 
125:     @property
126:     def has_embedding(self) -> bool:
127:         """Check if the chunk has an embedding."""
128:         return self.embedding is not None and len(self.embedding) > 0
````

## File: src/khora/core/models/entity.py
````python
  1: """Entity and relationship models for Khora Memory Lake.
  2: 
  3: Entities represent extracted knowledge (people, organizations, concepts, etc.)
  4: and relationships connect them in a knowledge graph stored in Neo4j.
  5: """
  6: 
  7: from __future__ import annotations
  8: 
  9: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
 10: from datetime import UTC, datetime
 11: from enum import Enum
 12: from typing import Any
 13: from uuid import UUID, uuid4
 14: 
 15: 
 16: class EntityType(str, Enum):
 17:     """Standard entity types for knowledge extraction."""
 18: 
 19:     PERSON = "PERSON"
 20:     ORGANIZATION = "ORGANIZATION"
 21:     LOCATION = "LOCATION"
 22:     CONCEPT = "CONCEPT"
 23:     EVENT = "EVENT"
 24:     PRODUCT = "PRODUCT"
 25:     TECHNOLOGY = "TECHNOLOGY"
 26:     DATE = "DATE"
 27:     CUSTOM = "CUSTOM"
 28: 
 29: 
 30: class RelationshipType(str, Enum):
 31:     """Standard relationship types for knowledge graphs."""
 32: 
 33:     # Person relationships
 34:     WORKS_FOR = "WORKS_FOR"
 35:     KNOWS = "KNOWS"
 36:     MANAGES = "MANAGES"
 37:     REPORTS_TO = "REPORTS_TO"
 38:     COLLABORATES_WITH = "COLLABORATES_WITH"
 39: 
 40:     # Organization relationships
 41:     OWNS = "OWNS"
 42:     PART_OF = "PART_OF"
 43:     COMPETES_WITH = "COMPETES_WITH"
 44:     PARTNERS_WITH = "PARTNERS_WITH"
 45: 
 46:     # Location relationships
 47:     LOCATED_IN = "LOCATED_IN"
 48:     HEADQUARTERED_IN = "HEADQUARTERED_IN"
 49: 
 50:     # Concept relationships
 51:     RELATES_TO = "RELATES_TO"
 52:     DEPENDS_ON = "DEPENDS_ON"
 53:     IMPLEMENTS = "IMPLEMENTS"
 54:     DERIVED_FROM = "DERIVED_FROM"
 55: 
 56:     # Temporal relationships
 57:     PRECEDES = "PRECEDES"
 58:     FOLLOWS = "FOLLOWS"
 59:     CONCURRENT_WITH = "CONCURRENT_WITH"
 60: 
 61:     # Generic
 62:     ASSOCIATED_WITH = "ASSOCIATED_WITH"
 63:     CUSTOM = "CUSTOM"
 64: 
 65: 
 66: @dataclass
 67: class Entity:
 68:     """An extracted entity from a document.
 69: 
 70:     Entities are nodes in the knowledge graph stored in Neo4j.
 71:     They represent people, organizations, concepts, and other
 72:     knowledge extracted from documents.
 73:     """
 74: 
 75:     id: UUID = field(default_factory=uuid4)
 76:     namespace_id: UUID = field(default_factory=uuid4)
 77:     name: str = ""
 78:     entity_type: EntityType = EntityType.CONCEPT
 79:     description: str = ""
 80: 
 81:     # Attributes from extraction
 82:     attributes: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
 83: 
 84:     # Source tracking
 85:     source_document_ids: list[UUID] = field(default_factory=list)
 86:     source_chunk_ids: list[UUID] = field(default_factory=list)
 87:     mention_count: int = 1
 88: 
 89:     # Embedding for entity similarity search
 90:     embedding: list[float] | None = None
 91:     embedding_model: str = ""
 92: 
 93:     # Temporal validity
 94:     valid_from: datetime | None = None
 95:     valid_until: datetime | None = None
 96: 
 97:     # Confidence score from extraction
 98:     confidence: float = 1.0
 99: 
100:     metadata: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
101:     created_at: datetime = field(default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(UTC))
102:     updated_at: datetime = field(default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(UTC))
103: 
104:     def merge_with(self, other: Entity) -> None:
105:         """Merge another entity into this one (deduplication)."""
106:         # Combine source references
107:         for doc_id in other.source_document_ids:
108:             if doc_id not in self.source_document_ids:
109:                 self.source_document_ids.append(doc_id)
110:         for chunk_id in other.source_chunk_ids:
111:             if chunk_id not in self.source_chunk_ids:
112:                 self.source_chunk_ids.append(chunk_id)
113: 
114:         # Update mention count
115:         self.mention_count += other.mention_count
116: 
117:         # Merge attributes (prefer existing)
118:         for key, value in other.attributes.items():
119:             if key not in self.attributes:
120:                 self.attributes[key] = value
121: 
122:         # Update confidence (take max)
123:         self.confidence = max(self.confidence, other.confidence)
124: 
125:         # Update description if empty
126:         if not self.description and other.description:
127:             self.description = other.description
128: 
129:         self.updated_at = datetime.now(UTC)
130: 
131: 
132: @dataclass
133: class Relationship:
134:     """A relationship between two entities.
135: 
136:     Relationships are edges in the knowledge graph stored in Neo4j.
137:     They connect entities and describe how they relate to each other.
138:     """
139: 
140:     id: UUID = field(default_factory=uuid4)
141:     namespace_id: UUID = field(default_factory=uuid4)
142:     source_entity_id: UUID = field(default_factory=uuid4)
143:     target_entity_id: UUID = field(default_factory=uuid4)
144:     relationship_type: RelationshipType = RelationshipType.RELATES_TO
145:     description: str = ""
146: 
147:     # Additional properties
148:     properties: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
149: 
150:     # Source tracking
151:     source_document_ids: list[UUID] = field(default_factory=list)
152:     source_chunk_ids: list[UUID] = field(default_factory=list)
153: 
154:     # Temporal validity
155:     valid_from: datetime | None = None
156:     valid_until: datetime | None = None
157: 
158:     # Confidence and weight
159:     confidence: float = 1.0
160:     weight: float = 1.0
161: 
162:     metadata: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
163:     created_at: datetime = field(default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(UTC))
164:     updated_at: datetime = field(default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(UTC))
165: 
166: 
167: @dataclass
168: class Episode:
169:     """An episodic memory representing a temporal event or experience.
170: 
171:     Episodes capture time-bound events with associated entities,
172:     supporting temporal queries and event-based recall.
173:     """
174: 
175:     id: UUID = field(default_factory=uuid4)
176:     namespace_id: UUID = field(default_factory=uuid4)
177:     name: str = ""
178:     description: str = ""
179: 
180:     # Temporal bounds
181:     occurred_at: datetime = field(default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(UTC))
182:     duration_seconds: int | None = None
183: 
184:     # Associated entities
185:     entity_ids: list[UUID] = field(default_factory=list)
186: 
187:     # Source tracking
188:     source_document_ids: list[UUID] = field(default_factory=list)
189:     source_chunk_ids: list[UUID] = field(default_factory=list)
190: 
191:     # Episode embedding for similarity search
192:     embedding: list[float] | None = None
193:     embedding_model: str = ""
194: 
195:     metadata: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
196:     created_at: datetime = field(default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(UTC))
197:     updated_at: datetime = field(default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(UTC))
198: 
199:     @property
200:     def end_time(self) -> datetime | None:
201:         """Calculate the end time of the episode."""
202:         if self.duration_seconds is not None:
203:             from datetime import timedelta
204: 
205:             return self.occurred_at + timedelta(seconds=self.duration_seconds)
206:         return None
````

## File: src/khora/core/models/event.py
````python
  1: """Event sourcing models for Khora Memory Lake.
  2: 
  3: All changes to the memory lake are captured as immutable events,
  4: enabling perfect audit trails, temporal queries, and replay.
  5: """
  6: 
  7: from __future__ import annotations
  8: 
  9: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
 10: from datetime import UTC, datetime
 11: from enum import Enum
 12: from typing import Any
 13: from uuid import UUID, uuid4
 14: 
 15: 
 16: class EventType(str, Enum):
 17:     """Types of events in the memory lake."""
 18: 
 19:     # Document events
 20:     DOCUMENT_CREATED = "document.created"
 21:     DOCUMENT_UPDATED = "document.updated"
 22:     DOCUMENT_DELETED = "document.deleted"
 23:     DOCUMENT_PROCESSED = "document.processed"
 24:     DOCUMENT_FAILED = "document.failed"
 25: 
 26:     # Chunk events
 27:     CHUNK_CREATED = "chunk.created"
 28:     CHUNK_EMBEDDED = "chunk.embedded"
 29:     CHUNK_DELETED = "chunk.deleted"
 30: 
 31:     # Entity events
 32:     ENTITY_CREATED = "entity.created"
 33:     ENTITY_UPDATED = "entity.updated"
 34:     ENTITY_MERGED = "entity.merged"
 35:     ENTITY_DELETED = "entity.deleted"
 36: 
 37:     # Relationship events
 38:     RELATIONSHIP_CREATED = "relationship.created"
 39:     RELATIONSHIP_UPDATED = "relationship.updated"
 40:     RELATIONSHIP_DELETED = "relationship.deleted"
 41: 
 42:     # Episode events
 43:     EPISODE_CREATED = "episode.created"
 44:     EPISODE_UPDATED = "episode.updated"
 45:     EPISODE_DELETED = "episode.deleted"
 46: 
 47:     # Namespace events
 48:     NAMESPACE_CREATED = "namespace.created"
 49:     NAMESPACE_UPDATED = "namespace.updated"
 50:     NAMESPACE_DELETED = "namespace.deleted"
 51: 
 52:     # Sync events
 53:     SYNC_STARTED = "sync.started"
 54:     SYNC_COMPLETED = "sync.completed"
 55:     SYNC_FAILED = "sync.failed"
 56:     SYNC_CHECKPOINT = "sync.checkpoint"
 57: 
 58:     # Query events (for analytics)
 59:     QUERY_EXECUTED = "query.executed"
 60: 
 61: 
 62: @dataclass
 63: class MemoryEvent:
 64:     """An immutable event in the memory lake.
 65: 
 66:     Events form an append-only log of all changes, enabling:
 67:     - Complete audit trail
 68:     - Temporal queries (state at any point in time)
 69:     - Event replay for recovery or migration
 70:     - Change data capture for external systems
 71:     """
 72: 
 73:     id: UUID = field(default_factory=uuid4)
 74:     namespace_id: UUID = field(default_factory=uuid4)
 75:     event_type: EventType = EventType.DOCUMENT_CREATED
 76:     timestamp: datetime = field(default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(UTC))
 77: 
 78:     # Reference to the affected resource
 79:     resource_type: str = ""  # document, chunk, entity, relationship, episode
 80:     resource_id: UUID = field(default_factory=uuid4)
 81: 
 82:     # Event data
 83:     data: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
 84: 
 85:     # Previous state for update events (enables undo)
 86:     previous_data: dict[str, Any] | None = None
 87: 
 88:     # Actor who triggered the event
 89:     actor_id: str | None = None
 90:     actor_type: str = "system"  # system, user, api, pipeline
 91: 
 92:     # Correlation ID for tracking related events
 93:     correlation_id: UUID | None = None
 94: 
 95:     # Version for optimistic locking
 96:     version: int = 1
 97: 
 98:     metadata: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
 99: 
100:     def __post_init__(self) -> None:
101:         """Extract resource type from event type if not set."""
102:         if not self.resource_type and self.event_type:
103:             # Extract from event type (e.g., "document.created" -> "document")
104:             self.resource_type = self.event_type.value.split(".")[0]
105: 
106:     @classmethod
107:     def document_created(cls, namespace_id: UUID, document_id: UUID, data: dict[str, Any], **kwargs) -> MemoryEvent:
108:         """Create a document created event."""
109:         return cls(
110:             namespace_id=namespace_id,
111:             event_type=EventType.DOCUMENT_CREATED,
112:             resource_type="document",
113:             resource_id=document_id,
114:             data=data,
115:             **kwargs,
116:         )
117: 
118:     @classmethod
119:     def entity_created(cls, namespace_id: UUID, entity_id: UUID, data: dict[str, Any], **kwargs) -> MemoryEvent:
120:         """Create an entity created event."""
121:         return cls(
122:             namespace_id=namespace_id,
123:             event_type=EventType.ENTITY_CREATED,
124:             resource_type="entity",
125:             resource_id=entity_id,
126:             data=data,
127:             **kwargs,
128:         )
129: 
130:     @classmethod
131:     def chunk_embedded(cls, namespace_id: UUID, chunk_id: UUID, data: dict[str, Any], **kwargs) -> MemoryEvent:
132:         """Create a chunk embedded event."""
133:         return cls(
134:             namespace_id=namespace_id,
135:             event_type=EventType.CHUNK_EMBEDDED,
136:             resource_type="chunk",
137:             resource_id=chunk_id,
138:             data=data,
139:             **kwargs,
140:         )
141: 
142:     @classmethod
143:     def relationship_created(
144:         cls, namespace_id: UUID, relationship_id: UUID, data: dict[str, Any], **kwargs
145:     ) -> MemoryEvent:
146:         """Create a relationship created event."""
147:         return cls(
148:             namespace_id=namespace_id,
149:             event_type=EventType.RELATIONSHIP_CREATED,
150:             resource_type="relationship",
151:             resource_id=relationship_id,
152:             data=data,
153:             **kwargs,
154:         )
````

## File: src/khora/core/models/tenancy.py
````python
 1: """Multi-tenancy models for Khora Memory Lake.
 2: 
 3: Supports two modes:
 4: - Shared: namespace_id filtering with row-level security
 5: - Isolated: Separate database instances per tenant
 6: """
 7: 
 8: from __future__ import annotations
 9: 
10: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
11: from datetime import UTC, datetime
12: from enum import Enum
13: from typing import Any
14: from uuid import UUID, uuid4
15: 
16: 
17: class TenancyMode(str, Enum):
18:     """Tenancy isolation mode."""
19: 
20:     SHARED = "shared"  # Shared database with namespace_id filtering + row-level security
21:     ISOLATED = "isolated"  # Separate database instances per tenant
22: 
23: 
24: @dataclass
25: class Organization:
26:     """Top-level tenant organization.
27: 
28:     An organization can have multiple workspaces and represents the billing
29:     and administrative boundary for tenants.
30:     """
31: 
32:     id: UUID = field(default_factory=uuid4)
33:     name: str = ""
34:     slug: str = ""  # URL-friendly identifier
35:     tenancy_mode: TenancyMode = TenancyMode.SHARED
36:     metadata: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
37:     created_at: datetime = field(default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(UTC))
38:     updated_at: datetime = field(default_factory=lambda: datetime.now(UTC))
39: 
40:     def __post_init__(self) -> None:
41:         if not self.slug and self.name:
42:             self.slug = self.name.lower().replace(" ", "-")
43:

47:     """Workspace within an organization.

50:     an organization. Each workspace can have multiple memory namespaces.
51:     """

94:             self.slug = self.name.lower().replace(" ", "-")
````

## File: src/khora/db/session.py
````python
  1: """Database session management for Khora."""
  2: 
  3: from __future__ import annotations
  4: 
  5: import os
  6: from collections.abc import AsyncGenerator
  7: from contextlib import asynccontextmanager
  8: 
  9: from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import (
 10:     AsyncEngine,
 11:     AsyncSession,
 12:     async_sessionmaker,
 13:     create_async_engine,
 14: )
 15: 
 16: 
 17: def get_database_url() -> str:
 18:     """Get database URL from environment.
 19: 
 20:     Converts postgresql:// to postgresql+asyncpg:// for async support.
 21:     """
 22:     url = os.getenv("KHORA_DATABASE_URL", "")
 23:     if not url:
 24:         raise ValueError("KHORA_DATABASE_URL environment variable not set")
 25: 
 26:     # Convert to async URL if needed
 27:     if url.startswith("postgresql://"):
 28:         url = url.replace("postgresql://", "postgresql+asyncpg://", 1)
 29:     elif url.startswith("postgres://"):
 30:         url = url.replace("postgres://", "postgresql+asyncpg://", 1)
 31: 
 32:     return url
 33: 
 34: 
 35: _engine: AsyncEngine | None = None
 36: _session_factory: async_sessionmaker[AsyncSession] | None = None
 37: 
 38: 
 39: def get_engine() -> AsyncEngine:
 40:     """Get or create the database engine."""
 41:     global _engine
 42:     if _engine is None:
 43:         _engine = create_async_engine(
 44:             get_database_url(),
 45:             echo=os.getenv("KHORA_DEBUG", "").lower() == "true",
 46:             pool_size=5,
 47:             max_overflow=10,
 48:         )
 49:     return _engine
 50: 
 51: 
 52: def get_session_factory() -> async_sessionmaker[AsyncSession]:
 53:     """Get or create the session factory."""
 54:     global _session_factory
 55:     if _session_factory is None:
 56:         _session_factory = async_sessionmaker(
 57:             get_engine(),
 58:             class_=AsyncSession,
 59:             expire_on_commit=False,
 60:         )
 61:     return _session_factory
 62: 
 63: 
 64: @asynccontextmanager
 65: async def get_db() -> AsyncGenerator[AsyncSession]:
 66:     """Get a database session.
 67: 
 68:     Usage:
 69:         async with get_db() as db:
 70:             result = await db.execute(...)
 71:     """
 72:     session = get_session_factory()()
 73:     try:
 74:         yield session
 75:         await session.commit()
 76:     except Exception:
 77:         await session.rollback()
 78:         raise
 79:     finally:
 80:         await session.close()
 81: 
 82: 
 83: async def init_db() -> None:
 84:     """Initialize database tables.
 85: 
 86:     For development/testing only. Use Alembic migrations in production.
 87:     """
 88:     from .models import Base
 89: 
 90:     engine = get_engine()
 91:     async with engine.begin() as conn:
 92:         await conn.run_sync(Base.metadata.create_all)
 93: 
 94: 
 95: async def close_db() -> None:
 96:     """Close database connections."""
 97:     global _engine, _session_factory
 98:     if _engine:
 99:         await _engine.dispose()
100:         _engine = None
101:         _session_factory = None
102: 
103: 
104: def _run_migrations_sync() -> None:
105:     """Internal function to run migrations synchronously."""
106:     from pathlib import Path
107: 
108:     from loguru import logger
109: 
110:     from alembic import command
111:     from alembic.config import Config
112: 
113:     # Check if database URL is configured
114:     url = os.getenv("KHORA_DATABASE_URL", "")
115:     if not url:
116:         logger.warning("KHORA_DATABASE_URL not set, skipping migrations")
117:         return
118: 
119:     # Find alembic.ini - look in common locations
120:     possible_paths = [
121:         Path(__file__).parent.parent.parent.parent / "alembic.ini",  # src/khora/db -> root
122:         Path.cwd() / "alembic.ini",
123:         Path("/app/alembic.ini"),  # Docker container path
124:     ]
125: 
126:     alembic_cfg_path = None
127:     for path in possible_paths:
128:         if path.exists():
129:             alembic_cfg_path = path
130:             break
131: 
132:     if alembic_cfg_path is None:
133:         logger.warning("alembic.ini not found, skipping migrations")
134:         return
135: 
136:     logger.info(f"Running database migrations from {alembic_cfg_path}")
137: 
138:     alembic_cfg = Config(str(alembic_cfg_path))
139:     # Override the script location to be relative to alembic.ini
140:     alembic_cfg.set_main_option("script_location", str(alembic_cfg_path.parent / "alembic"))
141: 
142:     command.upgrade(alembic_cfg, "head")
143:     logger.info("Database migrations completed")
144: 
145: 
146: async def run_migrations() -> None:
147:     """Run database migrations using Alembic.
148: 
149:     Runs migrations in a thread pool to avoid conflicts with the running event loop.
150:     """
151:     import asyncio
152:     import concurrent.futures
153: 
154:     loop = asyncio.get_running_loop()
155:     with concurrent.futures.ThreadPoolExecutor() as pool:
156:         await loop.run_in_executor(pool, _run_migrations_sync)
````

## File: src/khora/extraction/chunkers/__init__.py
````python
 1: """Text chunking strategies for Khora Memory Lake."""
 2: 
 3: from __future__ import annotations
 4: 
 5: from .base import Chunker, ChunkResult
 6: from .fixed import FixedChunker
 7: from .recursive import RecursiveChunker
 8: from .semantic import SemanticChunker
 9: 
10: 
11: def create_chunker(
12:     strategy: str = "semantic",
13:     *,
14:     chunk_size: int = 512,
15:     chunk_overlap: int = 50,
16:     **kwargs,
17: ) -> Chunker:
18:     """Create a chunker based on the specified strategy.
19: 
20:     Args:
21:         strategy: Chunking strategy (fixed, semantic, recursive)
22:         chunk_size: Target chunk size in tokens
23:         chunk_overlap: Overlap between chunks in tokens
24:         **kwargs: Additional strategy-specific arguments
25: 
26:     Returns:
27:         Configured Chunker instance
28:     """
29:     if strategy == "fixed":
30:         return FixedChunker(chunk_size=chunk_size, chunk_overlap=chunk_overlap)
31:     elif strategy == "semantic":
32:         return SemanticChunker(chunk_size=chunk_size, chunk_overlap=chunk_overlap, **kwargs)
33:     elif strategy == "recursive":
34:         return RecursiveChunker(chunk_size=chunk_size, chunk_overlap=chunk_overlap, **kwargs)
35:     else:
36:         raise ValueError(f"Unknown chunking strategy: {strategy}")
37: 
38: 
39: __all__ = [
40:     "Chunker",
41:     "ChunkResult",
42:     "FixedChunker",
43:     "SemanticChunker",
44:     "RecursiveChunker",
45:     "create_chunker",
46: ]
````

## File: src/khora/extraction/chunkers/base.py
````python
 1: """Base chunker protocol and types."""
 2: 
 3: from __future__ import annotations
 4: 
 5: from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
 6: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
 7: from typing import Any
 8: 
 9: 
10: @dataclass
11: class ChunkResult:
12:     """Result of chunking a document."""
13: 
14:     content: str
15:     index: int
16:     start_char: int
17:     end_char: int
18:     token_count: int
19:     metadata: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
20: 
21: 
22: class Chunker(ABC):
23:     """Abstract base class for text chunkers."""
24: 
25:     def __init__(self, *, chunk_size: int = 512, chunk_overlap: int = 50) -> None:
26:         """Initialize the chunker.
27: 
28:         Args:
29:             chunk_size: Target chunk size in tokens
30:             chunk_overlap: Overlap between chunks in tokens
31:         """
32:         self.chunk_size = chunk_size
33:         self.chunk_overlap = chunk_overlap
34: 
35:     @abstractmethod
36:     def chunk(self, text: str) -> list[ChunkResult]:
37:         """Split text into chunks.
38: 
39:         Args:
40:             text: Text to chunk
41: 
42:         Returns:
43:             List of ChunkResult objects
44:         """
45:         ...
46: 
47:     def count_tokens(self, text: str) -> int:
48:         """Count tokens in text.
49: 
50:         Uses tiktoken for accurate token counting.
51: 
52:         Args:
53:             text: Text to count tokens in
54: 
55:         Returns:
56:             Token count
57:         """
58:         try:
59:             import tiktoken
60: 
61:             encoding = tiktoken.get_encoding("cl100k_base")
62:             return len(encoding.encode(text))
63:         except ImportError:
64:             # Fallback: estimate ~4 chars per token
65:             return len(text) // 4
````

## File: src/khora/extraction/chunkers/fixed.py
````python
  1: """Fixed-size text chunker."""
  2: 
  3: from __future__ import annotations
  4: 
  5: from .base import Chunker, ChunkResult
  6: 
  7: 
  8: class FixedChunker(Chunker):
  9:     """Fixed-size chunker that splits text at token boundaries.
 10: 
 11:     Simple chunking strategy that creates chunks of approximately
 12:     equal size with configurable overlap.
 13:     """
 14: 
 15:     def chunk(self, text: str) -> list[ChunkResult]:
 16:         """Split text into fixed-size chunks.
 17: 
 18:         Args:
 19:             text: Text to chunk
 20: 
 21:         Returns:
 22:             List of ChunkResult objects
 23:         """
 24:         if not text.strip():
 25:             return []
 26: 
 27:         try:
 28:             import tiktoken
 29: 
 30:             encoding = tiktoken.get_encoding("cl100k_base")
 31:             tokens = encoding.encode(text)
 32:         except ImportError:
 33:             # Fallback: character-based chunking
 34:             return self._chunk_by_chars(text)
 35: 
 36:         chunks = []
 37:         start = 0
 38:         chunk_index = 0
 39: 
 40:         while start < len(tokens):
 41:             end = min(start + self.chunk_size, len(tokens))
 42: 
 43:             # Get the chunk tokens
 44:             chunk_tokens = tokens[start:end]
 45:             chunk_text = encoding.decode(chunk_tokens)
 46: 
 47:             # Calculate character positions
 48:             # This is approximate for token-based chunking
 49:             if chunk_index == 0:
 50:                 start_char = 0
 51:             else:
 52:                 start_char = text.find(chunk_text[:50])
 53:                 if start_char == -1:
 54:                     start_char = 0
 55: 
 56:             end_char = start_char + len(chunk_text)
 57: 
 58:             chunks.append(
 59:                 ChunkResult(
 60:                     content=chunk_text,
 61:                     index=chunk_index,
 62:                     start_char=start_char,
 63:                     end_char=end_char,
 64:                     token_count=len(chunk_tokens),
 65:                 )
 66:             )
 67: 
 68:             # Move start with overlap
 69:             start = end - self.chunk_overlap if end < len(tokens) else end
 70:             chunk_index += 1
 71: 
 72:         return chunks
 73: 
 74:     def _chunk_by_chars(self, text: str) -> list[ChunkResult]:
 75:         """Fallback character-based chunking."""
 76:         # Estimate chars per token (~4)
 77:         chars_per_chunk = self.chunk_size * 4
 78:         overlap_chars = self.chunk_overlap * 4
 79: 
 80:         chunks = []
 81:         start = 0
 82:         chunk_index = 0
 83: 
 84:         while start < len(text):
 85:             end = min(start + chars_per_chunk, len(text))
 86: 
 87:             # Try to break at word boundary
 88:             if end < len(text):
 89:                 space_pos = text.rfind(" ", start + chars_per_chunk // 2, end)
 90:                 if space_pos > start:
 91:                     end = space_pos
 92: 
 93:             chunk_text = text[start:end].strip()
 94:             if chunk_text:
 95:                 chunks.append(
 96:                     ChunkResult(
 97:                         content=chunk_text,
 98:                         index=chunk_index,
 99:                         start_char=start,
100:                         end_char=end,
101:                         token_count=len(chunk_text) // 4,
102:                     )
103:                 )
104:                 chunk_index += 1
105: 
106:             start = end - overlap_chars if end < len(text) else end
107: 
108:         return chunks
````

## File: src/khora/extraction/chunkers/recursive.py
````python
  1: """Recursive character text chunker."""
  2: 
  3: from __future__ import annotations
  4: 
  5: from .base import Chunker, ChunkResult
  6: 
  7: 
  8: class RecursiveChunker(Chunker):
  9:     """Recursive chunker that tries multiple separators.
 10: 
 11:     Attempts to split on increasingly smaller separators until
 12:     chunks are within the target size. Based on LangChain's
 13:     RecursiveCharacterTextSplitter approach.
 14:     """
 15: 
 16:     # Default separators in order of preference
 17:     DEFAULT_SEPARATORS = [
 18:         "\n\n",  # Paragraphs
 19:         "\n",  # Lines
 20:         ". ",  # Sentences
 21:         ", ",  # Clauses
 22:         " ",  # Words
 23:         "",  # Characters (last resort)
 24:     ]
 25: 
 26:     def __init__(
 27:         self,
 28:         *,
 29:         chunk_size: int = 512,
 30:         chunk_overlap: int = 50,
 31:         separators: list[str] | None = None,
 32:     ) -> None:
 33:         """Initialize the recursive chunker.
 34: 
 35:         Args:
 36:             chunk_size: Target chunk size in tokens
 37:             chunk_overlap: Overlap between chunks in tokens
 38:             separators: Custom list of separators to try
 39:         """
 40:         super().__init__(chunk_size=chunk_size, chunk_overlap=chunk_overlap)
 41:         self.separators = separators or self.DEFAULT_SEPARATORS
 42: 
 43:     def chunk(self, text: str) -> list[ChunkResult]:
 44:         """Split text recursively using separators.
 45: 
 46:         Args:
 47:             text: Text to chunk
 48: 
 49:         Returns:
 50:             List of ChunkResult objects
 51:         """
 52:         if not text.strip():
 53:             return []
 54: 
 55:         # Split recursively
 56:         splits = self._split_text(text, self.separators)
 57: 
 58:         # Merge small splits and create final chunks
 59:         chunks = self._merge_splits(splits, text)
 60: 
 61:         return chunks
 62: 
 63:     def _split_text(self, text: str, separators: list[str]) -> list[str]:
 64:         """Recursively split text using the separator list."""
 65:         if not separators:
 66:             return [text]
 67: 
 68:         separator = separators[0]
 69:         remaining_separators = separators[1:]
 70: 
 71:         # Split on current separator
 72:         if separator:
 73:             splits = text.split(separator)
 74:             # Re-add the separator to maintain text
 75:             splits = [s + separator if i < len(splits) - 1 else s for i, s in enumerate(splits)]
 76:         else:
 77:             # Character-level split (last resort)
 78:             return list(text)
 79: 
 80:         final_splits = []
 81:         for split in splits:
 82:             if not split.strip():
 83:                 continue
 84: 
 85:             split_tokens = self.count_tokens(split)
 86: 
 87:             if split_tokens <= self.chunk_size:
 88:                 final_splits.append(split)
 89:             elif remaining_separators:
 90:                 # Recursively split further
 91:                 final_splits.extend(self._split_text(split, remaining_separators))
 92:             else:
 93:                 # Can't split further, keep as is
 94:                 final_splits.append(split)
 95: 
 96:         return final_splits
 97: 
 98:     def _merge_splits(self, splits: list[str], original_text: str) -> list[ChunkResult]:
 99:         """Merge small splits into chunks of target size."""
100:         chunks = []
101:         current_chunk = ""
102:         current_tokens = 0
103:         chunk_index = 0
104: 
105:         for split in splits:
106:             split_tokens = self.count_tokens(split)
107: 
108:             # If adding this split keeps us under the limit
109:             if current_tokens + split_tokens <= self.chunk_size:
110:                 current_chunk += split
111:                 current_tokens += split_tokens
112:             else:
113:                 # Save current chunk if not empty
114:                 if current_chunk.strip():
115:                     chunks.append(self._create_chunk_result(current_chunk.strip(), chunk_index, original_text))
116:                     chunk_index += 1
117: 
118:                 # Handle overlap
119:                 if self.chunk_overlap > 0 and current_chunk:
120:                     overlap_text = self._get_overlap_text(current_chunk)
121:                     current_chunk = overlap_text + split
122:                     current_tokens = self.count_tokens(current_chunk)
123:                 else:
124:                     current_chunk = split
125:                     current_tokens = split_tokens
126: 
127:         # Add final chunk
128:         if current_chunk.strip():
129:             chunks.append(self._create_chunk_result(current_chunk.strip(), chunk_index, original_text))
130: 
131:         return chunks
132: 
133:     def _get_overlap_text(self, text: str) -> str:
134:         """Get the overlap portion from the end of text."""
135:         try:
136:             import tiktoken
137: 
138:             encoding = tiktoken.get_encoding("cl100k_base")
139:             tokens = encoding.encode(text)
140: 
141:             if len(tokens) <= self.chunk_overlap:
142:                 return text
143: 
144:             overlap_tokens = tokens[-self.chunk_overlap :]
145:             return encoding.decode(overlap_tokens)
146:         except ImportError:
147:             # Character-based fallback
148:             overlap_chars = self.chunk_overlap * 4
149:             return text[-overlap_chars:] if len(text) > overlap_chars else text
150: 
151:     def _create_chunk_result(self, content: str, index: int, original_text: str) -> ChunkResult:
152:         """Create a ChunkResult with character positions."""
153:         # Find position in original text
154:         start_char = original_text.find(content)
155:         if start_char == -1:
156:             # Try with first 50 chars for partial match
157:             start_char = original_text.find(content[:50]) if len(content) > 50 else 0
158: 
159:         end_char = start_char + len(content) if start_char >= 0 else len(content)
160: 
161:         return ChunkResult(
162:             content=content,
163:             index=index,
164:             start_char=max(0, start_char),
165:             end_char=end_char,
166:             token_count=self.count_tokens(content),
167:         )
````

## File: src/khora/extraction/chunkers/semantic.py
````python
  1: """Semantic text chunker that preserves meaning."""
  2: 
  3: from __future__ import annotations
  4: 
  5: import re
  6: 
  7: from .base import Chunker, ChunkResult
  8: 
  9: 
 10: class SemanticChunker(Chunker):
 11:     """Semantic chunker that respects document structure.
 12: 
 13:     Attempts to split text at natural boundaries (paragraphs, sentences)
 14:     while staying within token limits. Preserves semantic coherence.
 15:     """
 16: 
 17:     def __init__(
 18:         self,
 19:         *,
 20:         chunk_size: int = 512,
 21:         chunk_overlap: int = 50,
 22:         respect_sentences: bool = True,
 23:         respect_paragraphs: bool = True,
 24:     ) -> None:
 25:         """Initialize the semantic chunker.
 26: 
 27:         Args:
 28:             chunk_size: Target chunk size in tokens
 29:             chunk_overlap: Overlap between chunks in tokens
 30:             respect_sentences: Try to break at sentence boundaries
 31:             respect_paragraphs: Try to break at paragraph boundaries
 32:         """
 33:         super().__init__(chunk_size=chunk_size, chunk_overlap=chunk_overlap)
 34:         self.respect_sentences = respect_sentences
 35:         self.respect_paragraphs = respect_paragraphs
 36: 
 37:     def chunk(self, text: str) -> list[ChunkResult]:
 38:         """Split text into semantic chunks.
 39: 
 40:         Args:
 41:             text: Text to chunk
 42: 
 43:         Returns:
 44:             List of ChunkResult objects
 45:         """
 46:         if not text.strip():
 47:             return []
 48: 
 49:         # First split into paragraphs
 50:         if self.respect_paragraphs:
 51:             paragraphs = self._split_paragraphs(text)
 52:         else:
 53:             paragraphs = [text]
 54: 
 55:         # Build chunks from paragraphs
 56:         chunks = []
 57:         current_chunk = ""
 58:         current_tokens = 0
 59:         chunk_index = 0
 60:         current_start = 0
 61: 
 62:         for para in paragraphs:
 63:             para_tokens = self.count_tokens(para)
 64: 
 65:             # If paragraph fits in current chunk
 66:             if current_tokens + para_tokens <= self.chunk_size:
 67:                 if current_chunk:
 68:                     current_chunk += "\n\n" + para
 69:                 else:
 70:                     current_chunk = para
 71:                 current_tokens += para_tokens
 72:             else:
 73:                 # Save current chunk if not empty
 74:                 if current_chunk:
 75:                     chunks.append(self._create_chunk_result(current_chunk, chunk_index, current_start, text))
 76:                     chunk_index += 1
 77: 
 78:                 # Handle large paragraphs
 79:                 if para_tokens > self.chunk_size:
 80:                     # Split large paragraph into sentences
 81:                     sub_chunks = self._split_large_paragraph(para)
 82:                     for sub_chunk in sub_chunks:
 83:                         chunks.append(self._create_chunk_result(sub_chunk, chunk_index, current_start, text))
 84:                         chunk_index += 1
 85:                     current_chunk = ""
 86:                     current_tokens = 0
 87:                 else:
 88:                     current_chunk = para
 89:                     current_tokens = para_tokens
 90: 
 91:                 current_start = text.find(current_chunk) if current_chunk else current_start
 92: 
 93:         # Don't forget the last chunk
 94:         if current_chunk:
 95:             chunks.append(self._create_chunk_result(current_chunk, chunk_index, current_start, text))
 96: 
 97:         return chunks
 98: 
 99:     def _split_paragraphs(self, text: str) -> list[str]:
100:         """Split text into paragraphs."""
101:         # Split on double newlines or multiple newlines
102:         paragraphs = re.split(r"\n\s*\n", text)
103:         return [p.strip() for p in paragraphs if p.strip()]
104: 
105:     def _split_large_paragraph(self, para: str) -> list[str]:
106:         """Split a large paragraph that exceeds chunk size."""
107:         if not self.respect_sentences:
108:             # Fall back to fixed chunking
109:             return self._fixed_split(para)
110: 
111:         # Split into sentences
112:         sentences = self._split_sentences(para)
113: 
114:         chunks = []
115:         current_chunk = ""
116:         current_tokens = 0
117: 
118:         for sentence in sentences:
119:             sentence_tokens = self.count_tokens(sentence)
120: 
121:             if current_tokens + sentence_tokens <= self.chunk_size:
122:                 current_chunk = (current_chunk + " " + sentence).strip()
123:                 current_tokens += sentence_tokens
124:             else:
125:                 if current_chunk:
126:                     chunks.append(current_chunk)
127: 
128:                 # Handle sentences larger than chunk_size
129:                 if sentence_tokens > self.chunk_size:
130:                     chunks.extend(self._fixed_split(sentence))
131:                     current_chunk = ""
132:                     current_tokens = 0
133:                 else:
134:                     current_chunk = sentence
135:                     current_tokens = sentence_tokens
136: 
137:         if current_chunk:
138:             chunks.append(current_chunk)
139: 
140:         return chunks
141: 
142:     def _split_sentences(self, text: str) -> list[str]:
143:         """Split text into sentences."""
144:         # Simple sentence splitting - handles common cases
145:         # Could be improved with nltk or spacy for better accuracy
146:         sentence_endings = r"(?<=[.!?])\s+"
147:         sentences = re.split(sentence_endings, text)
148:         return [s.strip() for s in sentences if s.strip()]
149: 
150:     def _fixed_split(self, text: str) -> list[str]:
151:         """Fixed-size split for text that can't be split semantically."""
152:         try:
153:             import tiktoken
154: 
155:             encoding = tiktoken.get_encoding("cl100k_base")
156:             tokens = encoding.encode(text)
157:         except ImportError:
158:             # Character-based fallback
159:             chars_per_chunk = self.chunk_size * 4
160:             return [
161:                 text[i : i + chars_per_chunk] for i in range(0, len(text), chars_per_chunk - self.chunk_overlap * 4)
162:             ]
163: 
164:         chunks = []
165:         start = 0
166:         while start < len(tokens):
167:             end = min(start + self.chunk_size, len(tokens))
168:             chunk_tokens = tokens[start:end]
169:             chunks.append(encoding.decode(chunk_tokens))
170:             start = end - self.chunk_overlap if end < len(tokens) else end
171: 
172:         return chunks
173: 
174:     def _create_chunk_result(self, content: str, index: int, hint_start: int, full_text: str) -> ChunkResult:
175:         """Create a ChunkResult with proper character positions."""
176:         # Find actual position in text
177:         start_char = full_text.find(content, max(0, hint_start - 100))
178:         if start_char == -1:
179:             start_char = hint_start
180: 
181:         end_char = start_char + len(content)
182: 
183:         return ChunkResult(
184:             content=content,
185:             index=index,
186:             start_char=start_char,
187:             end_char=end_char,
188:             token_count=self.count_tokens(content),
189:         )
````

````python
 3: from __future__ import annotations
 4: 
 5: from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
 6: 
 7: 
 8: class Embedder(ABC):
 9:     """Abstract base class for text embedders."""
10: 
11:     @property
12:     @abstractmethod
13:     def model_name(self) -> str:
14:         """Get the model name."""
15:         ...
16: 
17:     @property
18:     @abstractmethod
19:     def dimension(self) -> int:
20:         """Get the embedding dimension."""
21:         ...
22: 
23:     @abstractmethod
24:     async def embed(self, text: str) -> list[float]:
25:         """Generate embedding for a single text.
26: 
27:         Args:
28:             text: Text to embed
29: 
30:         Returns:
31:             Embedding vector
32:         """
33:         ...
34: 
35:     @abstractmethod
36:     async def embed_batch(self, texts: list[str]) -> list[list[float]]:
37:         """Generate embeddings for multiple texts.
38: 
39:         Args:
40:             texts: List of texts to embed
41: 
42:         Returns:
43:             List of embedding vectors
44:         """
45:         ...
````

## File: src/khora/extraction/embedders/litellm.py
````python
  1: """LiteLLM-based embedder for unified embedding generation."""
  2: 
  3: from __future__ import annotations
  4: 
  5: import asyncio
  6: from typing import TYPE_CHECKING
  7: 
  8: from loguru import logger
  9: 
 10: from .base import Embedder
 11: 
 12: if TYPE_CHECKING:
 13:     from khora.config import LiteLLMConfig
 14: 
 15: 
 16: class LiteLLMEmbedder(Embedder):
 17:     """LiteLLM-based embedder for text embeddings.
 18: 
 19:     Uses LiteLLM to generate embeddings from various providers
 20:     (OpenAI, Cohere, etc.) through a unified interface.
 21:     """
 22: 
 23:     def __init__(
 24:         self,
 25:         model: str = "text-embedding-3-small",
 26:         dimension: int = 1536,
 27:         *,
 28:         timeout: int = 30,
 29:         max_retries: int = 3,
 30:         batch_size: int = 100,
 31:     ) -> None:
 32:         """Initialize the LiteLLM embedder.
 33: 
 34:         Args:
 35:             model: Embedding model name
 36:             dimension: Embedding vector dimension
 37:             timeout: Request timeout in seconds
 38:             max_retries: Maximum retries on failure
 39:             batch_size: Maximum batch size for embed_batch
 40:         """
 41:         self._model = model
 42:         self._dimension = dimension
 43:         self._timeout = timeout
 44:         self._max_retries = max_retries
 45:         self._batch_size = batch_size
 46: 
 47:     @classmethod
 48:     def from_config(cls, config: LiteLLMConfig) -> LiteLLMEmbedder:
 49:         """Create embedder from LiteLLM configuration.
 50: 
 51:         Args:
 52:             config: LiteLLMConfig instance
 53: 
 54:         Returns:
 55:             Configured LiteLLMEmbedder
 56:         """
 57:         return cls(
 58:             model=config.embedding_model,
 59:             dimension=config.embedding_dimension,
 60:             timeout=config.timeout,
 61:             max_retries=config.max_retries,
 62:         )
 63: 
 64:     @property
 65:     def model_name(self) -> str:
 66:         """Get the model name."""
 67:         return self._model
 68: 
 69:     @property
 70:     def dimension(self) -> int:
 71:         """Get the embedding dimension."""
 72:         return self._dimension
 73: 
 74:     async def embed(self, text: str) -> list[float]:
 75:         """Generate embedding for a single text.
 76: 
 77:         Args:
 78:             text: Text to embed
 79: 
 80:         Returns:
 81:             Embedding vector
 82:         """
 83:         embeddings = await self.embed_batch([text])
 84:         return embeddings[0]
 85: 
 86:     async def embed_batch(self, texts: list[str]) -> list[list[float]]:
 87:         """Generate embeddings for multiple texts.
 88: 
 89:         Args:
 90:             texts: List of texts to embed
 91: 
 92:         Returns:
 93:             List of embedding vectors
 94:         """
 95:         if not texts:
 96:             return []
 97: 
 98:         try:
 99:             import litellm  # noqa: F401
100:         except ImportError:
101:             raise RuntimeError("litellm package not installed. Run: pip install litellm")
102: 
103:         # Process in batches if needed
104:         if len(texts) > self._batch_size:
105:             all_embeddings = []
106:             for i in range(0, len(texts), self._batch_size):
107:                 batch = texts[i : i + self._batch_size]
108:                 batch_embeddings = await self._embed_batch_internal(batch)
109:                 all_embeddings.extend(batch_embeddings)
110:             return all_embeddings
111: 
112:         return await self._embed_batch_internal(texts)
113: 
114:     async def _embed_batch_internal(self, texts: list[str]) -> list[list[float]]:
115:         """Internal batch embedding without chunking."""
116:         import litellm
117: 
118:         for attempt in range(self._max_retries):
119:             try:
120:                 response = await litellm.aembedding(
121:                     model=self._model,
122:                     input=texts,
123:                     timeout=self._timeout,
124:                 )
125:                 return [item["embedding"] for item in response.data]
126:             except Exception as e:
127:                 if attempt < self._max_retries - 1:
128:                     wait_time = 2**attempt
129:                     logger.warning(f"Embedding attempt {attempt + 1} failed: {e}. Retrying in {wait_time}s...")
130:                     await asyncio.sleep(wait_time)
131:                 else:
132:                     logger.error(f"Embedding failed after {self._max_retries} attempts: {e}")
133:                     raise
````

## File: src/khora/extraction/extractors/base.py
````python
 1: """Base extractor protocol and types."""
 2: 
 3: from __future__ import annotations
 4: 
 5: from abc import ABC, abstractmethod
 6: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
 7: from typing import Any
 8: 
 9: 
10: @dataclass
11: class ExtractedEntity:
12:     """An entity extracted from text."""
13: 
14:     name: str
15:     entity_type: str
16:     description: str = ""
17:     attributes: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
18:     confidence: float = 1.0
19: 
20:     # Source tracking
21:     source_text: str = ""
22:     start_char: int = 0
23:     end_char: int = 0
24: 
25: 
26: @dataclass
27: class ExtractedRelationship:
28:     """A relationship extracted from text."""
29: 
30:     source_entity: str
31:     target_entity: str
32:     relationship_type: str
33:     description: str = ""
34:     properties: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
35:     confidence: float = 1.0
36: 
37: 
38: @dataclass
39: class ExtractionResult:
40:     """Result of entity extraction from text."""
41: 
42:     entities: list[ExtractedEntity] = field(default_factory=list)
43:     relationships: list[ExtractedRelationship] = field(default_factory=list)
44:     metadata: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
45: 
46: 
47: class EntityExtractor(ABC):
48:     """Abstract base class for entity extractors."""
49: 
50:     @abstractmethod
51:     async def extract(
52:         self,
53:         text: str,
54:         *,
55:         entity_types: list[str] | None = None,
56:     ) -> ExtractionResult:
57:         """Extract entities and relationships from text.
58: 
59:         Args:
60:             text: Text to extract from
61:             entity_types: Optional list of entity types to extract
62: 
63:         Returns:
64:             ExtractionResult containing entities and relationships
65:         """
66:         ...
67: 
68:     @abstractmethod
69:     async def extract_batch(
70:         self,
71:         texts: list[str],
72:         *,
73:         entity_types: list[str] | None = None,
74:     ) -> list[ExtractionResult]:
75:         """Extract from multiple texts.
76: 
77:         Args:
78:             texts: List of texts to extract from
79:             entity_types: Optional list of entity types to extract
80: 
81:         Returns:
82:             List of ExtractionResult objects
83:         """
84:         ...
````

## File: src/khora/extraction/extractors/llm.py
````python
  1: """LLM-based entity extraction using LiteLLM."""
  2: 
  3: from __future__ import annotations
  4: 
  5: import asyncio
  6: import json
  7: from typing import TYPE_CHECKING
  8: 
  9: from loguru import logger
 10: 
 11: from .base import EntityExtractor, ExtractedEntity, ExtractedRelationship, ExtractionResult
 12: 
 13: if TYPE_CHECKING:
 14:     from khora.config import LiteLLMConfig
 15: 
 16: 
 17: # Default entity types to extract
 18: DEFAULT_ENTITY_TYPES = ["PERSON", "ORGANIZATION", "LOCATION", "CONCEPT", "EVENT", "TECHNOLOGY"]
 19: 
 20: # Extraction prompt template
 21: EXTRACTION_PROMPT = """Extract entities and relationships from the following text.
 22: 
 23: Entity types to extract: {entity_types}
 24: 
 25: Text:
 26: {text}
 27: 
 28: Return a JSON object with the following structure:
 29: {{
 30:     "entities": [
 31:         {{
 32:             "name": "entity name",
 33:             "entity_type": "PERSON|ORGANIZATION|LOCATION|CONCEPT|EVENT|TECHNOLOGY|etc",
 34:             "description": "brief description",
 35:             "attributes": {{"key": "value"}}
 36:         }}
 37:     ],
 38:     "relationships": [
 39:         {{
 40:             "source_entity": "source entity name",
 41:             "target_entity": "target entity name",
 42:             "relationship_type": "WORKS_FOR|KNOWS|LOCATED_IN|RELATES_TO|etc",
 43:             "description": "brief description"
 44:         }}
 45:     ]
 46: }}
 47: 
 48: Extract all relevant entities and relationships. Be thorough but only include entities that are clearly mentioned.
 49: Return ONLY valid JSON, no other text."""
 50: 
 51: 
 52: class LLMEntityExtractor(EntityExtractor):
 53:     """LLM-based entity extractor using LiteLLM.
 54: 
 55:     Uses an LLM to extract entities and relationships from text
 56:     through structured JSON output.
 57:     """
 58: 
 59:     def __init__(
 60:         self,
 61:         model: str = "gpt-4o-mini",
 62:         *,
 63:         temperature: float = 0.3,  # Lower for more consistent extraction
 64:         max_tokens: int = 4000,
 65:         timeout: int = 60,
 66:         max_retries: int = 3,
 67:         max_concurrent: int = 5,
 68:     ) -> None:
 69:         """Initialize the LLM entity extractor.
 70: 
 71:         Args:
 72:             model: LLM model to use
 73:             temperature: Sampling temperature
 74:             max_tokens: Maximum tokens in response
 75:             timeout: Request timeout in seconds
 76:             max_retries: Maximum retries on failure
 77:             max_concurrent: Maximum concurrent extractions
 78:         """
 79:         self._model = model
 80:         self._temperature = temperature
 81:         self._max_tokens = max_tokens
 82:         self._timeout = timeout
 83:         self._max_retries = max_retries
 84:         self._semaphore = asyncio.Semaphore(max_concurrent)
 85: 
 86:     @classmethod
 87:     def from_config(cls, config: LiteLLMConfig) -> LLMEntityExtractor:
 88:         """Create extractor from LiteLLM configuration.
 89: 
 90:         Args:
 91:             config: LiteLLMConfig instance
 92: 
 93:         Returns:
 94:             Configured LLMEntityExtractor
 95:         """
 96:         return cls(
 97:             model=config.model,
 98:             temperature=0.3,  # Override for extraction
 99:             max_tokens=config.max_tokens,
100:             timeout=config.timeout,
101:             max_retries=config.max_retries,
102:             max_concurrent=config.max_concurrent_llm_calls,
103:         )
104: 
105:     async def extract(
106:         self,
107:         text: str,
108:         *,
109:         entity_types: list[str] | None = None,
110:     ) -> ExtractionResult:
111:         """Extract entities and relationships from text.
112: 
113:         Args:
114:             text: Text to extract from
115:             entity_types: Optional list of entity types to extract
116: 
117:         Returns:
118:             ExtractionResult containing entities and relationships
119:         """
120:         if not text.strip():
121:             return ExtractionResult()
122: 
123:         entity_types = entity_types or DEFAULT_ENTITY_TYPES
124: 
125:         try:
126:             import litellm
127:         except ImportError:
128:             raise RuntimeError("litellm package not installed. Run: pip install litellm")
129: 
130:         prompt = EXTRACTION_PROMPT.format(
131:             entity_types=", ".join(entity_types),
132:             text=text[:8000],  # Truncate very long texts
133:         )
134: 
135:         async with self._semaphore:
136:             for attempt in range(self._max_retries):
137:                 try:
138:                     response = await litellm.acompletion(
139:                         model=self._model,
140:                         messages=[
141:                             {
142:                                 "role": "system",
143:                                 "content": "You are an expert entity extraction system. Extract entities and relationships from text and return them as structured JSON.",
144:                             },
145:                             {"role": "user", "content": prompt},
146:                         ],
147:                         temperature=self._temperature,
148:                         max_tokens=self._max_tokens,
149:                         timeout=self._timeout,
150:                         response_format={"type": "json_object"},
151:                     )
152: 
153:                     content = response.choices[0].message.content
154:                     return self._parse_response(content)
155: 
156:                 except Exception as e:
157:                     if attempt < self._max_retries - 1:
158:                         wait_time = 2**attempt
159:                         logger.warning(f"Extraction attempt {attempt + 1} failed: {e}. Retrying in {wait_time}s...")
160:                         await asyncio.sleep(wait_time)
161:                     else:
162:                         logger.error(f"Extraction failed after {self._max_retries} attempts: {e}")
163:                         return ExtractionResult(metadata={"error": str(e)})
164: 
165:     async def extract_batch(
166:         self,
167:         texts: list[str],
168:         *,
169:         entity_types: list[str] | None = None,
170:     ) -> list[ExtractionResult]:
171:         """Extract from multiple texts concurrently.
172: 
173:         Args:
174:             texts: List of texts to extract from
175:             entity_types: Optional list of entity types to extract
176: 
177:         Returns:
178:             List of ExtractionResult objects
179:         """
180:         if not texts:
181:             return []
182: 
183:         tasks = [self.extract(text, entity_types=entity_types) for text in texts]
184:         return await asyncio.gather(*tasks)
185: 
186:     def _parse_response(self, content: str) -> ExtractionResult:
187:         """Parse the LLM response into an ExtractionResult."""
188:         try:
189:             # Try to parse as JSON
190:             data = json.loads(content)
191: 
192:             entities = []
193:             for e in data.get("entities", []):
194:                 entities.append(
195:                     ExtractedEntity(
196:                         name=e.get("name", ""),
197:                         entity_type=e.get("entity_type", "CONCEPT"),
198:                         description=e.get("description", ""),
199:                         attributes=e.get("attributes", {}),
200:                         confidence=e.get("confidence", 0.9),
201:                     )
202:                 )
203: 
204:             relationships = []
205:             for r in data.get("relationships", []):
206:                 relationships.append(
207:                     ExtractedRelationship(
208:                         source_entity=r.get("source_entity", ""),
209:                         target_entity=r.get("target_entity", ""),
210:                         relationship_type=r.get("relationship_type", "RELATES_TO"),
211:                         description=r.get("description", ""),
212:                         properties=r.get("properties", {}),
213:                         confidence=r.get("confidence", 0.9),
214:                     )
215:                 )
216: 
217:             return ExtractionResult(entities=entities, relationships=relationships)
218: 
219:         except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
220:             logger.warning(f"Failed to parse extraction response as JSON: {e}")
221:             # Try to extract JSON from the response
222:             return self._extract_json_from_text(content)
223: 
224:     def _extract_json_from_text(self, text: str) -> ExtractionResult:
225:         """Try to extract JSON from text that may contain other content."""
226:         import re
227: 
228:         # Look for JSON object in the text
229:         json_match = re.search(r"\{[\s\S]*\}", text)
230:         if json_match:
231:             try:
232:                 data = json.loads(json_match.group())
233:                 return self._parse_response(json.dumps(data))
234:             except json.JSONDecodeError:
235:                 pass
236: 
237:         logger.warning("Could not extract valid JSON from response")
238:         return ExtractionResult(metadata={"raw_response": text[:500]})
````

## File: src/khora/extraction/skills/base.py
````python
  1: """Base extraction skill definition."""
  2: 
  3: from __future__ import annotations
  4: 
  5: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
  6: from typing import Any
  7: 
  8: 
  9: @dataclass
 10: class ExtractionSkill:
 11:     """Configurable extraction skill definition.
 12: 
 13:     Skills define what types of entities and relationships to extract
 14:     from documents. They can be customized per namespace or document type.
 15:     """
 16: 
 17:     name: str
 18:     description: str = ""
 19: 
 20:     # Entity extraction configuration
 21:     entity_types: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
 22:     relationship_types: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
 23: 
 24:     # Custom extraction prompt (optional)
 25:     custom_prompt: str | None = None
 26: 
 27:     # Processing configuration
 28:     extract_entities: bool = True
 29:     extract_relationships: bool = True
 30: 
 31:     # Confidence thresholds
 32:     min_entity_confidence: float = 0.5
 33:     min_relationship_confidence: float = 0.5
 34: 
 35:     # Additional metadata
 36:     metadata: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
 37: 
 38:     @classmethod
 39:     def general_entities(cls) -> ExtractionSkill:
 40:         """Create a general entity extraction skill."""
 41:         return cls(
 42:             name="general_entities",
 43:             description="Extract general entities like people, organizations, and concepts",
 44:             entity_types=["PERSON", "ORGANIZATION", "CONCEPT", "LOCATION"],
 45:             relationship_types=["WORKS_FOR", "KNOWS", "RELATES_TO", "LOCATED_IN"],
 46:         )
 47: 
 48:     @classmethod
 49:     def technical_docs(cls) -> ExtractionSkill:
 50:         """Create a skill for technical documentation."""
 51:         return cls(
 52:             name="technical_docs",
 53:             description="Extract technical entities from documentation",
 54:             entity_types=["TECHNOLOGY", "CONCEPT", "PRODUCT", "ORGANIZATION"],
 55:             relationship_types=["DEPENDS_ON", "IMPLEMENTS", "PART_OF", "RELATES_TO"],
 56:         )
 57: 
 58:     @classmethod
 59:     def business_intel(cls) -> ExtractionSkill:
 60:         """Create a skill for business intelligence."""
 61:         return cls(
 62:             name="business_intel",
 63:             description="Extract business entities and relationships",
 64:             entity_types=["PERSON", "ORGANIZATION", "PRODUCT", "EVENT", "LOCATION"],
 65:             relationship_types=[
 66:                 "WORKS_FOR",
 67:                 "MANAGES",
 68:                 "OWNS",
 69:                 "COMPETES_WITH",
 70:                 "PARTNERS_WITH",
 71:                 "HEADQUARTERED_IN",
 72:             ],
 73:         )
 74: 
 75:     @classmethod
 76:     def research_papers(cls) -> ExtractionSkill:
 77:         """Create a skill for research papers."""
 78:         return cls(
 79:             name="research_papers",
 80:             description="Extract entities from academic research",
 81:             entity_types=["PERSON", "ORGANIZATION", "CONCEPT", "TECHNOLOGY", "EVENT"],
 82:             relationship_types=[
 83:                 "COLLABORATES_WITH",
 84:                 "DERIVED_FROM",
 85:                 "IMPLEMENTS",
 86:                 "RELATES_TO",
 87:                 "PRECEDES",
 88:             ],
 89:         )
 90: 
 91:     def to_dict(self) -> dict[str, Any]:
 92:         """Convert skill to dictionary."""
 93:         return {
 94:             "name": self.name,
 95:             "description": self.description,
 96:             "entity_types": self.entity_types,
 97:             "relationship_types": self.relationship_types,
 98:             "custom_prompt": self.custom_prompt,
 99:             "extract_entities": self.extract_entities,
100:             "extract_relationships": self.extract_relationships,
101:             "min_entity_confidence": self.min_entity_confidence,
102:             "min_relationship_confidence": self.min_relationship_confidence,
103:             "metadata": self.metadata,
104:         }
105: 
106:     @classmethod
107:     def from_dict(cls, data: dict[str, Any]) -> ExtractionSkill:
108:         """Create skill from dictionary."""
109:         return cls(
110:             name=data.get("name", "custom"),
111:             description=data.get("description", ""),
112:             entity_types=data.get("entity_types", []),
113:             relationship_types=data.get("relationship_types", []),
114:             custom_prompt=data.get("custom_prompt"),
115:             extract_entities=data.get("extract_entities", True),
116:             extract_relationships=data.get("extract_relationships", True),
117:             min_entity_confidence=data.get("min_entity_confidence", 0.5),
118:             min_relationship_confidence=data.get("min_relationship_confidence", 0.5),
119:             metadata=data.get("metadata", {}),
120:         )
````

## File: src/khora/extraction/skills/registry.py
````python
  1: """Skill registry for managing extraction skills."""
  2: 
  3: from __future__ import annotations
  4: 
  5: from typing import Any
  6: 
  7: from loguru import logger
  8: 
  9: from .base import ExtractionSkill
 10: 
 11: 
 12: class SkillRegistry:
 13:     """Registry for managing extraction skills.
 14: 
 15:     Provides a centralized way to register, retrieve, and manage
 16:     extraction skills that can be applied to different document types
 17:     or namespaces.
 18:     """
 19: 
 20:     def __init__(self) -> None:
 21:         """Initialize the skill registry."""
 22:         self._skills: dict[str, ExtractionSkill] = {}
 23:         self._register_builtins()
 24: 
 25:     def _register_builtins(self) -> None:
 26:         """Register built-in extraction skills."""
 27:         self.register(ExtractionSkill.general_entities())
 28:         self.register(ExtractionSkill.technical_docs())
 29:         self.register(ExtractionSkill.business_intel())
 30:         self.register(ExtractionSkill.research_papers())
 31: 
 32:     def register(self, skill: ExtractionSkill) -> None:
 33:         """Register an extraction skill.
 34: 
 35:         Args:
 36:             skill: ExtractionSkill to register
 37:         """
 38:         self._skills[skill.name] = skill
 39:         logger.debug(f"Registered extraction skill: {skill.name}")
 40: 
 41:     def get(self, name: str) -> ExtractionSkill | None:
 42:         """Get a skill by name.
 43: 
 44:         Args:
 45:             name: Skill name
 46: 
 47:         Returns:
 48:             ExtractionSkill or None if not found
 49:         """
 50:         return self._skills.get(name)
 51: 
 52:     def get_or_default(self, name: str) -> ExtractionSkill:
 53:         """Get a skill by name, falling back to general_entities.
 54: 
 55:         Args:
 56:             name: Skill name
 57: 
 58:         Returns:
 59:             ExtractionSkill (general_entities if not found)
 60:         """
 61:         return self._skills.get(name) or self._skills["general_entities"]
 62: 
 63:     def list_skills(self) -> list[str]:
 64:         """List all registered skill names.
 65: 
 66:         Returns:
 67:             List of skill names
 68:         """
 69:         return list(self._skills.keys())
 70: 
 71:     def all_skills(self) -> list[ExtractionSkill]:
 72:         """Get all registered skills.
 73: 
 74:         Returns:
 75:             List of ExtractionSkill objects
 76:         """
 77:         return list(self._skills.values())
 78: 
 79:     def unregister(self, name: str) -> bool:
 80:         """Unregister a skill.
 81: 
 82:         Args:
 83:             name: Skill name to unregister
 84: 
 85:         Returns:
 86:             True if skill was removed, False if not found
 87:         """
 88:         if name in self._skills:
 89:             del self._skills[name]
 90:             logger.debug(f"Unregistered extraction skill: {name}")
 91:             return True
 92:         return False
 93: 
 94:     def register_from_config(self, config: list[dict[str, Any]]) -> None:
 95:         """Register skills from configuration.
 96: 
 97:         Args:
 98:             config: List of skill configuration dictionaries
 99:         """
100:         for skill_config in config:
101:             skill = ExtractionSkill.from_dict(skill_config)
102:             self.register(skill)
103: 
104:     def to_dict(self) -> dict[str, dict[str, Any]]:
105:         """Export all skills as a dictionary.
106: 
107:         Returns:
108:             Dictionary of skill name to skill config
109:         """
110:         return {name: skill.to_dict() for name, skill in self._skills.items()}
111: 
112: 
113: # Global skill registry instance
114: _default_registry: SkillRegistry | None = None
115: 
116: 
117: def get_default_registry() -> SkillRegistry:
118:     """Get the default global skill registry.
119: 
120:     Returns:
121:         Default SkillRegistry instance
122:     """
123:     global _default_registry
124:     if _default_registry is None:
125:         _default_registry = SkillRegistry()
126:     return _default_registry
````

## File: src/khora/pipelines/flows/sync.py
````python
  1: """Source synchronization flows for Khora Memory Lake.
  2: 
  3: Provides incremental sync from external sources with checkpoint tracking.
  4: """
  5: 
  6: from __future__ import annotations
  7: 
  8: from typing import TYPE_CHECKING, Any
  9: from uuid import UUID
 10: 
 11: from loguru import logger
 12: from prefect import flow, task
 13: 
 14: from ..registry import pipeline
 15: 
 16: if TYPE_CHECKING:
 17:     from khora.storage import StorageCoordinator
 18: 
 19: 
 20: @task(name="get_sync_checkpoint")
 21: async def get_sync_checkpoint(
 22:     namespace_id: UUID,
 23:     source: str,
 24:     storage: StorageCoordinator,
 25: ) -> str | None:
 26:     """Get the last sync checkpoint for a source."""
 27:     return await storage.get_sync_checkpoint(namespace_id, source)
 28: 
 29: 
 30: @task(name="set_sync_checkpoint")
 31: async def set_sync_checkpoint(
 32:     namespace_id: UUID,
 33:     source: str,
 34:     checkpoint: str,
 35:     storage: StorageCoordinator,
 36: ) -> None:
 37:     """Set the sync checkpoint for a source."""
 38:     await storage.set_sync_checkpoint(namespace_id, source, checkpoint)
 39: 
 40: 
 41: @task(name="fetch_from_source")
 42: async def fetch_from_source(
 43:     source: str,
 44:     connector_config: dict[str, Any],
 45:     checkpoint: str | None,
 46: ) -> tuple[list[dict[str, Any]], str | None]:
 47:     """Fetch documents from an external source.
 48: 
 49:     This is a placeholder that should be replaced with actual connector
 50:     implementations for different sources (GitHub, Notion, etc.)
 51: 
 52:     Returns:
 53:         Tuple of (documents, new_checkpoint)
 54:     """
 55:     # This would be implemented by specific connectors
 56:     # For now, return empty results
 57:     logger.warning(f"No connector implemented for source: {source}")
 58:     return [], checkpoint
 59: 
 60: 
 61: @pipeline("sync_source", description="Sync from external source", tags=["sync"])
 62: @flow(name="sync_source", log_prints=True)
 63: async def sync_source(
 64:     namespace_id: UUID,
 65:     source: str,
 66:     storage: StorageCoordinator | None = None,
 67:     *,
 68:     connector_config: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 69:     skill_name: str = "general_entities",
 70:     **kwargs,
 71: ) -> dict[str, Any]:
 72:     """Sync documents from an external source.
 73: 
 74:     Performs incremental sync using checkpoints to track progress.
 75: 
 76:     Args:
 77:         namespace_id: Target namespace
 78:         source: Source name (e.g., "github", "notion")
 79:         storage: StorageCoordinator instance
 80:         connector_config: Configuration for the source connector
 81:         skill_name: Extraction skill to use
 82: 
 83:     Returns:
 84:         Summary of sync results
 85:     """
 86:     from .ingest import ingest_documents
 87: 
 88:     if storage is None:
 89:         raise ValueError("storage is required")
 90: 
 91:     connector_config = connector_config or {}
 92: 
 93:     logger.info(f"Starting sync from {source} into namespace {namespace_id}")
 94: 
 95:     # Get last checkpoint
 96:     checkpoint = await get_sync_checkpoint(namespace_id, source, storage)
 97:     if checkpoint:
 98:         logger.info(f"Resuming from checkpoint: {checkpoint[:50]}...")
 99: 
100:     # Fetch documents from source
101:     documents, new_checkpoint = await fetch_from_source(source, connector_config, checkpoint)
102: 
103:     if not documents:
104:         logger.info(f"No new documents from {source}")
105:         return {
106:             "source": source,
107:             "documents_fetched": 0,
108:             "documents_processed": 0,
109:         }
110: 
111:     logger.info(f"Fetched {len(documents)} documents from {source}")
112: 
113:     # Ingest the documents
114:     result = await ingest_documents(
115:         namespace_id=namespace_id,
116:         documents=documents,
117:         storage=storage,
118:         skill_name=skill_name,
119:         **kwargs,
120:     )
121: 
122:     # Update checkpoint
123:     if new_checkpoint:
124:         await set_sync_checkpoint(namespace_id, source, new_checkpoint, storage)
125:         logger.info(f"Updated checkpoint: {new_checkpoint[:50]}...")
126: 
127:     return {
128:         "source": source,
129:         "documents_fetched": len(documents),
130:         "documents_processed": result["processed_documents"],
131:         "checkpoint": new_checkpoint,
132:         **result,
133:     }
134: 
135: 
136: @pipeline("sync_all", description="Sync from all configured sources", tags=["sync"])
137: @flow(name="sync_all_sources", log_prints=True)
138: async def sync_all_sources(
139:     namespace_id: UUID,
140:     sources: list[dict[str, Any]],
141:     storage: StorageCoordinator | None = None,
142:     **kwargs,
143: ) -> dict[str, Any]:
144:     """Sync from multiple sources.
145: 
146:     Args:
147:         namespace_id: Target namespace
148:         sources: List of source configs with 'name' and 'config' keys
149:         storage: StorageCoordinator instance
150: 
151:     Returns:
152:         Summary of all sync results
153:     """
154:     if storage is None:
155:         raise ValueError("storage is required")
156: 
157:     results = []
158:     for source_config in sources:
159:         source_name = source_config.get("name", "unknown")
160:         connector_config = source_config.get("config", {})
161: 
162:         try:
163:             result = await sync_source(
164:                 namespace_id=namespace_id,
165:                 source=source_name,
166:                 storage=storage,
167:                 connector_config=connector_config,
168:                 **kwargs,
169:             )
170:             results.append({"source": source_name, "status": "success", **result})
171:         except Exception as e:
172:             logger.error(f"Sync failed for {source_name}: {e}")
173:             results.append({"source": source_name, "status": "failed", "error": str(e)})
174: 
175:     return {
176:         "namespace_id": str(namespace_id),
177:         "sources_synced": len([r for r in results if r["status"] == "success"]),
178:         "sources_failed": len([r for r in results if r["status"] == "failed"]),
179:         "results": results,
180:     }
````
