## File: src/khora/pipelines/tasks/chunk.py
````python
 1: """Chunking task for document processing."""
 2: 
 3: from __future__ import annotations
 4: 
 5: from typing import TYPE_CHECKING
 6: 
 7: from prefect import task
 8: 
 9: if TYPE_CHECKING:
10:     from khora.core.models import Chunk, Document
11: 
12: 
13: @task(name="chunk_document", retries=2, retry_delay_seconds=5)
14: async def chunk_document(
15:     document: Document,
16:     *,
17:     strategy: str = "semantic",
18:     chunk_size: int = 512,
19:     chunk_overlap: int = 50,
20: ) -> list[Chunk]:
21:     """Chunk a document into smaller pieces.
22: 
23:     Args:
24:         document: Document to chunk
25:         strategy: Chunking strategy (fixed, semantic, recursive)
26:         chunk_size: Target chunk size in tokens
27:         chunk_overlap: Overlap between chunks
28: 
29:     Returns:
30:         List of Chunk objects
31:     """
32:     from khora.core.models import Chunk, ChunkMetadata
33:     from khora.extraction.chunkers import create_chunker
34: 
35:     # Create chunker
36:     chunker = create_chunker(strategy, chunk_size=chunk_size, chunk_overlap=chunk_overlap)
37: 
38:     # Chunk the document
39:     chunk_results = chunker.chunk(document.content)
40: 
41:     # Convert to Chunk objects
42:     chunks = []
43:     for result in chunk_results:
44:         chunk = Chunk(
45:             namespace_id=document.namespace_id,
46:             document_id=document.id,
47:             content=result.content,
48:             metadata=ChunkMetadata(
49:                 document_id=document.id,
50:                 chunk_index=result.index,
51:                 start_char=result.start_char,
52:                 end_char=result.end_char,
53:                 token_count=result.token_count,
54:                 custom=result.metadata,
55:             ),
56:         )
57:         chunks.append(chunk)
58: 
59:     return chunks
````

## File: src/khora/pipelines/tasks/embed.py
````python
 1: """Embedding task for chunks."""
 2: 
 3: from __future__ import annotations
 4: 
 5: from typing import TYPE_CHECKING
 6: 
 7: from prefect import task
 8: 
 9: if TYPE_CHECKING:
10:     from khora.core.models import Chunk
11: 
12: 
13: @task(name="embed_chunks", retries=3, retry_delay_seconds=10)
14: async def embed_chunks(
15:     chunks: list[Chunk],
16:     *,
17:     model: str = "text-embedding-3-small",
18:     batch_size: int = 100,
19: ) -> list[Chunk]:
20:     """Generate embeddings for chunks.
21: 
22:     Args:
23:         chunks: Chunks to embed
24:         model: Embedding model to use
25:         batch_size: Batch size for embedding
26: 
27:     Returns:
28:         Chunks with embeddings set
29:     """
30:     from khora.extraction.embedders import LiteLLMEmbedder
31: 
32:     if not chunks:
33:         return []
34: 
35:     # Create embedder
36:     embedder = LiteLLMEmbedder(model=model, batch_size=batch_size)
37: 
38:     # Extract texts
39:     texts = [chunk.content for chunk in chunks]
40: 
41:     # Generate embeddings
42:     embeddings = await embedder.embed_batch(texts)
43: 
44:     # Update chunks with embeddings
45:     for chunk, embedding in zip(chunks, embeddings):
46:         chunk.embedding = embedding
47:         chunk.embedding_model = model
48: 
49:     return chunks
````

## File: src/khora/pipelines/tasks/extract.py
````python
  1: """Entity extraction task."""
  2: 
  3: from __future__ import annotations
  4: 
  5: from typing import TYPE_CHECKING
  6: 
  7: from prefect import task
  8: 
  9: if TYPE_CHECKING:
 10:     from khora.core.models import Chunk, Entity, Relationship
 11: 
 12: 
 13: @task(name="extract_entities", retries=2, retry_delay_seconds=10)
 14: async def extract_entities(
 15:     chunks: list[Chunk],
 16:     *,
 17:     skill_name: str = "general_entities",
 18:     model: str = "gpt-4o-mini",
 19: ) -> tuple[list[Entity], list[Relationship]]:
 20:     """Extract entities and relationships from chunks.
 21: 
 22:     Args:
 23:         chunks: Chunks to extract from
 24:         skill_name: Extraction skill to use
 25:         model: LLM model for extraction
 26: 
 27:     Returns:
 28:         Tuple of (entities, relationships)
 29:     """
 30:     from khora.core.models import Entity, Relationship
 31:     from khora.core.models.entity import EntityType, RelationshipType
 32:     from khora.extraction.extractors import LLMEntityExtractor
 33:     from khora.extraction.skills.registry import get_default_registry
 34: 
 35:     if not chunks:
 36:         return [], []
 37: 
 38:     # Get extraction skill
 39:     registry = get_default_registry()
 40:     skill = registry.get_or_default(skill_name)
 41: 
 42:     # Create extractor
 43:     extractor = LLMEntityExtractor(model=model)
 44: 
 45:     # Extract from each chunk
 46:     all_entities: dict[str, Entity] = {}  # name -> entity (for dedup)
 47:     all_relationships: list[Relationship] = []
 48: 
 49:     for chunk in chunks:
 50:         result = await extractor.extract(chunk.content, entity_types=skill.entity_types)
 51: 
 52:         # Process entities
 53:         for extracted in result.entities:
 54:             if extracted.confidence < skill.min_entity_confidence:
 55:                 continue
 56: 
 57:             # Deduplicate by name
 58:             key = f"{extracted.name}:{extracted.entity_type}"
 59:             if key in all_entities:
 60:                 # Merge into existing
 61:                 existing = all_entities[key]
 62:                 existing.mention_count += 1
 63:                 if chunk.document_id not in existing.source_document_ids:
 64:                     existing.source_document_ids.append(chunk.document_id)
 65:                 if chunk.id not in existing.source_chunk_ids:
 66:                     existing.source_chunk_ids.append(chunk.id)
 67:             else:
 68:                 # Create new entity
 69:                 entity_type = EntityType.CONCEPT
 70:                 try:
 71:                     entity_type = EntityType(extracted.entity_type)
 72:                 except ValueError:
 73:                     pass
 74: 
 75:                 entity = Entity(
 76:                     namespace_id=chunk.namespace_id,
 77:                     name=extracted.name,
 78:                     entity_type=entity_type,
 79:                     description=extracted.description,
 80:                     attributes=extracted.attributes,
 81:                     source_document_ids=[chunk.document_id],
 82:                     source_chunk_ids=[chunk.id],
 83:                     confidence=extracted.confidence,
 84:                 )
 85:                 all_entities[key] = entity
 86: 
 87:         # Process relationships
 88:         for extracted_rel in result.relationships:
 89:             if extracted_rel.confidence < skill.min_relationship_confidence:
 90:                 continue
 91: 
 92:             rel_type = RelationshipType.RELATES_TO
 93:             try:
 94:                 rel_type = RelationshipType(extracted_rel.relationship_type)
 95:             except ValueError:
 96:                 pass
 97: 
 98:             # Find source and target entities
 99:             source_key = next(
100:                 (k for k in all_entities if k.startswith(f"{extracted_rel.source_entity}:")),
101:                 None,
102:             )
103:             target_key = next(
104:                 (k for k in all_entities if k.startswith(f"{extracted_rel.target_entity}:")),
105:                 None,
106:             )
107: 
108:             if source_key and target_key:
109:                 relationship = Relationship(
110:                     namespace_id=chunk.namespace_id,
111:                     source_entity_id=all_entities[source_key].id,
112:                     target_entity_id=all_entities[target_key].id,
113:                     relationship_type=rel_type,
114:                     description=extracted_rel.description,
115:                     properties=extracted_rel.properties,
116:                     source_document_ids=[chunk.document_id],
117:                     source_chunk_ids=[chunk.id],
118:                     confidence=extracted_rel.confidence,
119:                 )
120:                 all_relationships.append(relationship)
121: 
122:     return list(all_entities.values()), all_relationships
````

## File: src/khora/pipelines/incremental.py
````python
  1: """Incremental update manager for Khora Memory Lake.
  2: 
  3: Handles change detection and incremental processing of documents.
  4: """
  5: 
  6: from __future__ import annotations
  7: 
  8: import hashlib
  9: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
 10: from typing import TYPE_CHECKING, Any
 11: from uuid import UUID
 12: 
 13: from loguru import logger
 14: 
 15: if TYPE_CHECKING:
 16:     from khora.storage import StorageCoordinator
 17: 
 18: 
 19: @dataclass
 20: class ChangeDetectionResult:
 21:     """Result of change detection for a batch of documents."""
 22: 
 23:     new_documents: list[dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)
 24:     updated_documents: list[dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)
 25:     unchanged_documents: list[dict[str, Any]] = field(default_factory=list)
 26:     deleted_document_ids: list[UUID] = field(default_factory=list)
 27: 
 28:     @property
 29:     def has_changes(self) -> bool:
 30:         """Check if there are any changes."""
 31:         return bool(self.new_documents or self.updated_documents or self.deleted_document_ids)
 32: 
 33:     @property
 34:     def total_changes(self) -> int:
 35:         """Get total number of changes."""
 36:         return len(self.new_documents) + len(self.updated_documents) + len(self.deleted_document_ids)
 37: 
 38: 
 39: class IncrementalUpdateManager:
 40:     """Manager for incremental document updates.
 41: 
 42:     Provides checksum-based change detection and incremental
 43:     processing of document changes.
 44:     """
 45: 
 46:     def __init__(self, storage: StorageCoordinator) -> None:
 47:         """Initialize the incremental update manager.
 48: 
 49:         Args:
 50:             storage: StorageCoordinator instance
 51:         """
 52:         self._storage = storage
 53: 
 54:     def compute_checksum(self, content: str) -> str:
 55:         """Compute SHA-256 checksum of content.
 56: 
 57:         Args:
 58:             content: Content to checksum
 59: 
 60:         Returns:
 61:             Hex digest of checksum
 62:         """
 63:         return hashlib.sha256(content.encode("utf-8")).hexdigest()
 64: 
 65:     async def detect_changes(
 66:         self,
 67:         namespace_id: UUID,
 68:         documents: list[dict[str, Any]],
 69:         *,
 70:         detect_deletions: bool = False,
 71:         existing_source_ids: list[str] | None = None,
 72:     ) -> ChangeDetectionResult:
 73:         """Detect changes in a batch of documents.
 74: 
 75:         Args:
 76:             namespace_id: Namespace to check against
 77:             documents: List of document dicts with 'content' and optionally 'source_id'
 78:             detect_deletions: Whether to detect deleted documents
 79:             existing_source_ids: List of source IDs for deletion detection
 80: 
 81:         Returns:
 82:             ChangeDetectionResult with categorized documents
 83:         """
 84:         result = ChangeDetectionResult()
 85: 
 86:         for doc in documents:
 87:             content = doc.get("content", "")
 88:             checksum = self.compute_checksum(content)
 89: 
 90:             # Check for existing document by checksum
 91:             existing = await self._storage.get_document_by_checksum(namespace_id, checksum)
 92: 
 93:             if existing is None:
 94:                 # New document
 95:                 doc["_checksum"] = checksum
 96:                 result.new_documents.append(doc)
 97:             elif not existing.is_processed:
 98:                 # Document exists but not processed (retry)
 99:                 doc["_checksum"] = checksum
100:                 doc["_existing_id"] = str(existing.id)
101:                 result.updated_documents.append(doc)
102:             else:
103:                 # Unchanged
104:                 result.unchanged_documents.append(doc)
105: 
106:         # Detect deletions if requested
107:         if detect_deletions and existing_source_ids:
108:             current_source_ids = {doc.get("source_id") for doc in documents if doc.get("source_id")}
109:             deleted_ids = set(existing_source_ids) - current_source_ids
110:             # Note: Would need to implement source_id lookup in storage
111:             # For now, this is a placeholder
112:             logger.debug(f"Deletion detection found {len(deleted_ids)} potential deletions")
113: 
114:         logger.info(
115:             f"Change detection: {len(result.new_documents)} new, "
116:             f"{len(result.updated_documents)} updated, "
117:             f"{len(result.unchanged_documents)} unchanged"
118:         )
119: 
120:         return result
121: 
122:     async def process_incremental(
123:         self,
124:         namespace_id: UUID,
125:         changes: ChangeDetectionResult,
126:         *,
127:         skill_name: str = "general_entities",
128:     ) -> dict[str, Any]:
129:         """Process incremental changes.
130: 
131:         Args:
132:             namespace_id: Target namespace
133:             changes: Change detection result
134:             skill_name: Extraction skill to use
135: 
136:         Returns:
137:             Processing results
138:         """
139:         from khora.pipelines.flows.ingest import ingest_documents
140: 
141:         if not changes.has_changes:
142:             return {
143:                 "processed": 0,
144:                 "skipped": len(changes.unchanged_documents),
145:             }
146: 
147:         # Process new and updated documents
148:         documents_to_process = changes.new_documents + changes.updated_documents
149: 
150:         result = await ingest_documents(
151:             namespace_id=namespace_id,
152:             documents=documents_to_process,
153:             storage=self._storage,
154:             skill_name=skill_name,
155:         )
156: 
157:         # Handle deletions
158:         if changes.deleted_document_ids:
159:             for doc_id in changes.deleted_document_ids:
160:                 await self._storage.delete_document(doc_id)
161:             logger.info(f"Deleted {len(changes.deleted_document_ids)} documents")
162: 
163:         return {
164:             "new_processed": len(changes.new_documents),
165:             "updated_processed": len(changes.updated_documents),
166:             "deleted": len(changes.deleted_document_ids),
167:             "unchanged": len(changes.unchanged_documents),
168:             **result,
169:         }
````

## File: src/khora/pipelines/manager.py
````python
  1: """Pipeline manager for orchestrating Prefect flows."""
  2: 
  3: from __future__ import annotations
  4: 
  5: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
  6: from datetime import datetime
  7: from typing import TYPE_CHECKING, Any
  8: from uuid import UUID
  9: 
 10: from loguru import logger
 11: 
 12: if TYPE_CHECKING:
 13:     from khora.config import KhoraConfig
 14:     from khora.storage import StorageCoordinator
 15: 
 16: 
 17: @dataclass
 18: class PipelineRun:
 19:     """Information about a pipeline run."""
 20: 
 21:     run_id: str
 22:     pipeline_name: str
 23:     namespace_id: UUID
 24:     status: str  # pending, running, completed, failed
 25:     started_at: datetime | None = None
 26:     completed_at: datetime | None = None
 27:     error: str | None = None
 28:     metadata: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
 29: 
 30: 
 31: class PipelineManager:
 32:     """Manager for running and tracking pipelines.
 33: 
 34:     Orchestrates Prefect flows and tracks their execution
 35:     within the context of a memory namespace.
 36:     """
 37: 
 38:     def __init__(
 39:         self,
 40:         storage: StorageCoordinator | None = None,
 41:         config: KhoraConfig | None = None,
 42:     ) -> None:
 43:         """Initialize the pipeline manager.
 44: 
 45:         Args:
 46:             storage: StorageCoordinator for data access
 47:             config: Khora configuration
 48:         """
 49:         self._storage = storage
 50:         self._config = config
 51:         self._runs: dict[str, PipelineRun] = {}
 52: 
 53:     async def run_pipeline(
 54:         self,
 55:         pipeline_name: str,
 56:         namespace_id: UUID,
 57:         *,
 58:         parameters: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
 59:         wait: bool = True,
 60:     ) -> PipelineRun:
 61:         """Run a registered pipeline.
 62: 
 63:         Args:
 64:             pipeline_name: Name of the pipeline to run
 65:             namespace_id: Namespace to run in
 66:             parameters: Pipeline parameters
 67:             wait: Wait for completion
 68: 
 69:         Returns:
 70:             PipelineRun with execution info
 71:         """
 72:         from .registry import get_registry
 73: 
 74:         registry = get_registry()
 75:         pipeline_info = registry.get(pipeline_name)
 76: 
 77:         if not pipeline_info:
 78:             raise ValueError(f"Unknown pipeline: {pipeline_name}")
 79: 
 80:         # Create run record
 81:         import uuid
 82: 
 83:         run_id = str(uuid.uuid4())
 84:         run = PipelineRun(
 85:             run_id=run_id,
 86:             pipeline_name=pipeline_name,
 87:             namespace_id=namespace_id,
 88:             status="running",
 89:             started_at=datetime.now(),
 90:         )
 91:         self._runs[run_id] = run
 92: 
 93:         logger.info(f"Starting pipeline {pipeline_name} (run_id={run_id})")
 94: 
 95:         try:
 96:             # Prepare parameters
 97:             params = parameters or {}
 98:             params["namespace_id"] = namespace_id
 99:             params["storage"] = self._storage
100:             params["config"] = self._config
101: 
102:             # Run the pipeline
103:             func = pipeline_info.func
104: 
105:             # Check if it's a Prefect flow
106:             if hasattr(func, "fn"):
107:                 # It's wrapped, call the flow directly
108:                 result = await func(**params)
109:             else:
110:                 # Regular async function
111:                 result = await func(**params)
112: 
113:             run.status = "completed"
114:             run.completed_at = datetime.now()
115:             run.metadata["result"] = result
116: 
117:             logger.info(f"Pipeline {pipeline_name} completed (run_id={run_id})")
118: 
119:         except Exception as e:
120:             run.status = "failed"
121:             run.error = str(e)
122:             run.completed_at = datetime.now()
123:             logger.error(f"Pipeline {pipeline_name} failed (run_id={run_id}): {e}")
124:             raise
125: 
126:         return run
127: 
128:     async def run_ingestion(
129:         self,
130:         namespace_id: UUID,
131:         documents: list[dict[str, Any]],
132:         *,
133:         skill_name: str = "general_entities",
134:     ) -> PipelineRun:
135:         """Run the standard ingestion pipeline.
136: 
137:         Args:
138:             namespace_id: Namespace to ingest into
139:             documents: List of documents to ingest
140:             skill_name: Extraction skill to use
141: 
142:         Returns:
143:             PipelineRun with execution info
144:         """
145:         return await self.run_pipeline(
146:             "ingest",
147:             namespace_id,
148:             parameters={
149:                 "documents": documents,
150:                 "skill_name": skill_name,
151:             },
152:         )
153: 
154:     async def run_sync(
155:         self,
156:         namespace_id: UUID,
157:         source: str,
158:         *,
159:         connector_config: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
160:     ) -> PipelineRun:
161:         """Run a sync pipeline for an external source.
162: 
163:         Args:
164:             namespace_id: Namespace to sync into
165:             source: Source name (e.g., "github", "notion")
166:             connector_config: Connector configuration
167: 
168:         Returns:
169:             PipelineRun with execution info
170:         """
171:         return await self.run_pipeline(
172:             f"sync_{source}",
173:             namespace_id,
174:             parameters={
175:                 "source": source,
176:                 "connector_config": connector_config or {},
177:             },
178:         )
179: 
180:     def get_run(self, run_id: str) -> PipelineRun | None:
181:         """Get a pipeline run by ID.
182: 
183:         Args:
184:             run_id: Run ID
185: 
186:         Returns:
187:             PipelineRun or None if not found
188:         """
189:         return self._runs.get(run_id)
190: 
191:     def list_runs(
192:         self,
193:         *,
194:         namespace_id: UUID | None = None,
195:         pipeline_name: str | None = None,
196:         status: str | None = None,
197:     ) -> list[PipelineRun]:
198:         """List pipeline runs with optional filtering.
199: 
200:         Args:
201:             namespace_id: Filter by namespace
202:             pipeline_name: Filter by pipeline name
203:             status: Filter by status
204: 
205:         Returns:
206:             List of matching PipelineRun objects
207:         """
208:         runs = list(self._runs.values())
209: 
210:         if namespace_id:
211:             runs = [r for r in runs if r.namespace_id == namespace_id]
212:         if pipeline_name:
213:             runs = [r for r in runs if r.pipeline_name == pipeline_name]
214:         if status:
215:             runs = [r for r in runs if r.status == status]
216: 
217:         return runs
````

## File: src/khora/pipelines/registry.py
````python
  1: """Pipeline registry with decorators for Khora Memory Lake."""
  2: 
  3: from __future__ import annotations
  4: 
  5: from collections.abc import Callable
  6: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
  7: from typing import Any
  8: 
  9: from loguru import logger
 10: 
 11: 
 12: @dataclass
 13: class PipelineInfo:
 14:     """Information about a registered pipeline."""
 15: 
 16:     name: str
 17:     description: str
 18:     func: Callable
 19:     tags: list[str] = field(default_factory=list)
 20:     version: str = "1.0.0"
 21:     metadata: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
 22: 
 23: 
 24: class PipelineRegistry:
 25:     """Registry for managing pipeline flows.
 26: 
 27:     Provides registration and discovery of pipeline flows
 28:     that can be run by the PipelineManager.
 29:     """
 30: 
 31:     _instance: PipelineRegistry | None = None
 32:     _pipelines: dict[str, PipelineInfo]
 33: 
 34:     def __new__(cls) -> PipelineRegistry:
 35:         """Singleton pattern for global registry."""
 36:         if cls._instance is None:
 37:             cls._instance = super().__new__(cls)
 38:             cls._instance._pipelines = {}
 39:         return cls._instance
 40: 
 41:     def register(
 42:         self,
 43:         name: str,
 44:         *,
 45:         description: str = "",
 46:         tags: list[str] | None = None,
 47:         version: str = "1.0.0",
 48:         **metadata: Any,
 49:     ) -> Callable[[Callable], Callable]:
 50:         """Decorator to register a pipeline flow.
 51: 
 52:         Args:
 53:             name: Pipeline name
 54:             description: Pipeline description
 55:             tags: Pipeline tags for categorization
 56:             version: Pipeline version
 57:             **metadata: Additional metadata
 58: 
 59:         Returns:
 60:             Decorator function
 61:         """
 62: 
 63:         def decorator(func: Callable) -> Callable:
 64:             info = PipelineInfo(
 65:                 name=name,
 66:                 description=description or func.__doc__ or "",
 67:                 func=func,
 68:                 tags=tags or [],
 69:                 version=version,
 70:                 metadata=metadata,
 71:             )
 72:             self._pipelines[name] = info
 73:             logger.debug(f"Registered pipeline: {name}")
 74:             return func
 75: 
 76:         return decorator
 77: 
 78:     def get(self, name: str) -> PipelineInfo | None:
 79:         """Get a pipeline by name.
 80: 
 81:         Args:
 82:             name: Pipeline name
 83: 
 84:         Returns:
 85:             PipelineInfo or None if not found
 86:         """
 87:         return self._pipelines.get(name)
 88: 
 89:     def list_pipelines(self) -> list[str]:
 90:         """List all registered pipeline names.
 91: 
 92:         Returns:
 93:             List of pipeline names
 94:         """
 95:         return list(self._pipelines.keys())
 96: 
 97:     def get_by_tag(self, tag: str) -> list[PipelineInfo]:
 98:         """Get pipelines by tag.
 99: 
100:         Args:
101:             tag: Tag to filter by
102: 
103:         Returns:
104:             List of matching PipelineInfo objects
105:         """
106:         return [p for p in self._pipelines.values() if tag in p.tags]
107: 
108:     def all_pipelines(self) -> list[PipelineInfo]:
109:         """Get all registered pipelines.
110: 
111:         Returns:
112:             List of PipelineInfo objects
113:         """
114:         return list(self._pipelines.values())
115: 
116:     def unregister(self, name: str) -> bool:
117:         """Unregister a pipeline.
118: 
119:         Args:
120:             name: Pipeline name to unregister
121: 
122:         Returns:
123:             True if removed, False if not found
124:         """
125:         if name in self._pipelines:
126:             del self._pipelines[name]
127:             logger.debug(f"Unregistered pipeline: {name}")
128:             return True
129:         return False
130: 
131: 
132: # Global registry instance
133: _registry = PipelineRegistry()
134: 
135: 
136: def pipeline(
137:     name: str,
138:     *,
139:     description: str = "",
140:     tags: list[str] | None = None,
141:     version: str = "1.0.0",
142:     **metadata: Any,
143: ) -> Callable[[Callable], Callable]:
144:     """Decorator to register a pipeline flow.
145: 
146:     Usage:
147:         @pipeline("my_pipeline", description="My pipeline", tags=["ingestion"])
148:         @flow
149:         async def my_pipeline(param: str):
150:             ...
151: 
152:     Args:
153:         name: Pipeline name
154:         description: Pipeline description
155:         tags: Pipeline tags
156:         version: Pipeline version
157:         **metadata: Additional metadata
158: 
159:     Returns:
160:         Decorator function
161:     """
162:     return _registry.register(name, description=description, tags=tags, version=version, **metadata)
163: 
164: 
165: def get_registry() -> PipelineRegistry:
166:     """Get the global pipeline registry.
167: 
168:     Returns:
169:         PipelineRegistry instance
170:     """
171:     return _registry
````

## File: src/khora/query/__init__.py
````python
 1: """Query engine for Khora Memory Lake.
 2: 
 3: Provides hybrid search combining vector, graph, and keyword search
 4: with Reciprocal Rank Fusion for result combination.
 5: """
 6: 
 7: from __future__ import annotations
 8: 
 9: from .engine import HybridQueryEngine, QueryConfig, QueryResult, SearchMode
10: from .fusion import reciprocal_rank_fusion
11: from .temporal import TemporalFilter, TemporalQuery
12: 
13: __all__ = [
14:     "HybridQueryEngine",
15:     "QueryConfig",
16:     "QueryResult",
17:     "SearchMode",
18:     "reciprocal_rank_fusion",
19:     "TemporalFilter",
20:     "TemporalQuery",
21: ]
````

## File: src/khora/query/engine.py
````python
  1: """Hybrid query engine for Khora Memory Lake.
  2: 
  3: Combines vector search, graph traversal, and keyword search
  4: with configurable fusion weights.
  5: """
  6: 
  7: from __future__ import annotations
  8: 
  9: import asyncio
 10: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
 11: from enum import Enum, auto
 12: from typing import TYPE_CHECKING, Any
 13: from uuid import UUID
 14: 
 15: from loguru import logger
 16: 
 17: from .fusion import reciprocal_rank_fusion
 18: from .temporal import TemporalFilter, TemporalQuery
 19: 
 20: if TYPE_CHECKING:
 21:     from khora.acl import ACLContext
 22:     from khora.core.models import Chunk, Entity
 23:     from khora.extraction.embedders import Embedder
 24:     from khora.storage import StorageCoordinator
 25: 
 26: 
 27: class SearchMode(Enum):
 28:     """Search mode for the query engine."""
 29: 
 30:     VECTOR = auto()  # Vector similarity only
 31:     GRAPH = auto()  # Graph traversal only
 32:     HYBRID = auto()  # Combine vector and graph
 33:     ALL = auto()  # Vector, graph, and keyword
 34: 
 35: 
 36: @dataclass
 37: class QueryResult:
 38:     """Result from a query."""
 39: 
 40:     chunks: list[tuple[Chunk, float]] = field(default_factory=list)
 41:     entities: list[tuple[Entity, float]] = field(default_factory=list)
 42:     graph_context: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
 43:     metadata: dict[str, Any] = field(default_factory=dict)
 44: 
 45:     @property
 46:     def top_chunks(self) -> list[Chunk]:
 47:         """Get top chunks without scores."""
 48:         return [chunk for chunk, _ in self.chunks]
 49: 
 50:     @property
 51:     def top_entities(self) -> list[Entity]:
 52:         """Get top entities without scores."""
 53:         return [entity for entity, _ in self.entities]
 54: 
 55:     def get_context_text(self, max_chunks: int = 5) -> str:
 56:         """Get concatenated text from top chunks for LLM context."""
 57:         texts = []
 58:         for chunk, score in self.chunks[:max_chunks]:
 59:             texts.append(chunk.content)
 60:         return "\n\n---\n\n".join(texts)
 61: 
 62: 
 63: @dataclass
 64: class QueryConfig:
 65:     """Configuration for query execution."""
 66: 
 67:     # Search mode
 68:     mode: SearchMode = SearchMode.HYBRID
 69: 
 70:     # Result limits
 71:     max_chunks: int = 10
 72:     max_entities: int = 10
 73:     max_graph_depth: int = 2
 74: 
 75:     # Similarity thresholds
 76:     min_chunk_similarity: float = 0.5
 77:     min_entity_similarity: float = 0.5
 78: 
 79:     # Fusion weights
 80:     vector_weight: float = 0.6
 81:     graph_weight: float = 0.3
 82:     keyword_weight: float = 0.1
 83: 
 84:     # RRF parameter
 85:     rrf_k: int = 60
 86: 
 87:     # Temporal settings
 88:     apply_recency_bias: bool = False
 89:     recency_weight: float = 0.2
 90:     recency_decay_days: float = 30.0
 91: 
 92: 
 93: class HybridQueryEngine:
 94:     """Hybrid query engine combining multiple search methods.
 95: 
 96:     Supports:
 97:     - Vector similarity search on chunks and entities
 98:     - Graph traversal for related entities
 99:     - Keyword search (via pgvector full-text)
100:     - Reciprocal Rank Fusion for combining results
101:     - Temporal filtering and recency bias
102:     """
103: 
104:     def __init__(
105:         self,
106:         storage: StorageCoordinator,
107:         embedder: Embedder | None = None,
108:         config: QueryConfig | None = None,
109:     ) -> None:
110:         """Initialize the query engine.
111: 
112:         Args:
113:             storage: StorageCoordinator for data access
114:             embedder: Embedder for query embedding
115:             config: Query configuration
116:         """
117:         self._storage = storage
118:         self._embedder = embedder
119:         self._config = config or QueryConfig()
120: 
121:     async def query(
122:         self,
123:         query_text: str,
124:         namespace_id: UUID,
125:         *,
126:         config: QueryConfig | None = None,
127:         temporal_filter: TemporalFilter | None = None,
128:         context: ACLContext | None = None,
129:     ) -> QueryResult:
130:         """Execute a hybrid query.
131: 
132:         Args:
133:             query_text: Query text
134:             namespace_id: Namespace to search in
135:             config: Optional query config override
136:             temporal_filter: Optional temporal filter
137:             context: Optional ACL context for permission filtering
138: 
139:         Returns:
140:             QueryResult with matched chunks and entities
141:         """
142:         cfg = config or self._config
143: 
144:         logger.debug(f"Executing query: {query_text[:50]}... (mode={cfg.mode.name})")
145: 
146:         # Get query embedding
147:         query_embedding = None
148:         if self._embedder and cfg.mode in (SearchMode.VECTOR, SearchMode.HYBRID, SearchMode.ALL):
149:             query_embedding = await self._embedder.embed(query_text)
150: 
151:         # Execute searches in parallel based on mode
152:         tasks = []
153: 
154:         if cfg.mode in (SearchMode.VECTOR, SearchMode.HYBRID, SearchMode.ALL) and query_embedding:
155:             tasks.append(self._vector_search(namespace_id, query_embedding, cfg))
156: 
157:         if cfg.mode in (SearchMode.GRAPH, SearchMode.HYBRID, SearchMode.ALL):
158:             tasks.append(self._graph_search(namespace_id, query_text, query_embedding, cfg))
159: 
160:         if cfg.mode == SearchMode.ALL:
161:             tasks.append(self._keyword_search(namespace_id, query_text, cfg))
162: 
163:         # Execute in parallel
164:         results = await asyncio.gather(*tasks, return_exceptions=True)
165: 
166:         # Process results
167:         chunk_results: dict[str, list[tuple[Any, float]]] = {}
168:         entity_results: dict[str, list[tuple[Any, float]]] = {}
169:         graph_context = {}
170: 
171:         for i, result in enumerate(results):
172:             if isinstance(result, Exception):
173:                 logger.error(f"Search {i} failed: {result}")
174:                 continue
175: 
176:             if isinstance(result, dict):
177:                 if "chunks" in result:
178:                     source = result.get("source", f"search_{i}")
179:                     chunk_results[source] = result["chunks"]
180:                 if "entities" in result:
181:                     source = result.get("source", f"search_{i}")
182:                     entity_results[source] = result["entities"]
183:                 if "graph_context" in result:
184:                     graph_context.update(result["graph_context"])
185: 
186:         # Apply RRF fusion
187:         fused_chunks = []
188:         if chunk_results:
189:             weights = {
190:                 "vector": cfg.vector_weight,
191:                 "graph": cfg.graph_weight,
192:                 "keyword": cfg.keyword_weight,
193:             }
194:             fused_chunks = reciprocal_rank_fusion(
195:                 chunk_results,
196:                 k=cfg.rrf_k,
197:                 weights=weights,
198:                 id_extractor=lambda c: str(c.id),
199:             )
200: 
201:         fused_entities = []
202:         if entity_results:
203:             weights = {
204:                 "vector": cfg.vector_weight,
205:                 "graph": cfg.graph_weight,
206:             }
207:             fused_entities = reciprocal_rank_fusion(
208:                 entity_results,
209:                 k=cfg.rrf_k,
210:                 weights=weights,
211:                 id_extractor=lambda e: str(e.id),
212:             )
213: 
214:         # Apply temporal filter
215:         if temporal_filter:
216:             fused_chunks = [(c, s) for c, s in fused_chunks if temporal_filter.matches(c.created_at)]
217: 
218:         # Apply recency bias
219:         if cfg.apply_recency_bias:
220:             temporal_query = TemporalQuery(query_text).with_recency_bias(
221:                 cfg.recency_weight,
222:                 cfg.recency_decay_days,
223:             )
224:             fused_chunks = [(c, s * temporal_query.calculate_recency_score(c.created_at)) for c, s in fused_chunks]
225:             # Re-sort after recency adjustment
226:             fused_chunks.sort(key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)
227: 
228:         # Limit results
229:         fused_chunks = fused_chunks[: cfg.max_chunks]
230:         fused_entities = fused_entities[: cfg.max_entities]
231: 
232:         return QueryResult(
233:             chunks=fused_chunks,
234:             entities=fused_entities,
235:             graph_context=graph_context,
236:             metadata={
237:                 "query": query_text,
238:                 "mode": cfg.mode.name,
239:                 "namespace_id": str(namespace_id),
240:             },
241:         )
242: 
243:     async def _vector_search(
244:         self,
245:         namespace_id: UUID,
246:         query_embedding: list[float],
247:         config: QueryConfig,
248:     ) -> dict[str, Any]:
249:         """Perform vector similarity search."""
250:         # Search chunks
251:         chunk_results = await self._storage.search_similar_chunks(
252:             namespace_id,
253:             query_embedding,
254:             limit=config.max_chunks * 2,  # Get extra for fusion
255:             min_similarity=config.min_chunk_similarity,
256:         )
257: 
258:         # Search entities
259:         entity_ids_scores = await self._storage.search_similar_entities(
260:             namespace_id,
261:             query_embedding,
262:             limit=config.max_entities * 2,
263:             min_similarity=config.min_entity_similarity,
264:         )
265: 
266:         # Fetch full entities
267:         entities = []
268:         for entity_id, score in entity_ids_scores:
269:             entity = await self._storage.get_entity(entity_id)
270:             if entity:
271:                 entities.append((entity, score))
272: 
273:         return {
274:             "source": "vector",
275:             "chunks": chunk_results,
276:             "entities": entities,
277:         }
278: 
279:     async def _graph_search(
280:         self,
281:         namespace_id: UUID,
282:         query_text: str,
283:         query_embedding: list[float] | None,
284:         config: QueryConfig,
285:     ) -> dict[str, Any]:
286:         """Perform graph-based search."""
287:         entities = []
288:         graph_context = {}
289: 
290:         # If we have embedding, find similar entities first
291:         if query_embedding:
292:             entity_ids_scores = await self._storage.search_similar_entities(
293:                 namespace_id,
294:                 query_embedding,
295:                 limit=5,  # Top entities for graph expansion
296:                 min_similarity=config.min_entity_similarity,
297:             )
298: 
299:             # Expand neighborhood for top entities
300:             for entity_id, score in entity_ids_scores[:3]:
301:                 entity = await self._storage.get_entity(entity_id)
302:                 if entity:
303:                     entities.append((entity, score))
304: 
305:                     # Get neighborhood
306:                     neighborhood = await self._storage.get_neighborhood(
307:                         entity_id,
308:                         depth=config.max_graph_depth,
309:                         limit=20,
310:                     )
311:                     graph_context[str(entity_id)] = neighborhood
312: 
313:         # Get related chunks through entities
314:         chunks = []
315:         for entity, score in entities:
316:             # Get chunks that mention this entity
317:             for chunk_id in entity.source_chunk_ids[:5]:
318:                 chunk = await self._storage.get_chunk(chunk_id)
319:                 if chunk:
320:                     # Score based on entity score and mention count
321:                     chunk_score = score * (1 + 0.1 * entity.mention_count)
322:                     chunks.append((chunk, chunk_score))
323: 
324:         return {
325:             "source": "graph",
326:             "chunks": chunks,
327:             "entities": entities,
328:             "graph_context": graph_context,
329:         }
330: 
331:     async def _keyword_search(
332:         self,
333:         namespace_id: UUID,
334:         query_text: str,
335:         config: QueryConfig,
336:     ) -> dict[str, Any]:
337:         """Perform keyword-based search.
338: 
339:         Note: This is a placeholder. Full implementation would use
340:         PostgreSQL full-text search or similar.
341:         """
342:         # For now, return empty results
343:         # Full implementation would query documents/chunks with full-text search
344:         return {
345:             "source": "keyword",
346:             "chunks": [],
347:             "entities": [],
348:         }
349: 
350:     async def find_related_entities(
351:         self,
352:         entity_id: UUID,
353:         namespace_id: UUID,
354:         *,
355:         max_depth: int = 2,
356:         limit: int = 20,
357:     ) -> list[tuple[Entity, float]]:
358:         """Find entities related to a given entity through the graph.
359: 
360:         Args:
361:             entity_id: Starting entity
362:             namespace_id: Namespace to search in
363:             max_depth: Maximum relationship depth
364:             limit: Maximum entities to return
365: 
366:         Returns:
367:             List of (entity, relevance_score) tuples
368:         """
369:         neighborhood = await self._storage.get_neighborhood(
370:             entity_id,
371:             depth=max_depth,
372:             limit=limit,
373:         )
374: 
375:         entities = []
376:         for node in neighborhood.get("entities", []):
377:             entity = await self._storage.get_entity(UUID(node["id"]))
378:             if entity:
379:                 # Score based on path length (shorter = higher score)
380:                 # This is simplified - full impl would consider actual path lengths
381:                 score = 1.0 / (1 + len(neighborhood.get("relationships", [])))
382:                 entities.append((entity, score))
383: 
384:         return entities
385: 
386:     async def temporal_query(
387:         self,
388:         query: TemporalQuery,
389:         namespace_id: UUID,
390:         *,
391:         config: QueryConfig | None = None,
392:     ) -> QueryResult:
393:         """Execute a query with temporal context.
394: 
395:         Args:
396:             query: TemporalQuery with filters and settings
397:             namespace_id: Namespace to search in
398:             config: Optional query config override
399: 
400:         Returns:
401:             QueryResult with temporal filtering applied
402:         """
403:         cfg = config or QueryConfig()
404: 
405:         # Apply temporal settings to config
406:         if query.recency_weight > 0:
407:             cfg.apply_recency_bias = True
408:             cfg.recency_weight = query.recency_weight
409:             cfg.recency_decay_days = query.decay_days
410: 
411:         # Get context filter
412:         temporal_filter = None
413:         if query.filters:
414:             temporal_filter = query.filters[0]  # Use first filter for now
415:         elif query.context_window_days:
416:             temporal_filter = query.get_context_filter()
417: 
418:         return await self.query(
419:             query.query,
420:             namespace_id,
421:             config=cfg,
422:             temporal_filter=temporal_filter,
423:         )
````

## File: src/khora/query/fusion.py
````python
  1: """Reciprocal Rank Fusion for combining search results."""
  2: 
  3: from __future__ import annotations
  4: 
  5: from dataclasses import dataclass
  6: from typing import Any, TypeVar
  7: 
  8: T = TypeVar("T")
  9: 
 10: 
 11: @dataclass
 12: class RankedItem:
 13:     """An item with its score and source."""
 14: 
 15:     item: Any
 16:     score: float
 17:     source: str  # Which search method produced this result
 18:     rank: int = 0  # Rank within its source
 19: 
 20: 
 21: def reciprocal_rank_fusion(
 22:     ranked_lists: dict[str, list[tuple[Any, float]]],
 23:     *,
 24:     k: int = 60,
 25:     weights: dict[str, float] | None = None,
 26:     id_extractor: callable = lambda x: x,
 27: ) -> list[tuple[Any, float]]:
 28:     """Combine multiple ranked lists using Reciprocal Rank Fusion.
 29: 
 30:     RRF is a simple but effective method for combining results from
 31:     multiple search systems without requiring score calibration.
 32: 
 33:     RRF score = sum(weight[source] / (k + rank[source]))
 34: 
 35:     Args:
 36:         ranked_lists: Dict of source name to list of (item, score) tuples
 37:         k: RRF parameter (default 60, higher = more even distribution)
 38:         weights: Optional weights for each source
 39:         id_extractor: Function to extract ID from item for deduplication
 40: 
 41:     Returns:
 42:         List of (item, rrf_score) tuples sorted by score descending
 43:     """
 44:     if not ranked_lists:
 45:         return []
 46: 
 47:     # Default equal weights
 48:     if weights is None:
 49:         weights = {source: 1.0 for source in ranked_lists}
 50: 
 51:     # Normalize weights
 52:     total_weight = sum(weights.get(s, 1.0) for s in ranked_lists)
 53:     normalized_weights = {s: weights.get(s, 1.0) / total_weight for s in ranked_lists}
 54: 
 55:     # Calculate RRF scores
 56:     rrf_scores: dict[Any, float] = {}
 57:     items_by_id: dict[Any, Any] = {}
 58: 
 59:     for source, ranked_list in ranked_lists.items():
 60:         weight = normalized_weights.get(source, 1.0)
 61: 
 62:         for rank, (item, _score) in enumerate(ranked_list, start=1):
 63:             item_id = id_extractor(item)
 64: 
 65:             # RRF formula: weight / (k + rank)
 66:             rrf_contribution = weight / (k + rank)
 67: 
 68:             if item_id in rrf_scores:
 69:                 rrf_scores[item_id] += rrf_contribution
 70:             else:
 71:                 rrf_scores[item_id] = rrf_contribution
 72:                 items_by_id[item_id] = item
 73: 
 74:     # Sort by RRF score
 75:     sorted_ids = sorted(rrf_scores.keys(), key=lambda x: rrf_scores[x], reverse=True)
 76: 
 77:     return [(items_by_id[item_id], rrf_scores[item_id]) for item_id in sorted_ids]
 78: 
 79: 
 80: def combine_with_weights(
 81:     results: list[list[tuple[Any, float]]],
 82:     weights: list[float],
 83:     *,
 84:     id_extractor: callable = lambda x: x,
 85: ) -> list[tuple[Any, float]]:
 86:     """Combine results using simple weighted scoring.
 87: 
 88:     Args:
 89:         results: List of ranked result lists
 90:         weights: Weight for each result list
 91:         id_extractor: Function to extract ID from item
 92: 
 93:     Returns:
 94:         Combined and sorted results
 95:     """
 96:     # Normalize weights
 97:     total_weight = sum(weights)
 98:     normalized_weights = [w / total_weight for w in weights]
 99: 
100:     # Combine scores
101:     combined_scores: dict[Any, float] = {}
102:     items_by_id: dict[Any, Any] = {}
103: 
104:     for result_list, weight in zip(results, normalized_weights):
105:         for item, score in result_list:
106:             item_id = id_extractor(item)
107:             weighted_score = score * weight
108: 
109:             if item_id in combined_scores:
110:                 combined_scores[item_id] += weighted_score
111:             else:
112:                 combined_scores[item_id] = weighted_score
113:                 items_by_id[item_id] = item
114: 
115:     # Sort by combined score
116:     sorted_ids = sorted(combined_scores.keys(), key=lambda x: combined_scores[x], reverse=True)
117: 
118:     return [(items_by_id[item_id], combined_scores[item_id]) for item_id in sorted_ids]
````

## File: src/khora/query/temporal.py
````python
  1: """Temporal query support for Khora Memory Lake."""
  2: 
  3: from __future__ import annotations
  4: 
  5: from dataclasses import dataclass, field
  6: from datetime import datetime, timedelta
  7: from enum import Enum
  8: 
  9: 
 10: class TemporalOperator(str, Enum):
 11:     """Temporal query operators."""
 12: 
 13:     BEFORE = "before"
 14:     AFTER = "after"
 15:     BETWEEN = "between"
 16:     DURING = "during"  # Within a specific time period
 17:     OVERLAPS = "overlaps"  # Overlaps with a time range
 18: 
 19: 
 20: @dataclass
 21: class TemporalFilter:
 22:     """Filter for temporal queries."""
 23: 
 24:     operator: TemporalOperator = TemporalOperator.AFTER
 25:     start_time: datetime | None = None
 26:     end_time: datetime | None = None
 27: 
 28:     # For relative time queries
 29:     relative_days: int | None = None
 30:     relative_hours: int | None = None
 31: 
 32:     @classmethod
 33:     def last_days(cls, days: int) -> TemporalFilter:
 34:         """Create a filter for the last N days."""
 35:         return cls(
 36:             operator=TemporalOperator.AFTER,
 37:             start_time=datetime.now() - timedelta(days=days),
 38:         )
 39: 
 40:     @classmethod
 41:     def last_hours(cls, hours: int) -> TemporalFilter:
 42:         """Create a filter for the last N hours."""
 43:         return cls(
 44:             operator=TemporalOperator.AFTER,
 45:             start_time=datetime.now() - timedelta(hours=hours),
 46:         )
 47: 
 48:     @classmethod
 49:     def before(cls, time: datetime) -> TemporalFilter:
 50:         """Create a filter for before a specific time."""
 51:         return cls(operator=TemporalOperator.BEFORE, end_time=time)
 52: 
 53:     @classmethod
 54:     def after(cls, time: datetime) -> TemporalFilter:
 55:         """Create a filter for after a specific time."""
 56:         return cls(operator=TemporalOperator.AFTER, start_time=time)
 57: 
 58:     @classmethod
 59:     def between(cls, start: datetime, end: datetime) -> TemporalFilter:
 60:         """Create a filter for a time range."""
 61:         return cls(operator=TemporalOperator.BETWEEN, start_time=start, end_time=end)
 62: 
 63:     def get_effective_times(self) -> tuple[datetime | None, datetime | None]:
 64:         """Get the effective start and end times."""
 65:         start = self.start_time
 66:         end = self.end_time
 67: 
 68:         # Handle relative times
 69:         if self.relative_days is not None:
 70:             start = datetime.now() - timedelta(days=self.relative_days)
 71:         if self.relative_hours is not None:
 72:             start = datetime.now() - timedelta(hours=self.relative_hours)
 73: 
 74:         return start, end
 75: 
 76:     def matches(self, timestamp: datetime) -> bool:
 77:         """Check if a timestamp matches this filter."""
 78:         start, end = self.get_effective_times()
 79: 
 80:         if self.operator == TemporalOperator.BEFORE:
 81:             return end is not None and timestamp < end
 82:         elif self.operator == TemporalOperator.AFTER:
 83:             return start is not None and timestamp > start
 84:         elif self.operator == TemporalOperator.BETWEEN:
 85:             if start is None or end is None:
 86:                 return True
 87:             return start <= timestamp <= end
 88:         else:
 89:             return True
 90: 
 91: 
 92: @dataclass
 93: class TemporalQuery:
 94:     """Query with temporal context."""
 95: 
 96:     query: str
 97:     filters: list[TemporalFilter] = field(default_factory=list)
 98: 
 99:     # Temporal weighting
100:     recency_weight: float = 0.0  # 0 = no recency bias, 1 = strong recency bias
101:     decay_days: float = 30.0  # Half-life for recency decay
102: 
103:     # Context window
104:     context_window_days: int | None = None  # Limit context to recent period
105: 
106:     def add_filter(self, filter: TemporalFilter) -> TemporalQuery:
107:         """Add a temporal filter."""
108:         self.filters.append(filter)
109:         return self
110: 
111:     def with_recency_bias(self, weight: float = 0.3, decay_days: float = 30.0) -> TemporalQuery:
112:         """Add recency bias to scoring."""
113:         self.recency_weight = weight
114:         self.decay_days = decay_days
115:         return self
116: 
117:     def calculate_recency_score(self, timestamp: datetime) -> float:
118:         """Calculate recency score for a timestamp.
119: 
120:         Uses exponential decay with configurable half-life.
121:         """
122:         if self.recency_weight == 0:
123:             return 1.0
124: 
125:         now = datetime.now()
126:         if timestamp.tzinfo:
127:             from datetime import UTC
128: 
129:             now = datetime.now(UTC)
130: 
131:         age_days = (now - timestamp).total_seconds() / (24 * 60 * 60)
132: 
133:         # Exponential decay: score = 0.5^(age/half_life)
134:         import math
135: 
136:         decay = math.pow(0.5, age_days / self.decay_days)
137: 
138:         # Blend with recency weight
139:         return (1 - self.recency_weight) + (self.recency_weight * decay)
140: 
141:     def get_context_filter(self) -> TemporalFilter | None:
142:         """Get a filter for the context window."""
143:         if self.context_window_days is None:
144:             return None
145:         return TemporalFilter.last_days(self.context_window_days)
````

````python
  1: """Abstract protocols for storage backends.
  2: 
  3: These protocols define the interface that all storage backends must implement,
  4: enabling dependency injection and easy testing with mocks.
  5: """
  6: 
  7: from __future__ import annotations
  8: 
  9: from abc import abstractmethod
 10: from datetime import datetime
 11: from typing import TYPE_CHECKING, Any, Protocol, runtime_checkable
 12: from uuid import UUID
 13: 
 14: if TYPE_CHECKING:
 15:     from khora.core.models import (

 28: @runtime_checkable
 29: class RelationalBackendProtocol(Protocol):
 30:     """Protocol for relational database backends (PostgreSQL).
 31: 
 32:     Handles storage of documents, tenancy data, ACLs, and sync checkpoints.
 33:     """
 34: 
 35:     @abstractmethod
 36:     async def connect(self) -> None:
 37:         """Establish connection to the database."""
 38:         ...
 39:

 42:         """Close database connections."""
 43:         ...
 44: 
 45:     @abstractmethod
 46:     async def is_healthy(self) -> bool:
 47:         """Check if the backend is healthy and connected."""
 48:         ...
 49:

 54:         ...
````

## File: src/khora/storage/backends/pgvector.py
````python
  1: """pgvector backend for vector embeddings storage.
  2: 
  3: Handles storage and retrieval of embeddings for semantic search
  4: using pgvector extension in PostgreSQL.
  5: """
  6: 
  7: from __future__ import annotations
  8: 
  9: from datetime import UTC, datetime
 10: from typing import TYPE_CHECKING
 11: from uuid import UUID
 12: 
 13: from loguru import logger
 14: from sqlalchemy import delete, func, select, text, update
 15: from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import AsyncEngine, AsyncSession, async_sessionmaker, create_async_engine
 16: 
 17: from khora.core.models import Chunk, ChunkMetadata
 18: from khora.db.models import Base, ChunkModel, EntityModel
 19: 
 20: if TYPE_CHECKING:
 21:     pass
 22: 
 23: 
 24: class PgVectorBackend:
 25:     """pgvector backend for vector embeddings.
 26: 
 27:     Handles all vector operations including chunk storage,
 28:     similarity search, and entity embeddings.
 29:     """
 30: 
 31:     def __init__(
 32:         self,
 33:         database_url: str,
 34:         *,
 35:         embedding_dimension: int = 1536,
 36:         echo: bool = False,
 37:         pool_size: int = 5,
 38:         max_overflow: int = 10,
 39:     ) -> None:
 40:         """Initialize the pgvector backend.
 41: 
 42:         Args:
 43:             database_url: PostgreSQL connection URL (with pgvector extension)
 44:             embedding_dimension: Dimension of embedding vectors
 45:             echo: Enable SQL echo logging
 46:             pool_size: Connection pool size
 47:             max_overflow: Maximum overflow connections
 48:         """
 49:         # Convert to async URL if needed
 50:         if database_url.startswith("postgresql://"):
 51:             database_url = database_url.replace("postgresql://", "postgresql+asyncpg://", 1)
 52:         elif database_url.startswith("postgres://"):
 53:             database_url = database_url.replace("postgres://", "postgresql+asyncpg://", 1)
 54: 
 55:         self._database_url = database_url
 56:         self._embedding_dimension = embedding_dimension
 57:         self._echo = echo
 58:         self._pool_size = pool_size
 59:         self._max_overflow = max_overflow
 60:         self._engine: AsyncEngine | None = None
 61:         self._session_factory: async_sessionmaker[AsyncSession] | None = None
 62: 
 63:     async def connect(self) -> None:
 64:         """Establish connection to the database."""
 65:         if self._engine is not None:
 66:             return
 67: 
 68:         logger.info("Connecting to pgvector...")
 69:         self._engine = create_async_engine(
 70:             self._database_url,
 71:             echo=self._echo,
 72:             pool_size=self._pool_size,
 73:             max_overflow=self._max_overflow,
 74:         )
 75:         self._session_factory = async_sessionmaker(
 76:             self._engine,
 77:             class_=AsyncSession,
 78:             expire_on_commit=False,
 79:         )
 80: 
 81:         # Ensure pgvector extension is enabled
 82:         async with self._engine.begin() as conn:
 83:             await conn.execute(text("CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS vector"))
 84: 
 85:         logger.info("Connected to pgvector")
 86: 
 87:     async def disconnect(self) -> None:
 88:         """Close database connections."""
 89:         if self._engine is not None:
 90:             logger.info("Disconnecting from pgvector...")
 91:             await self._engine.dispose()
 92:             self._engine = None
 93:             self._session_factory = None
 94:             logger.info("Disconnected from pgvector")
 95: 
 96:     async def is_healthy(self) -> bool:
 97:         """Check if the backend is healthy and connected."""
 98:         if self._engine is None or self._session_factory is None:
 99:             return False
100:         try:
101:             async with self._session_factory() as session:
102:                 await session.execute(select(1))
103:             return True
104:         except Exception as e:
105:             logger.error(f"pgvector health check failed: {e}")
106:             return False
107: 
108:     def _get_session(self) -> AsyncSession:
109:         """Get a new database session."""
110:         if self._session_factory is None:
111:             raise RuntimeError("Backend not connected. Call connect() first.")
112:         return self._session_factory()
113: 
114:     async def create_tables(self) -> None:
115:         """Create all database tables (for testing/development)."""
116:         if self._engine is None:
117:             raise RuntimeError("Backend not connected. Call connect() first.")
118:         async with self._engine.begin() as conn:
119:             await conn.run_sync(Base.metadata.create_all)
120: 
121:     # =========================================================================
122:     # Chunk operations
123:     # =========================================================================
124: 
125:     async def create_chunk(self, chunk: Chunk) -> Chunk:
126:         """Create a new chunk with its embedding."""
127:         async with self._get_session() as session:
128:             model = ChunkModel(
129:                 id=str(chunk.id),
130:                 namespace_id=str(chunk.namespace_id),
131:                 document_id=str(chunk.document_id),
132:                 content=chunk.content,
133:                 chunk_index=chunk.metadata.chunk_index,
134:                 start_char=chunk.metadata.start_char,
135:                 end_char=chunk.metadata.end_char,
136:                 token_count=chunk.metadata.token_count,
137:                 metadata_=chunk.metadata.custom,
138:                 embedding=chunk.embedding,
139:                 embedding_model=chunk.embedding_model,
140:                 created_at=chunk.created_at,
141:             )
142:             session.add(model)
143:             await session.commit()
144:             await session.refresh(model)
145:             return self._chunk_model_to_domain(model)
146: 
147:     async def create_chunks_batch(self, chunks: list[Chunk]) -> list[Chunk]:
148:         """Create multiple chunks in a batch."""
149:         if not chunks:
150:             return []
151: 
152:         async with self._get_session() as session:
153:             models = [
154:                 ChunkModel(
155:                     id=str(chunk.id),
156:                     namespace_id=str(chunk.namespace_id),
157:                     document_id=str(chunk.document_id),
158:                     content=chunk.content,
159:                     chunk_index=chunk.metadata.chunk_index,
160:                     start_char=chunk.metadata.start_char,
161:                     end_char=chunk.metadata.end_char,
162:                     token_count=chunk.metadata.token_count,
163:                     metadata_=chunk.metadata.custom,
164:                     embedding=chunk.embedding,
165:                     embedding_model=chunk.embedding_model,
166:                     created_at=chunk.created_at,
167:                 )
168:                 for chunk in chunks
169:             ]
170:             session.add_all(models)
171:             await session.commit()
172:             return chunks
173: 
174:     async def get_chunk(self, chunk_id: UUID) -> Chunk | None:
175:         """Get a chunk by ID."""
176:         async with self._get_session() as session:
177:             result = await session.execute(select(ChunkModel).where(ChunkModel.id == str(chunk_id)))
178:             model = result.scalar_one_or_none()
179:             return self._chunk_model_to_domain(model) if model else None
180: 
181:     async def get_chunks_by_document(self, document_id: UUID) -> list[Chunk]:
182:         """Get all chunks for a document."""
183:         async with self._get_session() as session:
184:             result = await session.execute(
185:                 select(ChunkModel).where(ChunkModel.document_id == str(document_id)).order_by(ChunkModel.chunk_index)
186:             )
187:             return [self._chunk_model_to_domain(m) for m in result.scalars().all()]
188: 
189:     async def delete_chunks_by_document(self, document_id: UUID) -> int:
190:         """Delete all chunks for a document."""
191:         async with self._get_session() as session:
192:             result = await session.execute(delete(ChunkModel).where(ChunkModel.document_id == str(document_id)))
193:             await session.commit()
194:             return result.rowcount
195: 
196:     async def search_similar(
197:         self,
198:         namespace_id: UUID,
199:         query_embedding: list[float],
200:         *,
201:         limit: int = 10,
202:         min_similarity: float = 0.0,
203:         filter_document_ids: list[UUID] | None = None,
204:     ) -> list[tuple[Chunk, float]]:
205:         """Search for similar chunks using vector similarity.
206: 
207:         Uses cosine similarity for matching. Returns list of (chunk, similarity_score) tuples.
208:         """
209:         async with self._get_session() as session:
210:             # Build cosine similarity expression
211:             # pgvector uses <=> for cosine distance, so similarity = 1 - distance
212:             similarity = 1 - ChunkModel.embedding.cosine_distance(query_embedding)
213: 
214:             query = (
215:                 select(ChunkModel, similarity.label("similarity"))
216:                 .where(
217:                     ChunkModel.namespace_id == str(namespace_id),
218:                     ChunkModel.embedding.is_not(None),
219:                 )
220:                 .order_by(similarity.desc())
221:                 .limit(limit)
222:             )
223: 
224:             if filter_document_ids:
225:                 query = query.where(ChunkModel.document_id.in_([str(d) for d in filter_document_ids]))
226: 
227:             if min_similarity > 0:
228:                 query = query.where(similarity >= min_similarity)
229: 
230:             result = await session.execute(query)
231:             rows = result.all()
232: 
233:             return [(self._chunk_model_to_domain(row.ChunkModel), row.similarity) for row in rows]
234: 
235:     def _chunk_model_to_domain(self, model: ChunkModel) -> Chunk:
236:         """Convert ChunkModel to domain Chunk."""
237:         return Chunk(
238:             id=UUID(model.id),
239:             namespace_id=UUID(model.namespace_id),
240:             document_id=UUID(model.document_id),
241:             content=model.content,
242:             metadata=ChunkMetadata(
243:                 document_id=UUID(model.document_id),
244:                 chunk_index=model.chunk_index,
245:                 start_char=model.start_char,
246:                 end_char=model.end_char,
247:                 token_count=model.token_count,
248:                 custom=model.metadata_,
249:             ),
250:             embedding=list(model.embedding) if model.embedding else None,
251:             embedding_model=model.embedding_model,
252:             created_at=model.created_at,
253:         )
254: 
255:     # =========================================================================
256:     # Entity embedding operations
257:     # =========================================================================
258: 
259:     async def update_entity_embedding(self, entity_id: UUID, embedding: list[float], model: str) -> None:
260:         """Update the embedding for an entity."""
261:         async with self._get_session() as session:
262:             await session.execute(
263:                 update(EntityModel)
264:                 .where(EntityModel.id == str(entity_id))
265:                 .values(
266:                     embedding=embedding,
267:                     embedding_model=model,
268:                     updated_at=datetime.now(UTC),
269:                 )
270:             )
271:             await session.commit()
272: 
273:     async def search_similar_entities(
274:         self,
275:         namespace_id: UUID,
276:         query_embedding: list[float],
277:         *,
278:         limit: int = 10,
279:         min_similarity: float = 0.0,
280:     ) -> list[tuple[UUID, float]]:
281:         """Search for similar entities by embedding.
282: 
283:         Returns list of (entity_id, similarity_score) tuples.
284:         """
285:         async with self._get_session() as session:
286:             similarity = 1 - EntityModel.embedding.cosine_distance(query_embedding)
287: 
288:             query = (
289:                 select(EntityModel.id, similarity.label("similarity"))
290:                 .where(
291:                     EntityModel.namespace_id == str(namespace_id),
292:                     EntityModel.embedding.is_not(None),
293:                 )
294:                 .order_by(similarity.desc())
295:                 .limit(limit)
296:             )
297: 
298:             if min_similarity > 0:
299:                 query = query.where(similarity >= min_similarity)
300: 
301:             result = await session.execute(query)
302:             return [(UUID(row.id), row.similarity) for row in result.all()]
303: 
304:     # =========================================================================
305:     # Utility operations
306:     # =========================================================================
307: 
308:     async def get_embedding_stats(self, namespace_id: UUID) -> dict:
309:         """Get statistics about embeddings in a namespace."""
310:         async with self._get_session() as session:
311:             # Count chunks with embeddings
312:             chunk_count = await session.execute(
313:                 select(func.count(ChunkModel.id)).where(
314:                     ChunkModel.namespace_id == str(namespace_id),
315:                     ChunkModel.embedding.is_not(None),
316:                 )
317:             )
318:             # Count entities with embeddings
319:             entity_count = await session.execute(
320:                 select(func.count(EntityModel.id)).where(
321:                     EntityModel.namespace_id == str(namespace_id),
322:                     EntityModel.embedding.is_not(None),
323:                 )
324:             )
325: 
326:             return {
327:                 "chunk_embeddings": chunk_count.scalar_one(),
328:                 "entity_embeddings": entity_count.scalar_one(),
329:             }
````

````python
  1: """PostgreSQL backend for relational data storage.
  2: 
  3: Handles storage of documents, tenancy data, ACLs, and sync checkpoints
  4: using SQLAlchemy async with asyncpg.
  5: """
  6: 
  7: from __future__ import annotations
  8: 
  9: from datetime import UTC, datetime
 10: from typing import TYPE_CHECKING
 11: from uuid import UUID
 12: 
 13: from loguru import logger
 14: from sqlalchemy import select, update
 15: from sqlalchemy.ext.asyncio import AsyncEngine, AsyncSession, async_sessionmaker, create_async_engine
 16: 
 17: from khora.core.models import Document, DocumentMetadata, MemoryNamespace, Organization, TenancyMode, Workspace
 18: from khora.core.models.document import DocumentStatus
 19: from khora.db.models import (
 20:     Base,
 21:     DocumentModel,
 22:     MemoryNamespaceModel,
 23:     OrganizationModel,
 24:     SyncCheckpointModel,
 25:     WorkspaceModel,
 26: )
 27: 
 28: if TYPE_CHECKING:
 29:     pass
 30: 
 31: 
 32: class PostgreSQLBackend:
 33:     """PostgreSQL backend for relational data.
 34: 
 35:     Handles all relational data operations including multi-tenancy
 36:     hierarchy, documents, and sync checkpoints.
 37:     """
 38: 
 39:     def __init__(self, database_url: str, *, echo: bool = False, pool_size: int = 5, max_overflow: int = 10) -> None:
 40:         """Initialize the PostgreSQL backend.
 41: 
 42:         Args:
 43:             database_url: PostgreSQL connection URL
 44:             echo: Enable SQL echo logging
 45:             pool_size: Connection pool size
 46:             max_overflow: Maximum overflow connections
 47:         """
 48:         # Convert to async URL if needed
 49:         if database_url.startswith("postgresql://"):
 50:             database_url = database_url.replace("postgresql://", "postgresql+asyncpg://", 1)
 51:         elif database_url.startswith("postgres://"):
 52:             database_url = database_url.replace("postgres://", "postgresql+asyncpg://", 1)
 53: 
 54:         self._database_url = database_url
 55:         self._echo = echo
 56:         self._pool_size = pool_size
 57:         self._max_overflow = max_overflow
 58:         self._engine: AsyncEngine | None = None
 59:         self._session_factory: async_sessionmaker[AsyncSession] | None = None
 60: 
 61:     async def connect(self) -> None:
 62:         """Establish connection to the database."""
 63:         if self._engine is not None:
 64:             return
 65: 
 66:         logger.info("Connecting to PostgreSQL...")
 67:         self._engine = create_async_engine(
 68:             self._database_url,
 69:             echo=self._echo,
 70:             pool_size=self._pool_size,
 71:             max_overflow=self._max_overflow,
 72:         )
 73:         self._session_factory = async_sessionmaker(
 74:             self._engine,
 75:             class_=AsyncSession,
 76:             expire_on_commit=False,
 77:         )
 78:         logger.info("Connected to PostgreSQL")
 79: 
 80:     async def disconnect(self) -> None:
 81:         """Close database connections."""
 82:         if self._engine is not None:
 83:             logger.info("Disconnecting from PostgreSQL...")
 84:             await self._engine.dispose()
 85:             self._engine = None
 86:             self._session_factory = None
 87:             logger.info("Disconnected from PostgreSQL")
 88: 
 89:     async def is_healthy(self) -> bool:
 90:         """Check if the backend is healthy and connected."""
 91:         if self._engine is None or self._session_factory is None:
 92:             return False
 93:         try:
 94:             async with self._session_factory() as session:
 95:                 await session.execute(select(1))
 96:             return True
 97:         except Exception as e:
 98:             logger.error(f"PostgreSQL health check failed: {e}")
 99:             return False
100: 
101:     def _get_session(self) -> AsyncSession:
102:         """Get a new database session."""
103:         if self._session_factory is None:
104:             raise RuntimeError("Backend not connected. Call connect() first.")
105:         return self._session_factory()
106: 
107:     async def create_tables(self) -> None:
108:         """Create all database tables (for testing/development)."""
109:         if self._engine is None:
110:             raise RuntimeError("Backend not connected. Call connect() first.")
111:         async with self._engine.begin() as conn:
112:             await conn.run_sync(Base.metadata.create_all)
113:

119:         """Create a new organization."""
120:         async with self._get_session() as session:
121:             model = OrganizationModel(
122:                 id=str(org.id),
123:                 name=org.name,
124:                 slug=org.slug,
125:                 tenancy_mode=org.tenancy_mode,
126:                 metadata_=org.metadata,
127:                 created_at=org.created_at,
128:                 updated_at=org.updated_at,
129:             )
130:             session.add(model)
131:             await session.commit()
132:             await session.refresh(model)
133:             return self._org_model_to_domain(model)

337:     async def list_documents(
338:         self,
339:         namespace_id: UUID,
340:         *,
341:         status: str | None = None,
342:         limit: int = 100,
343:         offset: int = 0,
344:     ) -> list[Document]:
345:         """List documents in a namespace."""
346:         async with self._get_session() as session:
347:             query = select(DocumentModel).where(DocumentModel.namespace_id == str(namespace_id))
348:             if status:
349:                 query = query.where(DocumentModel.status == status)
350:             query = query.limit(limit).offset(offset).order_by(DocumentModel.created_at.desc())
351:             result = await session.execute(query)
352:             return [self._document_model_to_domain(m) for m in result.scalars().all()]

360:                 .values(
361:                     content=document.content,
362:                     status=document.status,
363:                     source=document.metadata.source,

365:                     content_type=document.metadata.content_type,
````
